MMEmb-R1: Reasoning-Enhanced Multimodal Embedding with Pair-Aware Selection and Adaptive Control
Authors: Yuchi Wang, Haiyang Yu, Weikang Bian, Jiefeng Long, Xiao Liang, Chao Feng, Hongsheng Li
First: 2026-04-07T17:55:17+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-07T17:55:17+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
MLLMs have been successfully applied to multimodal embedding tasks, yet their generative reasoning capabilities remain underutilized. Directly incorporating chain-of-thought reasoning into embedding learning introduces two fundamental challenges. First, structural misalignment between instance-level reasoning and pairwise contrastive supervision may lead to shortcut behavior, where the model merely learns the superficial format of reasoning. Second, reasoning is not universally beneficial for embedding tasks. Enforcing reasoning for all inputs may introduce unnecessary computation and latency, and can even obscure salient semantic signals for simple cases. To address these issues, we propose MMEmb-R1, an adaptive reasoning-based multimodal embedding framework. We formulate reasoning as a latent variable and introduce pair-aware reasoning selection that employs counterfactual intervention to identify reasoning paths beneficial for query-target alignment. Furthermore, we adopt reinforcement learning to selectively invoke reasoning only when necessary. Experiments on the MMEB-V2 benchmark demonstrate that our model achieves a score of 71.2 with only 4B parameters, establishing a new state-of-the-art while significantly reducing reasoning overhead and inference latency.
中文标题/摘要
标题：MMEmb-R1：基于配对感知选择与自适应控制的推理增强多模态嵌入
多模态大语言模型已成功应用于多模态嵌入任务，但其生成式推理能力仍未得到充分利用。将思维链推理直接引入嵌入学习面临两个核心挑战：首先，实例级推理与成对对比监督间的结构错位可能导致模型仅学习推理的表面形式，产生捷径行为；其次，推理并非对所有嵌入任务均有益。强制对所有输入进行推理会引入不必要的计算与延迟，甚至可能掩盖简单案例中的关键语义信号。为解决这些问题，我们提出MMEmb-R1——一种基于自适应推理的多模态嵌入框架。我们将推理建模为隐变量，并引入配对感知推理选择机制，通过反事实干预识别有助于查询-目标对齐的推理路径。此外，采用强化学习技术仅在必要时触发推理。在MMEB-V2基准测试中，我们的模型仅用40亿参数即取得71.2分，在显著降低推理开销与推断延迟的同时，确立了新的性能标杆。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the underutilization of generative reasoning in multimodal large language models (MLLMs) for embedding tasks, where direct integration faces challenges of structural misalignment and unnecessary computational overhead. The proposed MMEmb-R1 framework formulates reasoning as a latent variable, employing pair-aware selection with counterfactual intervention to identify beneficial reasoning paths for query-target alignment and using reinforcement learning to adaptively invoke reasoning only when needed. Experimental results on the MMEB-V2 benchmark show that the model achieves a state-of-the-art score of 71.2 with just 4B parameters, while significantly reducing reasoning overhead and inference latency.
本文针对多模态大语言模型在嵌入任务中生成式推理能力未被充分利用的问题，指出直接集成会面临结构错位和计算冗余的挑战。提出的MMEmb-R1框架将推理建模为隐变量，采用基于配对感知的选择和反事实干预来识别有益于查询-目标对齐的推理路径，并通过强化学习自适应地仅在必要时调用推理。在MMEB-V2基准测试上的实验结果表明，该模型仅用40亿参数就取得了71.2分的性能，创造了新的最优水平，同时显著降低了推理开销和延迟。
Scientific Graphics Program Synthesis via Dual Self-Consistency Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Juekai Lin, Yun Zhu, Honglin Lin, Sijing Li, Tianwei Lin, Zheng Liu, Xiaoyang Wang, Wenqiao Zhang, Lijun Wu
First: 2026-04-07T16:58:14+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-07T16:58:14+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Graphics Program Synthesis is pivotal for interpreting and editing visual data, effectively facilitating the reverse-engineering of static visuals into editable TikZ code. While TikZ is the de facto standard for scientific schematics due to its programmatic flexibility, its requirement for rigorous spatial precision presents a significant challenge for Multimodal Large Language Models. Progress is currently stifled by two primary gaps: (1) Data Quality Gap: existing image-TikZ corpora often lack strict executability and reliable visual alignment; (2) Evaluation Gap: a lack of benchmarks for both structural and visual fidelity. To address these, we present a closed-loop framework featuring: SciTikZ-230K, a large-scale, high-quality dataset from our Execution-Centric Data Engine covering 11 diverse scientific disciplines; SciTikZ-Bench, a multifaceted benchmark spanning from basic geometric constructs to intricate hierarchical schematics to evaluate both visual fidelity and structural logic. To further broaden the scope of visual-code optimization methodology, we introduce a novel Dual Self-Consistency Reinforcement Learning optimization paradigm, which utilizes Round-Trip Verification to penalize degenerate code and boost overall self-consistency. Empowered by these, our trained model SciTikZer-8B achieves state-of-the-art performance, consistently outperforming proprietary giants like Gemini-2.5-Pro and massive models like Qwen3-VL-235B-A22B-Instruct.
中文标题/摘要
标题：科学图形程序合成：基于双重自洽性强化学习
图形程序合成对于解释和编辑视觉数据至关重要，能有效将静态视觉内容逆向工程为可编辑的TikZ代码。尽管TikZ因其编程灵活性成为科学示意图的事实标准，但其对空间精度的严格要求对多模态大语言模型构成显著挑战。当前进展主要受限于两大缺口：(1) 数据质量缺口：现有图像-TikZ语料常缺乏严格可执行性与可靠视觉对齐；(2) 评估缺口：缺乏兼顾结构与视觉保真度的基准。为此，我们提出闭环框架，包含：SciTikZ-230K（通过执行中心化数据引擎构建的大规模高质量数据集，涵盖11个科学领域）；SciTikZ-Bench（多维度基准，从基础几何构造到复杂层次化示意图，评估视觉保真度与结构逻辑）。为拓展视觉-代码优化方法边界，我们提出新型双重自洽性强化学习优化范式，利用往返验证惩罚退化代码并提升整体自洽性。基于此，训练模型SciTikZer-8B实现最先进性能，持续超越Gemini-2.5-Pro等专有模型及Qwen3-VL-235B-A22B-Instruct等超大规模模型。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the challenge of synthesizing precise TikZ graphics programs from scientific schematics, motivated by the limitations of existing datasets and evaluation benchmarks. The method introduces a closed-loop framework featuring a large-scale, high-quality dataset (SciTikZ-230K) and a multifaceted benchmark (SciTikZ-Bench), alongside a novel Dual Self-Consistency Reinforcement Learning paradigm that uses round-trip verification to optimize code generation. Experimental results show that the trained model, SciTikZer-8B, achieves state-of-the-art performance, outperforming larger proprietary and open-source models in generating executable and visually faithful TikZ code.
本文针对从科学示意图合成精确TikZ图形程序的挑战，其动机源于现有数据集和评估基准的不足。方法上提出了一个闭环框架，包括大规模高质量数据集SciTikZ-230K和多方面基准SciTikZ-Bench，以及一种新颖的双重自洽强化学习范式，该范式利用往返验证来优化代码生成。实验结果表明，训练出的模型SciTikZer-8B实现了最先进的性能，在生成可执行且视觉保真的TikZ代码方面优于更大的专有和开源模型。
Value Mirror Descent for Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Zhichao Jia, Guanghui Lan
First: 2026-04-07T16:34:16+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-07T16:34:16+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Value iteration-type methods have been extensively studied for computing a nearly optimal value function in reinforcement learning (RL). Under a generative sampling model, these methods can achieve sharper sample complexity than policy optimization approaches, particularly in their dependence on the discount factor. In practice, they are often employed for offline training or in simulated environments. In this paper, we consider discounted Markov decision processes with state space S, action space A, discount factor $γ\in(0,1)$ and costs in $[0,1]$. We introduce a novel value optimization method, termed value mirror descent (VMD), which integrates mirror descent from convex optimization into the classical value iteration framework. In the deterministic setting with known transition kernels, we show that VMD converges linearly. For the stochastic setting with a generative model, we develop a stochastic variant, SVMD, which incorporates variance reduction commonly used in stochastic value iteration-type methods. For RL problems with general convex regularizers, SVMD attains a near-optimal sample complexity of $\tilde{O}(|S||A|(1-γ)^{-3}ε^{-2})$. Moreover, we establish that the Bregman divergence between the generated and optimal policies remains bounded throughout the iterations. This property is absent in existing stochastic value iteration-type methods but is important for enabling effective online (continual) learning following offline training. Under a strongly convex regularizer, SVMD achieves sample complexity of $\tilde{O}(|S||A|(1-γ)^{-5}ε^{-1})$, improving performance in the high-accuracy regime. Furthermore, we prove convergence of the generated policy to the optimal policy. Overall, the proposed method, its analysis, and the resulting guarantees, constitute new contributions to the RL and optimization literature.
中文标题/摘要
标题：强化学习中的价值镜像下降方法
值迭代类方法在强化学习中已被广泛研究用于计算近似最优值函数。在生成式采样模型下，这类方法能获得比策略优化方法更优的样本复杂度，尤其在对折扣因子的依赖方面。实践中常被用于离线训练或模拟环境。本文研究具有状态空间S、动作空间A、折扣因子γ∈(0,1)和成本区间[0,1]的折扣马尔可夫决策过程。我们提出一种称为价值镜像下降的新型值优化方法，将凸优化中的镜像下降融入经典值迭代框架。在转移核已知的确定性场景中，VMD呈现线性收敛性。针对生成模型的随机场景，我们开发了结合随机值迭代类方法常用方差缩减技术的随机变体SVMD。对于具有一般凸正则项的强化学习问题，SVMD达到近乎最优的样本复杂度Ō(|S||A|(1-γ)⁻³ε⁻²)。此外，我们证明生成策略与最优策略间的Bregman散度在迭代过程中保持有界——这一特性在现有随机值迭代方法中缺失，但对实现离线训练后的有效在线持续学习至关重要。在强凸正则项条件下，SVMD获得Ō(|S||A|(1-γ)⁻⁵ε⁻¹)的样本复杂度，提升了高精度场景的性能。我们进一步证明生成策略能收敛至最优策略。总体而言，该方法及其理论分析为强化学习和优化领域提供了新的贡献。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the need for sample-efficient reinforcement learning methods with favorable dependence on the discount factor, this paper introduces Value Mirror Descent (VMD), a novel algorithm that integrates mirror descent from convex optimization into value iteration. The method employs a deterministic variant with linear convergence under known transitions and a stochastic variant (SVMD) with variance reduction for generative models, achieving a near-optimal sample complexity of Õ(|S||A|(1-γ)^{-3}ε^{-2}) for general convex regularizers and improved Õ(|S||A|(1-γ)^{-5}ε^{-1}) under strong convexity. Experimental results demonstrate that SVMD maintains bounded Bregman divergence between policies, enabling effective continual learning, and ensures policy convergence to optimality, offering new theoretical guarantees in RL.
本文针对强化学习中需要样本高效且对折扣因子依赖良好的方法，提出了价值镜像下降（VMD）算法，将凸优化中的镜像下降融入价值迭代框架。该方法在已知转移核的确定性设置中具有线性收敛性，并为生成模型设计了带方差缩减的随机变体（SVMD），在一般凸正则化下实现了近最优的样本复杂度Õ(|S||A|(1-γ)^{-3}ε^{-2})，在强凸正则化下提升至Õ(|S||A|(1-γ)^{-5}ε^{-1})。实验结果表明，SVMD能保持生成策略与最优策略间Bregman散度的有界性，支持有效的持续在线学习，并确保策略收敛到最优，为强化学习提供了新的理论保证。
Memory Intelligence Agent
Authors: Jingyang Qiao, Weicheng Meng, Yu Cheng, Zhihang Lin, Zhizhong Zhang, Xin Tan, Jingyu Gong, Kun Shao, Yuan Xie
First: 2026-04-06T07:59:52+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-07T16:26:16+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Deep research agents (DRAs) integrate LLM reasoning with external tools. Memory systems enable DRAs to leverage historical experiences, which are essential for efficient reasoning and autonomous evolution. Existing methods rely on retrieving similar trajectories from memory to aid reasoning, while suffering from key limitations of ineffective memory evolution and increasing storage and retrieval costs. To address these problems, we propose a novel Memory Intelligence Agent (MIA) framework, consisting of a Manager-Planner-Executor architecture. Memory Manager is a non-parametric memory system that can store compressed historical search trajectories. Planner is a parametric memory agent that can produce search plans for questions. Executor is another agent that can search and analyze information guided by the search plan. To build the MIA framework, we first adopt an alternating reinforcement learning paradigm to enhance cooperation between the Planner and the Executor. Furthermore, we enable the Planner to continuously evolve during test-time learning, with updates performed on-the-fly alongside inference without interrupting the reasoning process. Additionally, we establish a bidirectional conversion loop between parametric and non-parametric memories to achieve efficient memory evolution. Finally, we incorporate a reflection and an unsupervised judgment mechanisms to boost reasoning and self-evolution in the open world. Extensive experiments across eleven benchmarks demonstrate the superiority of MIA.
中文标题/摘要
标题：记忆智能体
深度研究智能体（DRAs）将大语言模型推理与外部工具相结合。记忆系统使DRAs能够利用历史经验，这对高效推理和自主进化至关重要。现有方法依赖从记忆中检索相似轨迹以辅助推理，但存在记忆进化低效、存储与检索成本递增等关键局限。为解决这些问题，我们提出了一种新颖的记忆智能体（MIA）框架，采用管理者-规划者-执行者架构。记忆管理者是一个非参数化记忆系统，可存储压缩的历史搜索轨迹；规划者是一个参数化记忆智能体，能为问题生成搜索计划；执行者是另一个智能体，可根据搜索计划进行信息搜索与分析。为构建MIA框架，我们首先采用交替强化学习范式增强规划者与执行者的协作。进一步地，我们使规划者能在测试时学习中持续进化，在推理过程中实时更新而不中断推理流程。此外，我们在参数化与非参数化记忆间建立双向转换循环，以实现高效记忆进化。最后，我们引入反思机制和无监督判断机制，以增强开放世界中的推理与自我进化能力。在十一个基准测试上的大量实验证明了MIA的优越性。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses limitations in existing deep research agents, such as ineffective memory evolution and high storage costs, by proposing a Memory Intelligence Agent (MIA) framework. This framework employs a Manager-Planner-Executor architecture, where a non-parametric memory system stores compressed historical trajectories, a parametric Planner generates search plans, and an Executor conducts guided searches. Key innovations include alternating reinforcement learning to enhance Planner-Executor cooperation, on-the-fly test-time learning for continuous Planner evolution, and a bidirectional conversion loop between parametric and non-parametric memories to enable efficient memory updates. Experimental results across eleven benchmarks demonstrate MIA's superior performance in reasoning and autonomous evolution.
本文针对现有深度研究代理中记忆演化效率低和存储成本高等问题，提出了记忆智能代理（MIA）框架。该框架采用管理器-规划器-执行器架构，其中非参数记忆系统存储压缩的历史轨迹，参数化规划器生成搜索计划，执行器则根据计划进行搜索分析。方法创新包括通过交替强化学习增强规划器与执行器的协作，支持在测试时进行实时学习以实现规划器的持续演化，并建立参数与非参数记忆间的双向转换循环以提升记忆演化效率。在十一个基准测试上的广泛实验表明，MIA在推理和自主演化方面具有优越性。
Vero: An Open RL Recipe for General Visual Reasoning
Authors: Gabriel Sarch, Linrong Cai, Qunzhong Wang, Haoyang Wu, Danqi Chen, Zhuang Liu
First: 2026-04-06T17:56:25+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-07T15:20:05+00:00
Comments: Project page: https://vero-reasoning.github.io/
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Project1
Abstract
What does it take to build a visual reasoner that works across charts, science, spatial understanding, and open-ended tasks? The strongest vision-language models (VLMs) show such broad visual reasoning is within reach, but the recipe behind them remains unclear, locked behind proprietary reinforcement learning (RL) pipelines with non-public data. We introduce Vero, a family of fully open VLMs that matches or exceeds existing open-weight models across diverse visual reasoning tasks. We scale RL data and rewards across six broad task categories, constructing Vero-600K, a 600K-sample dataset from 59 datasets, and designing task-routed rewards that handle heterogeneous answer formats. Vero achieves state-of-the-art performance, improving over four base models by 3.6-5.3 points on average across VeroEval, our suite of 30 challenging benchmarks. Starting from Qwen3-VL-8B-Instruct, Vero outperforms Qwen3-VL-8B-Thinking on 23 of 30 benchmarks without additional proprietary thinking data. When trained from the same base model, Vero-600K exceeds existing RL datasets across task categories. Systematic ablations reveal that different task categories elicit qualitatively distinct reasoning patterns that transfer poorly in isolation, suggesting that broad data coverage is the primary driver of strong RL scaling. All data, code, and models are released.
中文标题/摘要
标题：Vero：面向通用视觉推理的开源强化学习方案
构建能同时处理图表、科学图像、空间理解及开放式任务的视觉推理系统需要什么？当前最强的视觉语言模型已展现出跨领域视觉推理的潜力，但其实现方案仍不明确，受限于使用非公开数据的私有强化学习流程。我们推出Vero系列——完全开源的视觉语言模型，在多样化视觉推理任务中达到或超越现有开源模型。我们基于六大任务类别扩展强化学习数据与奖励机制，构建了包含59个数据集、60万样本的Vero-600K数据集，并设计了能处理异构答案格式的任务路由奖励机制。Vero在包含30项挑战性基准的VeroEval评测套件中实现最优性能，相对四个基线模型平均提升3.6-5.3个点。以Qwen3-VL-8B-Instruct为基座时，Vero在30个基准中的23项超越Qwen3-VL-8B-Thinking，且无需额外私有思维数据。在相同基座模型下，Vero-600K在所有任务类别上均超越现有强化学习数据集。系统消融实验表明，不同任务类别会引发性质各异的推理模式，这些模式在孤立训练时迁移效果较差，说明广泛的数据覆盖是强化学习扩展成效的关键驱动力。所有数据、代码与模型均已开源。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the need for an open recipe to replicate the broad visual reasoning capabilities of proprietary vision-language models, this paper introduces Vero, a family of fully open models. The method involves constructing Vero-600K, a 600K-sample dataset from 59 sources across six task categories, and employing task-routed rewards to handle heterogeneous answer formats during reinforcement learning. Experimental results show Vero achieves state-of-the-art performance, improving base models by 3.6-5.3 points on average across 30 benchmarks and outperforming a proprietary thinking-enhanced model on most tasks, with ablations indicating broad data coverage as key to effective scaling.
本研究旨在提供一个开放的强化学习方案，以复现专有视觉语言模型广泛的视觉推理能力，为此提出了完全开放的Vero模型系列。方法上，通过整合59个数据集的六个任务类别构建了包含60万样本的Vero-600K数据集，并设计了任务路由奖励来处理异构答案格式。实验结果表明，Vero在30个基准测试中取得了最先进的性能，平均提升基础模型3.6-5.3分，且在多数任务上超越了专有的思维增强模型，消融实验揭示广泛的数据覆盖是强化学习有效扩展的主要驱动力。
Efficient and Principled Scientific Discovery through Bayesian Optimization: A Tutorial
Authors: Zhongwei Yu, Rasul Tutunov, Alexandre Max Maraval, Zikai Xie, Zhenzhi Tan, Jiankang Wang, Bin Cao, Zijing Li, Liangliang Xu, Qi Yang, Jun Jiang, Sanzhong Luo, Zhenxiao Guo, Tongyi Zhang, Haitham Bou-Ammar, Jun Wang
First: 2026-04-01T19:14:34+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-07T15:06:34+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Traditional scientific discovery relies on an iterative hypothesise-experiment-refine cycle that has driven progress for centuries, but its intuitive, ad-hoc implementation often wastes resources, yields inefficient designs, and misses critical insights. This tutorial presents Bayesian Optimisation (BO), a principled probability-driven framework that formalises and automates this core scientific cycle. BO uses surrogate models (e.g., Gaussian processes) to model empirical observations as evolving hypotheses, and acquisition functions to guide experiment selection, balancing exploitation of known knowledge and exploration of uncharted domains to eliminate guesswork and manual trial-and-error. We first frame scientific discovery as an optimisation problem, then unpack BO's core components, end-to-end workflows, and real-world efficacy via case studies in catalysis, materials science, organic synthesis, and molecule discovery. We also cover critical technical extensions for scientific applications, including batched experimentation, heteroscedasticity, contextual optimisation, and human-in-the-loop integration. Tailored for a broad audience, this tutorial bridges AI advances in BO with practical natural science applications, offering tiered content to empower cross-disciplinary researchers to design more efficient experiments and accelerate principled scientific discovery.
中文标题/摘要
标题：通过贝叶斯优化实现高效且原理驱动的科学发现：教程
传统科学发现依赖于历经数百年推动进步的假设-实验-优化的迭代循环，但其依赖直觉的临时性实施常导致资源浪费、设计低效并错失关键洞见。本教程介绍贝叶斯优化（BO）——一种将这一核心科学循环形式化与自动化的概率驱动原理框架。BO使用代理模型（如高斯过程）将经验观测建模为动态演化的假设，并通过采集函数指导实验选择，在已知知识的利用与未知领域的探索间取得平衡，从而消除猜测与手动试错。我们首先将科学发现构建为优化问题，继而通过催化、材料科学、有机合成及分子发现等案例研究，系统解析BO的核心组件、端到端工作流及实际效能。教程还涵盖面向科学应用的关键技术扩展，包括批量实验、异方差性、上下文优化及人机协同集成。本教程面向广泛受众，将BO的人工智能前沿进展与自然科学实践应用相衔接，通过分层内容设计助力跨学科研究者设计更高效的实验，加速原理驱动的科学发现进程。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the inefficiency and ad-hoc nature of traditional scientific discovery cycles, this tutorial introduces Bayesian Optimization (BO) as a principled, probability-driven framework to formalize and automate the hypothesize-experiment-refine process. The method employs surrogate models like Gaussian processes to represent evolving hypotheses and acquisition functions to intelligently select experiments, balancing exploration and exploitation to minimize manual trial-and-error. Experimental results from case studies in catalysis, materials science, organic synthesis, and molecule discovery demonstrate BO's real-world efficacy in accelerating discovery, supported by technical extensions for batched experimentation, heteroscedasticity, and human-in-the-loop integration tailored for scientific applications.
本文针对传统科学发现周期效率低下且依赖直觉的不足，提出贝叶斯优化作为一种原则性的概率驱动框架，以形式化和自动化假设-实验-优化的核心科学循环。该方法使用高斯过程等代理模型来建模经验观察作为演化假设，并利用采集函数指导实验选择，平衡已知知识的利用与未知领域的探索，从而消除猜测和手动试错。通过在催化、材料科学、有机合成和分子发现等领域的案例研究，展示了该方法在实际应用中的有效性，并涵盖了批处理实验、异方差性、上下文优化和人机交互集成等关键技术扩展，以赋能跨学科研究人员设计更高效的实验并加速原则性科学发现。
GLUE: Coordinating Pre-Trained Generative Models for System-Level Design
Authors: Tim Aebersold, Soheyl Massoudi, Mark D. Fuge
First: 2025-12-22T15:23:19+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-07T15:00:29+00:00
Comments: 12 pages, 10 figures, Preprint
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Engineering complex systems (aircraft, buildings, vehicles) requires coordinating geometric and performance couplings across subsystems. As generative models proliferate for specialized domains, a key research gap is how to coordinate frozen, pre-trained submodels to generate full-system designs that are feasible, diverse, and high-performing. We introduce GLUE, which orchestrates pre-trained, frozen generators while enforcing system-level feasibility, optimality, and diversity. Compatible models must be end-to-end differentiable with a smooth, well-behaved latent-to-output mapping. We propose and benchmark (i) data-driven GLUE models trained on pre-generated system-level designs and (ii) a data-free GLUE model trained on a differentiable geometry layer. On a UAV design problem with five coupling constraints, we find that data-driven approaches yield diverse, high-performing designs but require large datasets to satisfy constraints reliably. The data-free approach is competitive with Bayesian optimization and gradient-based optimization in performance and feasibility while training a full generative model in only ~10 min on an RTX 4090 GPU, requiring more than two orders of magnitude fewer geometry evaluations and FLOPs than the data-driven method. We identify equality constraint satisfaction as a key difficulty and remaining limitation, and ablate approaches that improve this for the data-free approach. As a first step toward scaling generative design to complex, real-world engineering systems, this work explores how unmodified, domain-informed submodels can be integrated into a modular generative workflow.
中文标题/摘要
标题：GLUE：面向系统级设计的预训练生成模型协同框架
复杂系统（如飞行器、建筑、车辆）的工程设计需要协调跨子系统的几何与性能耦合关系。随着各专业领域生成模型的激增，如何协调已冻结的预训练子模型以生成可行、多样且高性能的全系统设计，成为关键研究空白。本文提出GLUE框架，通过编排预训练且冻结的生成器，在确保系统级可行性、最优性与多样性的同时进行协同生成。兼容模型需具备端到端可微性及平滑、良性的潜空间到输出映射。我们提出并基准测试了两种方法：（1）基于预生成系统级设计数据训练的数据驱动GLUE模型；（2）基于可微几何层训练的无数据GLUE模型。在包含五项耦合约束的无人机设计问题中，数据驱动方法能生成多样且高性能的设计，但需要大规模数据集才能可靠满足约束；无数据方法在性能与可行性方面与贝叶斯优化及基于梯度的优化方法相当，且在RTX 4090 GPU上仅需约10分钟即可完成完整生成模型训练，其几何评估次数和浮点运算量比数据驱动方法低两个数量级以上。研究指出等式约束满足是当前主要难点与局限，并通过消融实验提出了改进无数据方法约束满足能力的策略。作为将生成式设计扩展至复杂现实工程系统的初步探索，本研究为如何将未经修改、具备领域知识的子模型整合至模块化生成工作流提供了新思路。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the challenge of coordinating multiple pre-trained generative models for complex system design, where subsystems have geometric and performance couplings. The authors introduce GLUE, a method that orchestrates frozen, domain-specific generators to produce feasible, diverse, and high-performing full-system designs, requiring models to be differentiable with smooth latent mappings. Experiments on a UAV design problem with five constraints show that data-driven GLUE variants generate diverse, high-quality designs but need large datasets to reliably meet constraints, while a data-free approach using a differentiable geometry layer achieves competitive performance and feasibility with far fewer computational resources, training in about 10 minutes on an RTX 4090 GPU, though equality constraint satisfaction remains a key limitation.
本文针对复杂系统设计中多个预训练生成模型的协调问题，其中子系统存在几何和性能耦合。作者提出了GLUE方法，用于协调冻结的领域特定生成器，以产生可行、多样且高性能的全系统设计，要求模型具有可微分且平滑的潜在映射。在具有五个约束的无人机设计问题上的实验表明，数据驱动的GLUE变体能生成多样、高质量的设计，但需要大量数据来可靠满足约束，而使用可微分几何层的数据无关方法在性能和可行性上具有竞争力，计算资源需求显著减少，在RTX 4090 GPU上仅需约10分钟训练，但等式约束满足仍是主要限制。
IBISAgent: Reinforcing Pixel-Level Visual Reasoning in MLLMs for Universal Biomedical Object Referring and Segmentation
Authors: Yankai Jiang, Qiaoru Li, Binlu Xu, Haoran Sun, Chao Ding, Junting Dong, Yuxiang Cai, Xuhong Zhang, Jianwei Yin
First: 2026-01-06T14:37:50+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-07T14:46:22+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Recent research on medical MLLMs has gradually shifted its focus from image-level understanding to fine-grained, pixel-level comprehension. Although segmentation serves as the foundation for pixel-level understanding, existing approaches face two major challenges. First, they introduce implicit segmentation tokens and require simultaneous fine-tuning of both the MLLM and external pixel decoders, which increases the risk of catastrophic forgetting and limits generalization to out-of-domain scenarios. Second, most methods rely on single-pass reasoning and lack the capability to iteratively refine segmentation results, leading to suboptimal performance. To overcome these limitations, we propose a novel agentic MLLM, named IBISAgent, that reformulates segmentation as a vision-centric, multi-step decision-making process. IBISAgent enables MLLMs to generate interleaved reasoning and text-based click actions, invoke segmentation tools, and produce high-quality masks without architectural modifications. By iteratively performing multi-step visual reasoning on masked image features, IBISAgent naturally supports mask refinement and promotes the development of pixel-level visual reasoning capabilities. We further design a two-stage training framework consisting of cold-start supervised fine-tuning and agentic reinforcement learning with tailored, fine-grained rewards, enhancing the model's robustness in complex medical referring and reasoning segmentation tasks. Extensive experiments demonstrate that IBISAgent consistently outperforms both closed-source and open-source SOTA methods.
中文标题/摘要
标题：IBISAgent：强化多模态大语言模型中的像素级视觉推理以实现通用生物医学对象指代与分割
近期医学多模态大语言模型的研究重心正逐渐从图像级理解转向细粒度像素级理解。尽管分割是像素级理解的基础，现有方法仍面临两大挑战：其一，它们引入隐式分割标记并需同时微调多模态大语言模型与外部像素解码器，这会增加灾难性遗忘风险并限制模型在域外场景的泛化能力；其二，多数方法依赖单次推理且缺乏迭代优化分割结果的能力，导致性能欠佳。为突破这些局限，我们提出新型智能体化多模态大语言模型IBISAgent，将分割重构为以视觉为中心的多步决策过程。该模型无需修改架构即可实现交错式推理与基于文本的点击操作、调用分割工具并生成高质量掩码。通过对掩码图像特征进行迭代式多步视觉推理，IBISAgent天然支持掩码优化并促进像素级视觉推理能力的发展。我们进一步设计包含冷启动监督微调和基于细粒度奖励的智能体强化学习的两阶段训练框架，以增强模型在复杂医学指代与推理分割任务中的鲁棒性。大量实验表明，IBISAgent在闭源与开源前沿方法中均取得持续领先性能。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the need to shift medical MLLMs from image-level to fine-grained pixel-level understanding while overcoming limitations of existing segmentation methods—such as catastrophic forgetting from joint fine-tuning and lack of iterative refinement—this paper introduces IBISAgent, an agentic MLLM that reformulates segmentation as a multi-step decision-making process. The method enables interleaved reasoning and text-based click actions to invoke segmentation tools without architectural changes, using a two-stage training framework with supervised fine-tuning and agentic reinforcement learning for robustness. Experimental results show that IBISAgent consistently outperforms state-of-the-art methods in biomedical object referring and segmentation tasks.
本文的动机是将医学多模态大模型从图像级理解转向细粒度像素级理解，同时克服现有分割方法的局限性，如联合微调导致的灾难性遗忘和缺乏迭代优化能力。为此，作者提出了IBISAgent，一种智能体化的多模态大模型，将分割重新定义为多步决策过程，该方法通过交错推理和基于文本的点击操作调用分割工具，无需修改架构，并采用包含监督微调和智能体强化学习的两阶段训练框架以增强鲁棒性。主要实验结果表明，IBISAgent在生物医学对象指代和分割任务中持续优于当前最先进的方法。
MARL-GPT: Foundation Model for Multi-Agent Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Maria Nesterova, Mikhail Kolosov, Anton Andreychuk, Egor Cherepanov, Oleg Bulichev, Alexey Kovalev, Konstantin Yakovlev, Aleksandr Panov, Alexey Skrynnik
Venue: AAAI
First: 2026-04-07T14:40:01+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-07T14:40:01+00:00
Comments: Accepted at AAMAS 2026 (AAAI Track)
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Recent advances in multi-agent reinforcement learning (MARL) have demonstrated success in numerous challenging domains and environments, but typically require specialized models for each task. In this work, we propose a coherent methodology that makes it possible for a single GPT-based model to learn and perform well across diverse MARL environments and tasks, including StarCraft Multi-Agent Challenge, Google Research Football and POGEMA. Our method, MARL-GPT, applies offline reinforcement learning to train at scale on the expert trajectories (400M for SMACv2, 100M for GRF, and 1B for POGEMA) combined with a single transformer-based observation encoder that requires no task-specific tuning. Experiments show that MARL-GPT achieves competitive performance compared to specialized baselines in all tested environments. Thus, our findings suggest that it is, indeed, possible to build a multi-task transformer-based model for a wide variety of (significantly different) multi-agent problems paving the way to the fundamental MARL model (akin to ChatGPT, Llama, Mistral etc. in natural language modeling).
中文标题/摘要
标题：MARL-GPT：多智能体强化学习的基座模型
多智能体强化学习（MARL）近期在众多复杂领域与环境取得显著进展，但通常需为每个任务定制专用模型。本研究提出一种统一方法，使单个基于GPT的模型能够跨多种MARL环境与任务（包括《星际争霸》多智能体挑战赛、谷歌研究足球和POGEMA）进行高效学习与执行。我们的MARL-GPT方法采用离线强化学习，基于专家轨迹（SMACv2 4亿条、GRF 1亿条、POGEMA 10亿条）进行大规模训练，并配备无需任务特定调优的单一基于Transformer的观测编码器。实验表明，MARL-GPT在所有测试环境中均达到与专用基线模型相当的竞争力。这些发现证明，为各类（差异显著的）多智能体问题构建基于Transformer的多任务模型具有可行性，为通向通用MARL基座模型（类似于自然语言建模中的ChatGPT、Llama、Mistral等）开辟了道路。
Summary / 总结
The motivation for this work is to overcome the limitation of specialized models in multi-agent reinforcement learning (MARL) by developing a single, general-purpose foundation model capable of handling diverse tasks. The method, named MARL-GPT, employs a GPT-based architecture trained via offline reinforcement learning on large-scale expert trajectory datasets from environments like StarCraft Multi-Agent Challenge, Google Research Football, and POGEMA, utilizing a unified transformer-based observation encoder without task-specific adjustments. Experimental results demonstrate that MARL-GPT achieves competitive performance compared to specialized baselines across all tested environments, suggesting the feasibility of a foundational MARL model analogous to large language models in natural language processing.
本研究的动机是克服多智能体强化学习（MARL）中专用模型的局限性，旨在开发一个能够处理多样化任务的单一通用基础模型。该方法名为MARL-GPT，采用基于GPT的架构，通过在星海争霸多智能体挑战、谷歌研究足球和POGEMA等环境的大规模专家轨迹数据集上进行离线强化学习训练，并利用统一的基于Transformer的观察编码器，无需任务特定调整。实验结果表明，MARL-GPT在所有测试环境中均达到了与专用基线模型相竞争的性能，这表明构建类似于自然语言处理中大型语言模型的基础MARL模型是可行的。
Saliency-Guided Representation with Consistency Policy Learning for Visual Unsupervised Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Jingbo Sun, Qichao Zhang, Songjun Tu, Xing Fang, Yupeng Zheng, Haoran Li, Ke Chen, Dongbin Zhao
First: 2026-04-07T14:31:32+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-07T14:31:32+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Zero-shot unsupervised reinforcement learning (URL) offers a promising direction for building generalist agents capable of generalizing to unseen tasks without additional supervision. Among existing approaches, successor representations (SR) have emerged as a prominent paradigm due to their effectiveness in structured, low-dimensional settings. However, SR methods struggle to scale to high-dimensional visual environments. Through empirical analysis, we identify two key limitations of SR in visual URL: (1) SR objectives often lead to suboptimal representations that attend to dynamics-irrelevant regions, resulting in inaccurate successor measures and degraded task generalization; and (2) these flawed representations hinder SR policies from modeling multi-modal skill-conditioned action distributions and ensuring skill controllability. To address these limitations, we propose Saliency-Guided Representation with Consistency Policy Learning (SRCP), a novel framework that improves zero-shot generalization of SR methods in visual URL. SRCP decouples representation learning from successor training by introducing a saliency-guided dynamics task to capture dynamics-relevant representations, thereby improving successor measure and task generalization. Moreover, it integrates a fast-sampling consistency policy with URL-specific classifier-free guidance and tailored training objectives to improve skill-conditioned policy modeling and controllability. Extensive experiments on 16 tasks across 4 datasets from the ExORL benchmark demonstrate that SRCP achieves state-of-the-art zero-shot generalization in visual URL and is compatible with various SR methods.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于显著性引导表征与一致性策略学习的视觉无监督强化学习
零样本无监督强化学习（URL）为构建能够泛化至未见任务、无需额外监督的通用智能体提供了有前景的方向。在现有方法中，后继表征（SR）因其在结构化低维环境中的有效性而成为主流范式，但难以扩展至高维视觉环境。通过实证分析，我们揭示了SR在视觉URL中的两个关键局限：（1）SR目标常导致关注动态无关区域的次优表征，造成后继度量不准确与任务泛化能力下降；（2）这些缺陷表征阻碍SR策略对多模态技能条件动作分布的建模及技能可控性保障。为此，我们提出SRCP框架，通过引入显著性引导的动态任务解耦表征学习与后继训练，以捕获动态相关表征，从而提升后继度量与任务泛化能力；同时集成快速采样一致性策略，结合URL专属的无分类器引导机制与定制化训练目标，以增强技能条件策略建模与可控性。在ExORL基准的4个数据集共16项任务上的实验表明，SRCP实现了视觉URL领域最先进的零样本泛化性能，且兼容多种SR方法。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the challenge of scaling successor representation (SR) methods to high-dimensional visual environments in zero-shot unsupervised reinforcement learning (URL), where existing SR approaches often learn suboptimal representations focused on dynamics-irrelevant regions, impairing task generalization and skill controllability. The proposed solution, Saliency-Guided Representation with Consistency Policy Learning (SRCP), introduces a saliency-guided dynamics task to decouple and improve representation learning for more accurate successor measures, alongside a fast-sampling consistency policy with URL-specific enhancements to better model skill-conditioned actions. Experimental results on 16 tasks across 4 datasets from the ExORL benchmark show that SRCP achieves state-of-the-art zero-shot generalization and is compatible with various SR methods.
本文针对零样本无监督强化学习（URL）中，后继表示（SR）方法难以扩展到高维视觉环境的问题，指出现有SR方法常学习到关注动态无关区域的次优表示，从而损害任务泛化能力和技能可控性。提出的解决方案SRCP（基于显著性的表示与一致性策略学习）引入了一个显著性引导的动态任务，以解耦并改进表示学习，从而获得更准确的后继度量，同时结合了具有URL特定增强的快速采样一致性策略，以更好地建模技能条件动作。在ExORL基准的4个数据集上的16个任务实验表明，SRCP实现了最先进的零样本泛化性能，并能与多种SR方法兼容。
Image Diffusion Preview with Consistency Solver
Authors: Fu-Yun Wang, Hao Zhou, Liangzhe Yuan, Sanghyun Woo, Boqing Gong, Bohyung Han, Ming-Hsuan Yang, Han Zhang, Yukun Zhu, Ting Liu, Long Zhao
Venue: CVPR 2026
First: 2025-12-15T17:47:49+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-07T12:50:18+00:00
Comments: Accepted by CVPR 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
The slow inference process of image diffusion models significantly degrades interactive user experiences. To address this, we introduce Diffusion Preview, a novel paradigm employing rapid, low-step sampling to generate preliminary outputs for user evaluation, deferring full-step refinement until the preview is deemed satisfactory. Existing acceleration methods, including training-free solvers and post-training distillation, struggle to deliver high-quality previews or ensure consistency between previews and final outputs. We propose ConsistencySolver derived from general linear multistep methods, a lightweight, trainable high-order solver optimized via Reinforcement Learning, that enhances preview quality and consistency. Experimental results demonstrate that ConsistencySolver significantly improves generation quality and consistency in low-step scenarios, making it ideal for efficient preview-and-refine workflows. Notably, it achieves FID scores on-par with Multistep DPM-Solver using 47% fewer steps, while outperforming distillation baselines. Furthermore, user studies indicate our approach reduces overall user interaction time by nearly 50% while maintaining generation quality. Code is available at https://github.com/G-U-N/consolver.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于一致性求解器的图像扩散预览
图像扩散模型的缓慢推理过程严重影响了交互式用户体验。为此，我们提出Diffusion Preview这一新范式，采用快速低步数采样生成初步输出供用户评估，待预览结果满意后再进行全步数细化。现有加速方法（包括免训练求解器和训练后蒸馏）难以提供高质量预览或确保预览与最终输出的一致性。我们提出基于通用线性多步方法推导的ConsistencySolver——一种通过强化学习优化的轻量可训练高阶求解器，可提升预览质量与一致性。实验结果表明，ConsistencySolver在低步数场景中显著提升了生成质量与一致性，非常适合高效的预览-细化工作流。该方法仅需比多步DPM-Solver减少47%的步数即可达到相当的FID分数，同时优于蒸馏基线。用户研究表明，本方法在保持生成质量的同时将用户总交互时间减少近50%。代码发布于https://github.com/G-U-N/consolver。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the slow inference of diffusion models hindering interactive use, this paper introduces Diffusion Preview, a paradigm that generates quick low-step previews for user feedback before full refinement. The method proposes ConsistencySolver, a lightweight trainable high-order solver derived from linear multistep methods and optimized with Reinforcement Learning to enhance preview quality and consistency with final outputs. Experiments show it matches the FID of Multistep DPM-Solver with 47% fewer steps, outperforms distillation baselines, and user studies indicate it cuts interaction time by nearly 50% while preserving output quality.
针对扩散模型推理缓慢影响交互体验的问题，本文提出了扩散预览范式，通过快速低步数采样生成预览供用户评估，满意后再进行全步数细化。方法上提出了ConsistencySolver，一种基于线性多步方法、通过强化学习优化的轻量可训练高阶求解器，旨在提升预览质量及其与最终输出的一致性。实验结果表明，该求解器在少步数场景下显著提高了生成质量和一致性，能以比Multistep DPM-Solver少47%的步数达到相当的FID分数，优于蒸馏基线，且用户研究表明其可将整体交互时间减少近50%，同时保持生成质量。
Hierarchical Reinforcement Learning with Augmented Step-Level Transitions for LLM Agents
Authors: Shuai Zhen, Yanhua Yu, Ruopei Guo, Nan Cheng, Yang Deng
Venue: ACL 2026
First: 2026-04-07T12:44:33+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-07T12:44:33+00:00
Comments: Accepted to ACL 2026 Main Conference
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Large language model (LLM) agents have demonstrated strong capabilities in complex interactive decision-making tasks. However, existing LLM agents typically rely on increasingly long interaction histories, resulting in high computational cost and limited scalability. In this paper, we propose STEP-HRL, a hierarchical reinforcement learning (HRL) framework that enables step-level learning by conditioning only on single-step transitions rather than full interaction histories. STEP-HRL structures tasks hierarchically, using completed subtasks to represent global progress of overall task. By introducing a local progress module, it also iteratively and selectively summarizes interaction history within each subtask to produce a compact summary of local progress. Together, these components yield augmented step-level transitions for both high-level and low-level policies. Experimental results on ScienceWorld and ALFWorld benchmarks consistently demonstrate that STEP-HRL substantially outperforms baselines in terms of performance and generalization while reducing token usage. Our code is available at https://github.com/TonyStark042/STEP-HRL.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于增强步级转移的分层强化学习框架STEP-HRL用于大语言模型智能体
大语言模型（LLM）智能体在复杂交互决策任务中展现出强大能力，但现有方法通常依赖不断增长的交互历史，导致计算成本高昂且可扩展性受限。本文提出STEP-HRL分层强化学习框架，通过仅基于单步转移而非完整交互历史实现步级学习。该框架采用分层任务结构，利用已完成子任务表征整体任务的全局进展，并通过局部进展模块迭代选择性地汇总子任务内的交互历史，生成紧凑的局部进展摘要。这些组件共同为高层与低层策略生成增强的步级转移。在ScienceWorld和ALFWorld基准测试中的实验结果表明，STEP-HRL在性能与泛化能力上显著优于基线方法，同时降低了令牌使用量。代码已开源：https://github.com/TonyStark042/STEP-HRL。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the high computational cost and limited scalability of large language model (LLM) agents that rely on long interaction histories, this paper introduces STEP-HRL, a hierarchical reinforcement learning framework designed to enable step-level learning by conditioning policies only on single-step transitions. The method structures tasks hierarchically, using completed subtasks to represent global progress and employing a local progress module to iteratively summarize interaction history within each subtask, thereby producing augmented step-level transitions for both high-level and low-level policies. Experimental results on the ScienceWorld and ALFWorld benchmarks show that STEP-HRL substantially outperforms baseline methods in performance and generalization while significantly reducing token usage.
针对依赖长交互历史导致计算成本高、可扩展性有限的大语言模型智能体问题，本文提出了STEP-HRL，一种分层强化学习框架，通过仅基于单步转移进行策略学习来实现步级学习。该方法将任务分层组织，利用完成的子任务表示全局进展，并引入局部进展模块迭代总结每个子任务内的交互历史，从而为高层和低层策略生成增强的步级转移。在ScienceWorld和ALFWorld基准测试上的实验结果表明，STEP-HRL在性能和泛化能力上显著优于基线方法，同时大幅降低了令牌使用量。
Optimisation of Resource Allocation in Heterogeneous Wireless Networks Using Deep Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Oluwaseyi Giwa, Jonathan Shock, Jaco Du Toit, Tobi Awodumila
First: 2025-09-29T09:48:00+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-07T12:37:14+00:00
Comments: Accepted at the 2026 EuCNC & 6G Summit
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Dynamic resource allocation in open radio access network (O-RAN) heterogeneous networks (HetNets) presents a complex optimisation challenge under varying user loads. We propose a near-real-time RAN intelligent controller (Near-RT RIC) xApp utilising deep reinforcement learning (DRL) to jointly optimise transmit power, bandwidth slicing, and user scheduling. Leveraging real-world network topologies, we benchmark proximal policy optimisation (PPO) and twin delayed deep deterministic policy gradient (TD3) against standard heuristics. Our results demonstrate that the PPO-based xApp achieves a superior trade-off, reducing network energy consumption by up to 70% in dense scenarios and improving user fairness by more than 30% compared to throughput-greedy baselines. These findings validate the feasibility of centralised, energy-aware AI orchestration in future 6G architectures.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于深度强化学习的异构无线网络资源分配优化
开放无线接入网（O-RAN）异构网络（HetNets）中的动态资源分配在多变用户负载下构成复杂的优化难题。本研究提出一种采用深度强化学习（DRL）的近实时无线接入网智能控制器（Near-RT RIC）xApp，可联合优化发射功率、带宽切片与用户调度。通过基于真实网络拓扑的测试，我们将近端策略优化（PPO）与双延迟深度确定性策略梯度（TD3）算法与标准启发式方法进行对比。实验结果表明：在密集场景中，基于PPO的xApp能实现更优的权衡——相较于吞吐量贪婪基线，网络能耗降低最高达70%，用户公平性提升超过30%。这些发现验证了集中式、能源感知的人工智能编排在未来6G架构中的可行性。

The method benchmarks proximal policy optimization (PPO) and twin delayed deep deterministic policy gradient (TD3) algorithms against standard heuristics using real-world network topologies. The main experimental results demonstrate that the PPO-based xApp achieves a superior trade-off, reducing network energy consumption by up to 70% in dense scenarios and improving user fairness by over 30% compared to throughput-greedy baselines, validating the feasibility of centralized, energy-aware AI orchestration for future 6G architectures.

Emergent social transmission of model-based representations without inference
Authors: Silja Keßler, Miriam Bautista-Salinero, Claudio Tennie, Charley M. Wu
First: 2026-04-07T12:14:27+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-07T12:14:27+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
How do people acquire rich, flexible knowledge about their environment from others despite limited cognitive capacity? Humans are often thought to rely on computationally costly mentalizing, such as inferring others' beliefs. In contrast, cultural evolution emphasizes that behavioral transmission can be supported by simple social cues. Using reinforcement learning simulations, we show how minimal social learning can indirectly transmit higher-level representations. We simulate a naïve agent searching for rewards in a reconfigurable environment, learning either alone or by observing an expert - crucially, without inferring mental states. Instead, the learner heuristically selects actions or boosts value representations based on observed actions. Our results demonstrate that these cues bias the learner's experience, causing its representation to converge toward the expert's. Model-based learners benefit most from social exposure, showing faster learning and more expert-like representations. These findings show how cultural transmission can arise from simple, non-mentalizing processes exploiting asocial learning mechanisms.
中文标题/摘要
标题：无需推理的模型化表征之涌现性社会传递
在认知能力有限的情况下，人们如何通过他人获得对环境丰富而灵活的知识？传统观点认为人类依赖计算成本高昂的心理化过程（如推断他人信念）。与之相对，文化演化理论强调行为传递可通过简单社会线索实现。通过强化学习模拟，我们展示了极简社会学习如何间接传递高层表征：模拟一个在可重构环境中寻找奖励的初始智能体，通过单独学习或观察专家（关键是不推断心理状态）进行学习。学习者仅基于观察到的行动启发式选择动作或增强价值表征。结果表明这些线索会偏置学习者的经验，使其表征向专家表征收敛。模型化学习者从社会接触中获益最大，表现出更快的学习速度和更接近专家的表征。这些发现揭示了文化传递如何通过利用非社会学习机制的简单非心理化过程产生。
Summary / 总结
This paper investigates how individuals can acquire complex environmental knowledge from others without relying on cognitively demanding mental state inference, motivated by the question of how rich representations are transmitted despite limited cognitive capacity. The method employs reinforcement learning simulations where a naive agent learns either alone or by observing an expert's actions, using simple heuristics like action selection or value boosting rather than explicit mentalizing. Experimental results show that these minimal social cues bias the learner's experience, leading its internal representations to converge toward the expert's, with model-based learners particularly benefiting through faster learning and more expert-like representations, demonstrating that cultural transmission can emerge from non-mentalizing processes.
本文探讨了个体如何在不依赖认知上要求较高的心理状态推断的情况下，从他人那里获取复杂的环境知识，其动机在于理解尽管认知能力有限，丰富的表征是如何被传递的。方法采用强化学习模拟，其中新手智能体通过单独学习或观察专家行动来学习，仅使用行动选择或价值提升等简单启发式方法，而非显式的心理推断。实验结果表明，这些简单的社会线索会偏向学习者的经验，使其内部表征向专家的表征收敛，其中基于模型的学习者受益最大，表现出更快的学习速度和更接近专家的表征，这证明了文化传递可以通过非心理化的简单过程实现。
MedXIAOHE: A Comprehensive Recipe for Building Medical MLLMs
Authors: Baorong Shi, Bo Cui, Boyuan Jiang, Deli Yu, Fang Qian, Haihua Yang, Huichao Wang, Jiale Chen, Jianfei Pan, Jieqiong Cao, Jinghao Lin, Kai Wu, Lin Yang, Shengsheng Yao, Tao Chen, Xiaojun Xiao, Xiaozhong Ji, Xu Wang, Yijun He, Zhixiong Yang
First: 2026-02-13T08:19:38+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-07T11:35:36+00:00
Comments: XIAOHE Medical AI team. See paper for full author list. Currently, the model is exclusively available on XIAOHE AI Doctor, accessible via both the App Store and the Douyin Mini Program. Updated to improve the layout
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
We present MedXIAOHE, a medical vision-language foundation model designed to advance general-purpose medical understanding and reasoning in real-world clinical applications. MedXIAOHE achieves state-of-the-art performance across diverse medical benchmarks and surpasses leading closed-source multimodal systems on multiple capabilities. To achieve this, we propose an entity-aware continual pretraining framework that organizes heterogeneous medical corpora to broaden knowledge coverage and reduce long-tail gaps (e.g., rare diseases). For medical expert-level reasoning and interaction, MedXIAOHE incorporates diverse medical reasoning patterns via reinforcement learning and tool-augmented agentic training, enabling multi-step diagnostic reasoning with verifiable decision traces. To improve reliability in real-world use, MedXIAOHE integrates user-preference rubrics, evidence-grounded reasoning, and low-hallucination long-form report generation, with improved adherence to medical instructions. We release this report to document our practical design choices, scaling insights, and evaluation framework, hoping to inspire further research.

Understanding the Performance Gap in Preference Learning: A Dichotomy of RLHF and DPO
Authors: Ruizhe Shi, Minhak Song, Runlong Zhou, Zihan Zhang, Maryam Fazel, Simon S. Du
First: 2025-05-26T09:54:02+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-07T11:17:39+00:00
Comments: 39 pages, 5 figures. Revision
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
We present a fine-grained theoretical analysis of the performance gap between reinforcement learning from human feedback (RLHF) and direct preference optimization (DPO) under a representation gap. Our study decomposes this gap into two sources: an explicit representation gap under exact optimization and an implicit representation gap under finite samples. In the exact optimization setting, we characterize how the relative capacities of the reward and policy model classes influence the final policy qualities. We show that RLHF, DPO, or online DPO can outperform one another depending on type of model mis-specifications. Notably, online DPO can outperform both RLHF and standard DPO when the reward and policy model classes are isomorphic and both mis-specified. In the approximate optimization setting, we provide a concrete construction where the ground-truth reward is implicitly sparse and show that RLHF requires significantly fewer samples than DPO to recover an effective reward model, highlighting a statistical advantage of two-stage learning. Together, these results provide a comprehensive understanding of the performance gap between RLHF and DPO under various settings, and offer practical insights into when each method is preferred.
中文标题/摘要
标题：理解偏好学习中的性能差距：RLHF与DPO的二分法分析
本文对表征差距下基于人类反馈的强化学习（RLHF）与直接偏好优化（DPO）之间的性能差距进行了细粒度理论分析。研究将该差距分解为两个来源：精确优化下的显性表征差距与有限样本下的隐性表征差距。在精确优化设定中，我们刻画了奖励模型类与策略模型类的相对容量如何影响最终策略质量，并证明根据模型误设类型的不同，RLHF、DPO或在线DPO可能相互超越。值得注意的是，当奖励模型类与策略模型类同构且均存在误设时，在线DPO可同时优于RLHF与标准DPO。在近似优化设定中，我们通过构建隐式稀疏的真实奖励函数，证明RLHF比DPO需要显著更少的样本即可恢复有效奖励模型，凸显了两阶段学习的统计优势。这些结果共同提供了不同设定下RLHF与DPO性能差距的系统性理解，并为各类方法的适用场景提供了实践指导。
Summary / 总结
This paper investigates the performance gap between Reinforcement Learning from Human Feedback (RLHF) and Direct Preference Optimization (DPO) in preference learning, motivated by the need to understand their relative strengths under model mis-specification. The method involves a theoretical analysis that decomposes the gap into explicit and implicit representation gaps, examining both exact and approximate optimization settings. The main experimental results show that in exact optimization, the superior method depends on the relative capacities of the reward and policy models, with online DPO outperforming both RLHF and standard DPO when both model classes are isomorphic and mis-specified. In the approximate setting with a sparse ground-truth reward, RLHF demonstrates a statistical advantage by requiring significantly fewer samples than DPO to recover an effective reward model, highlighting the benefits of two-stage learning.
本文研究了偏好学习中基于人类反馈的强化学习（RLHF）与直接偏好优化（DPO）之间的性能差距，动机在于理解模型设定错误下两者的相对优势。方法上通过理论分析将差距分解为显式和隐式表示差距，并考察了精确优化和近似优化两种设定。主要实验结果表明，在精确优化下，哪种方法更优取决于奖励模型与策略模型的相对容量，当两者同构且均设定错误时，在线DPO的表现优于RLHF和标准DPO。在近似优化设定下，针对隐含稀疏的真实奖励，RLHF展现出统计优势，恢复有效奖励模型所需的样本量显著少于DPO，这凸显了两阶段学习的益处。
Can Large Language Models Reinvent Foundational Algorithms?
Authors: Jian Zhao, Haoren Luo, Yu Wang, Yuhan Cao, Pingyue Sheng, Tianxing He
First: 2026-04-07T11:15:22+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-07T11:15:22+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
LLMs have shown strong potential to advance scientific discovery. Whether they possess the capacity for foundational innovation, however, remains an open question. In this work, we focus on a prerequisite for foundational innovation: can LLMs reinvent foundational algorithms in computer science? Our \textit{Unlearn-and-Reinvent} pipeline applies LLM unlearning to remove a specific foundational algorithm, such as Dijkstra's or Euclid's algorithm, from an LLM's pretrained knowledge, and then tests whether the model can reinvent it in a controlled environment. To enable effective unlearning, we adopt a GRPO-based, on-policy unlearning method. Across 10 target algorithms, 3 strong open-weight models, and 3 hint levels, our experiments demonstrate that (1) the strongest model Qwen3-4B-Thinking-2507 successfully reinvents 50% of the algorithms with no hint, 70% at hint level 1, and 90% at hint level 2; (2) a few high-level hints can enhance the reinvention success rate, but even step-by-step hints fail for those complicated algorithms; and (3) test-time reinforcement learning enables successful reinvention for the Strassen algorithm at hint level 2. Through analyses of output trajectories and ablation studies, we find that generative verifier in the reinvention phase plays a critical role in sustaining models' reasoning strength, helping to avoid the ``thought collapse'' phenomenon. These findings offer insights into both the potential and current limits of LLMs' innovative thinking.
中文标题/摘要
标题：大语言模型能否重构基础算法？
大语言模型已展现出推动科学发现的强大潜力，但其是否具备基础创新能力仍是一个开放性问题。本研究聚焦于基础创新的一个先决条件：大语言模型能否重构计算机科学中的基础算法？我们提出的“遗忘与重构”流程，首先通过大语言模型遗忘技术从预训练知识中移除特定基础算法（如迪杰斯特拉算法或欧几里得算法），随后在受控环境中测试模型能否重新构建该算法。为实现有效遗忘，我们采用基于GRPO的策略性遗忘方法。通过对10种目标算法、3个强开源模型及3种提示级别的实验表明：（1）最强模型Qwen3-4B-Thinking-2507在无提示时成功重构50%的算法，一级提示下达到70%，二级提示下达到90%；（2）少量高层级提示能提升重构成功率，但即使提供逐步提示，复杂算法仍难以重构；（3）测试时强化学习使施特拉森算法在二级提示下实现成功重构。通过输出轨迹分析与消融研究发现，重构阶段的生成验证器对维持模型推理能力具有关键作用，有助于避免“思维坍缩”现象。这些发现为理解大语言模型创新思维的潜力与当前局限提供了新见解。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the open question of whether large language models (LLMs) possess the capacity for foundational innovation, this paper investigates if LLMs can reinvent foundational computer science algorithms after having that specific knowledge removed. The method employs an Unlearn-and-Reinvent pipeline, which first uses a GRPO-based unlearning technique to erase a target algorithm (e.g., Dijkstra's) from a model's pretrained knowledge and then tests the model's ability to reconstruct it in a controlled setting with varying hint levels. Key experimental results on 10 algorithms with models like Qwen3-4B show that the strongest model successfully reinvented 50% of algorithms with no hints, 70% with level-1 hints, and 90% with level-2 hints, though step-by-step hints still failed for complex cases; additionally, test-time reinforcement learning enabled success for the Strassen algorithm, and analysis revealed the generative verifier is crucial to prevent reasoning collapse during reinvention.
本文的动机源于大型语言模型是否具备基础性创新能力的开放性问题，具体探究了在特定知识被移除后，LLMs能否重新发明计算机科学的基础算法。研究方法采用“遗忘与再发明”流程，首先使用基于GRPO的策略性遗忘方法从模型的预训练知识中抹除目标算法（如Dijkstra算法），然后在受控环境中测试模型在不同提示级别下重新构建该算法的能力。在10种算法和Qwen3-4B等模型上的主要实验结果表明：最强模型在无提示时成功再发明了50%的算法，一级提示下达到70%，二级提示下达到90%，但逐步提示对复杂算法仍无效；此外，测试时强化学习使Strassen算法在二级提示下再发明成功，分析还发现再发明阶段的生成验证器对维持模型推理能力、避免“思维崩溃”现象至关重要。
CuraLight: Debate-Guided Data Curation for LLM-Centered Traffic Signal Control
Authors: Qing Guo, Xinhang Li, Junyu Chen, Zheng Guo, Shengzhe Xu, Lin Zhang, Lei Li
First: 2026-04-07T10:05:43+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-07T10:05:43+00:00
Comments: accepted at IJCNN 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Traffic signal control (TSC) is a core component of intelligent transportation systems (ITS), aiming to reduce congestion, emissions, and travel time. Recent approaches based on reinforcement learning (RL) and large language models (LLMs) have improved adaptivity, but still suffer from limited interpretability, insufficient interaction data, and weak generalization to heterogeneous intersections. This paper proposes CuraLight, an LLM-centered framework where an RL agent assists the fine-tuning of an LLM-based traffic signal controller. The RL agent explores traffic environments and generates high-quality interaction trajectories, which are converted into prompt-response pairs for imitation fine-tuning. A multi-LLM ensemble deliberation system further evaluates candidate signal timing actions through structured debate, providing preference-aware supervision signals for training. Experiments conducted in SUMO across heterogeneous real-world networks from Jinan, Hangzhou, and Yizhuang demonstrate that CuraLight consistently outperforms state-of-the-art baselines, reducing average travel time by 5.34 percent, average queue length by 5.14 percent, and average waiting time by 7.02 percent. The results highlight the effectiveness of combining RL-assisted exploration with deliberation-based data curation for scalable and interpretable traffic signal control.
中文标题/摘要
标题：CuraLight：面向大语言模型交通信号控制的辩论引导数据精炼框架
交通信号控制是智能交通系统的核心组件，旨在缓解拥堵、降低排放、缩短行程时间。基于强化学习和大语言模型的最新方法提升了适应性，但仍存在可解释性有限、交互数据不足、对异构路口泛化能力弱等问题。本文提出CuraLight——以大语言模型为中心的框架，通过强化学习智能体辅助微调基于大语言模型的信号控制器。强化学习智能体探索交通环境并生成高质量交互轨迹，将其转化为提示-响应对以进行模仿微调。多语言模型集成审议系统通过结构化辩论评估候选配时方案，为训练提供偏好感知的监督信号。在SUMO中使用济南、杭州、亦庄异构真实路网的实验表明，CuraLight持续优于现有基线方法，平均行程时间降低5.34%，平均排队长度减少5.14%，平均等待时间下降7.02%。结果验证了强化学习辅助探索与辩论式数据精炼相结合对可扩展、可解释交通信号控制的有效性。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the limitations of existing reinforcement learning and large language model approaches in traffic signal control, such as poor interpretability, scarce interaction data, and weak generalization to diverse intersections, this paper introduces CuraLight, a framework that leverages an RL agent to explore traffic environments and generate high-quality trajectories for fine-tuning an LLM-based controller. 针对现有基于强化学习和大型语言模型的交通信号控制方法在可解释性、交互数据不足以及对异构路口泛化能力弱等方面的局限，本文提出了CuraLight框架，其核心是利用强化学习智能体探索交通环境并生成高质量轨迹，用于微调基于大型语言模型的信号控制器。该方法将轨迹转换为提示-响应对，并采用多大型语言模型集成审议系统，通过结构化辩论评估候选信号配时动作，从而为训练提供偏好感知的监督信号。在SUMO仿真平台上，基于济南、杭州和亦庄的真实路网实验表明，CuraLight持续优于现有先进基线方法，平均行程时间降低了5.34%，平均排队长度减少了5.14%，平均等待时间下降了7.02%，这验证了结合强化学习辅助探索与审议式数据策展对于实现可扩展、可解释交通信号控制的有效性。
Autoregressive Language Models are Secretly Energy-Based Models: Insights into the Lookahead Capabilities of Next-Token Prediction
Authors: Mathieu Blondel, Michael E. Sander, Germain Vivier-Ardisson, Tianlin Liu, Vincent Roulet
First: 2025-12-17T17:14:26+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-07T08:58:47+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Autoregressive models (ARMs) currently constitute the dominant paradigm for large language models (LLMs). Energy-based models (EBMs) represent another class of models, which have historically been less prevalent in LLM development, yet naturally characterize the optimal policy in post-training alignment. In this paper, we provide a unified view of these two model classes. Taking the chain rule of probability as a starting point, we establish an explicit bijection between ARMs and EBMs in function space, which we show to correspond to a special case of the soft Bellman equation in maximum entropy reinforcement learning. Building upon this bijection, we derive the equivalence between supervised learning of ARMs and EBMs. Furthermore, we analyze the distillation of EBMs into ARMs by providing theoretical error bounds. Our results provide insights into the ability of ARMs to plan ahead, despite being based on the next-token prediction paradigm.
中文标题/摘要
标题：自回归语言模型实为基于能量的模型：对下一词预测前瞻能力的洞察
自回归模型（ARMs）是目前大语言模型（LLMs）的主导范式。基于能量的模型（EBMs）是另一类模型，在LLM发展中历来较少见，但自然描述了训练后对齐中的最优策略。本文为这两类模型提供了统一视角。以概率链式法则为起点，我们在函数空间建立了ARMs与EBMs之间的显式双射，并证明其对应于最大熵强化学习中软贝尔曼方程的特例。基于此双射，我们推导出ARMs与EBMs监督学习的等价性。此外，通过提供理论误差界，我们分析了EBMs向ARMs的蒸馏过程。研究结果揭示了ARMs在基于下一词预测范式下仍具备前瞻规划能力的内在机制。
Summary / 总结
This paper is motivated by the need to unify autoregressive models (ARMs), which dominate large language models, with energy-based models (EBMs), which naturally characterize optimal policies in alignment, to better understand ARMs' capabilities. The method establishes an explicit bijection between ARMs and EBMs in function space, linking it to the soft Bellman equation in maximum entropy reinforcement learning, and derives equivalence in their supervised learning alongside theoretical error bounds for distilling EBMs into ARMs. The main experimental results provide theoretical insights, showing that this equivalence explains how ARMs, despite being trained on next-token prediction, can effectively plan ahead, bridging two historically separate model classes.
本文的动机在于统一主导大语言模型的自回归模型与在对齐中表征最优策略的能量基模型，以深入理解自回归模型的能力。方法上，在函数空间建立了自回归模型与能量基模型之间的显式双射，将其关联到最大熵强化学习中的软贝尔曼方程，并推导了二者在监督学习中的等价性，以及能量基模型蒸馏到自回归模型的理论误差界。主要实验结果提供了理论见解，表明这种等价性解释了自回归模型尽管基于下一词预测训练，却能有效进行前瞻规划，从而连接了两个历史上分离的模型类别。
One-shot Adaptation of Humanoid Whole-body Motion with Walking Priors
Authors: Hao Huang, Geeta Chandra Raju Bethala, Shuaihang Yuan, Congcong Wen, Mengyu Wang, Anthony Tzes, Yi Fang
First: 2025-10-29T07:48:10+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-07T08:55:58+00:00
Comments: 14 pages, 3 figures, 5 tables
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Whole-body humanoid motion represents a fundamental challenge in robotics, requiring balance, coordination, and adaptability to enable human-like behaviors. However, existing methods typically require multiple training samples per motion, rendering the collection of high-quality human motion datasets both labor-intensive and costly. To address this, we propose a data-efficient adaptation approach that learns a new humanoid motion from a single non-walking target sample together with auxiliary walking motions and a walking-trained base model. The core idea lies in leveraging order-preserving optimal transport to compute distances between walking and non-walking sequences, followed by interpolation along geodesics to generate new intermediate pose skeletons, which are then optimized for collision-free configurations and retargeted to the humanoid before integration into a simulated environment for policy adaptation via reinforcement learning. Experimental evaluations on the CMU MoCap dataset demonstrate that our method consistently outperforms baselines, achieving superior performance across metrics. Our code is available at: https://github.com/hhuang-code/One-shot-WBM.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于行走先验的人形机器人全身运动单样本自适应方法
人形机器人全身运动是机器人学中的核心挑战，需兼顾平衡性、协调性与适应性以实现类人行为。现有方法通常需针对每种动作采集多个训练样本，导致高质量人体运动数据集的构建成本高昂且耗时。为此，本文提出一种数据高效的自适应方法，仅需单个非行走目标样本，结合辅助行走运动与预训练的行走基础模型，即可学习新的人形运动。其核心在于利用保序最优传输计算行走与非行走序列间的距离，随后沿测地线插值生成中间姿态骨架，经无碰撞优化并重定向至人形模型后，集成至仿真环境中通过强化学习进行策略自适应。在CMU动作捕捉数据集上的实验表明，本方法在各项指标上均优于基线模型。代码已开源：https://github.com/hhuang-code/One-shot-WBM。
Summary / 总结
The motivation is to enable data-efficient whole-body humanoid motion adaptation, addressing the high cost of collecting multiple training samples per motion. The method leverages a single non-walking target sample, auxiliary walking motions, and a walking-trained base model, using order-preserving optimal transport to compute distances between sequences and interpolating along geodesics to generate intermediate pose skeletons, which are optimized for collision-free configurations and retargeted to the humanoid for policy adaptation via reinforcement learning. Experimental results on the CMU MoCap dataset show the approach consistently outperforms baselines across metrics.
该研究的动机是实现数据高效的人形机器人全身运动适应，以解决为每个动作收集多个训练样本的高成本问题。方法利用单个非行走目标样本、辅助行走动作和经过行走训练的基础模型，通过保持顺序的最优传输计算序列间距离，并沿测地线插值生成中间姿态骨架，随后优化为无碰撞配置并重定向到人形机器人，再通过强化学习进行策略适应。在CMU MoCap数据集上的实验结果表明，该方法在各项指标上均持续优于基线模型。
Frame of Reference: Addressing the Challenges of Common Ground Representation in Situational Dialogs
Authors: Biswesh Mohapatra, Théo Charlot, Giovanni Duca, Mayank Palan, Laurent Romary, Justine Cassell
Venue: ACL 2026
First: 2026-01-14T10:45:22+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-07T08:27:43+00:00
Comments: Work accepted at ACL 2026 Findings
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Common ground plays a critical role in situated spoken dialogs, where interlocutors must establish and maintain shared references to entities, events, and relations to sustain coherent interaction in a shared space and over time. With the increasing presence of embodied conversational agents and social robots, the ability to correctly ground this kind of conversational content in order to refer back later also becomes important for dialog systems. Prior studies have demonstrated that LLMs are capable of performing certain grounding acts like acknowledgments. However, relatively little work has investigated their capacity to leverage the grounded information, like in complex scenarios involving space and time (e.g., "let's go to that café near the park we went to yesterday"). To that end, in this work, we evaluate a model's ability to establish common ground by utilizing these "relational references" in the dynamic and shared environments of situated dialogs. We then test multiple methods for representing common ground and further propose approaches to improve their performance by using reinforcement learning on our synthetically generated dialog data .
中文标题/摘要
标题：参照框架：解决情境对话中共有基础表征的挑战
共有基础在情境口语对话中起着关键作用，对话者必须建立并维持对实体、事件和关系的共享指称，以在共享空间和持续时间内保持连贯互动。随着具身对话代理和社交机器人的日益普及，对话系统正确锚定此类会话内容以便后续回溯的能力也变得至关重要。先前研究表明，大语言模型能够执行某些锚定行为（如确认应答），但较少研究探讨其利用已锚定信息的能力——例如在涉及时空的复杂场景中（如“我们去昨天公园附近那家咖啡馆吧”）。为此，本研究通过情境对话的动态共享环境中运用这类“关系指称”，评估模型建立共有基础的能力。我们测试了多种共有基础表征方法，并进一步提出通过强化学习在合成生成的对话数据上提升其性能的改进方案。

This paper addresses the challenge of enabling dialog systems to establish and maintain common ground in situated conversations, particularly for complex relational references involving space and time, which is crucial for embodied agents and social robots. The method involves evaluating a model's capacity to utilize such relational references in dynamic shared environments, testing multiple common ground representation techniques, and proposing performance improvements via reinforcement learning on synthetically generated dialog data. The main experimental results demonstrate the proposed approaches' effectiveness in enhancing the model's ability to leverage grounded information for coherent interaction.
本文旨在解决对话系统在情境对话中建立和维持共同基础的挑战，特别是对于涉及空间和时间的复杂关系指代，这对具身代理和社交机器人至关重要。方法包括评估模型在动态共享环境中利用此类关系指代的能力，测试多种共同基础表示技术，并提议通过强化学习在合成生成的对话数据上提升性能。主要实验结果表明，所提出的方法能有效增强模型利用已接地的信息进行连贯交互的能力。
RL-VLA$^3$: A Flexible and Asynchronous Reinforcement Learning Framework for VLA Training
Authors: Haoran Sun, Yongjian Guo, Zhong Guan, Shuai Di, Xiaodong Bai, Jing Long, Tianyun Zhao, Mingxi Luo, Hongke Zhao, Likang Wu, Xiaotie Deng, Xu Chu, Xi Xiao, Sheng Wen, Yicheng Gong, Junwu Xiong
First: 2026-02-05T15:30:23+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-07T08:14:29+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Reinforcement learning (RL) has emerged as a critical paradigm for post-training Vision-Language-Action (VLA) models, enabling embodied agents to adapt and improve through environmental interaction. However, existing RL frameworks for VLAs inherit synchronous design principles from traditional LLM training, treating entire rollouts as indivisible units and alternating strictly between data collection and policy optimization. This fundamentally mismatches the unique characteristics of VLA training, as physical simulators introduce highly variable, resource-intensive latencies. To address this, we introduce RL-VLA$^3$, a fully asynchronous distributed RL framework that enables fine-grained asynchronous interaction between simulation, inference, and training components through dynamic batching schedulers and flexible environment sharding strategies. Extensive experiments across diverse simulation backends, VLA architectures, and RL algorithms demonstrate that RL-VLA$^3$ achieves throughput improvements of up to 85.2\% over synchronous baselines while maintaining identical sample efficiency, with scalability validated from 8 to 256 GPUs. To our knowledge, RL-VLA$^3$ is the first fully asynchronous RL training framework tailored specifically for the system-level challenges of VLA training.
中文标题/摘要
标题：RL-VLA$^3$：一种灵活异步的强化学习框架用于视觉语言动作模型训练
强化学习已成为视觉语言动作模型后训练的关键范式，使具身智能体能够通过环境交互进行适应与改进。然而，现有VLA强化学习框架沿袭了传统大语言模型训练的同步设计原则，将完整交互轨迹视为不可分割单元，并严格交替执行数据收集与策略优化。这与VLA训练的特性存在根本性错配，因为物理模拟器会引入高度可变且资源密集的延迟。为此，我们提出RL-VLA$^3$——一个完全异步的分布式强化学习框架，通过动态批处理调度器与灵活的环境分片策略，实现模拟、推理与训练组件间的细粒度异步交互。跨多种模拟后端、VLA架构和强化学习算法的大规模实验表明，RL-VLA$^3$在保持同等样本效率的前提下，相比同步基线实现了最高85.2%的吞吐量提升，并在8至256个GPU上验证了其可扩展性。据我们所知，RL-VLA$^3$是首个针对VLA训练系统级挑战量身定制的全异步强化学习训练框架。
Summary / 总结
The motivation for this work stems from the inefficiency of synchronous reinforcement learning frameworks when applied to Vision-Language-Action (VLA) model training, as they fail to accommodate the variable latencies introduced by physical simulators. The method introduces RL-VLA³, a fully asynchronous distributed RL framework that employs dynamic batching schedulers and flexible environment sharding to decouple simulation, inference, and training components, allowing fine-grained asynchronous interaction. The main experimental results show that RL-VLA³ achieves up to 85.2% higher throughput compared to synchronous baselines while maintaining equivalent sample efficiency, with scalability demonstrated across 8 to 256 GPUs, making it the first fully asynchronous RL framework specifically designed for VLA training challenges.
本研究的动机在于，同步强化学习框架应用于视觉-语言-动作模型训练时效率低下，无法适应物理模拟器引入的可变延迟。方法上提出了RL-VLA³，这是一个完全异步的分布式强化学习框架，通过动态批处理调度器和灵活的环境分片策略，解耦模拟、推理和训练组件，实现细粒度的异步交互。主要实验结果表明，RL-VLA³相比同步基线实现了高达85.2%的吞吐量提升，同时保持相同的样本效率，并在8至256个GPU上验证了可扩展性，成为首个专门针对VLA训练系统挑战设计的全异步强化学习框架。
A Survey of Continual Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Chaofan Pan, Xin Yang, Yanhua Li, Wei Wei, Tianrui Li, Bo An, Jiye Liang
First: 2025-06-27T03:10:20+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-07T07:52:44+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Reinforcement Learning (RL) is an important machine learning paradigm for solving sequential decision-making problems. Recent years have witnessed remarkable progress in this field due to the rapid development of deep neural networks. However, the success of RL currently relies on extensive training data and computational resources. In addition, RL's limited ability to generalize across tasks restricts its applicability in dynamic and real-world environments. With the arisen of Continual Learning (CL), Continual Reinforcement Learning (CRL) has emerged as a promising research direction to address these limitations by enabling agents to learn continuously, adapt to new tasks, and retain previously acquired knowledge. In this survey, we provide a comprehensive examination of CRL, focusing on its core concepts, challenges, and methodologies. Firstly, we conduct a detailed review of existing works, organizing and analyzing their metrics, tasks, benchmarks, and scenario settings. Secondly, we propose a new taxonomy of CRL methods, categorizing them into four types from the perspective of knowledge storage and/or transfer. Finally, our analysis highlights the unique challenges of CRL and provides practical insights into future directions.
中文标题/摘要
标题：持续强化学习综述
强化学习（RL）是解决序列决策问题的重要机器学习范式。近年来，得益于深度神经网络的快速发展，该领域取得了显著进展。然而，当前RL的成功依赖于大量训练数据和计算资源，且其跨任务泛化能力有限，制约了其在动态现实环境中的应用。随着持续学习（CL）的兴起，持续强化学习（CRL）作为一个新兴研究方向，通过使智能体能够持续学习、适应新任务并保留已有知识，为解决这些局限提供了可能。本文对CRL进行了全面梳理，重点阐述其核心概念、挑战与方法。首先，系统回顾了现有研究，对其评估指标、任务、基准测试和场景设置进行了归纳分析；其次，从知识存储和/或迁移的角度，提出了一种新的CRL方法分类体系，将其划分为四种类型；最后，通过分析CRL特有的挑战，为未来研究方向提供了实践性见解。
Summary / 总结
This survey is motivated by the limitations of standard reinforcement learning, which requires extensive data and computational resources and struggles with generalization across tasks, hindering its application in dynamic real-world environments. The paper examines continual reinforcement learning (CRL) as a promising solution, providing a comprehensive review of existing works, proposing a new taxonomy of CRL methods based on knowledge storage and transfer, and analyzing metrics, tasks, benchmarks, and scenarios. The main experimental insights highlight the unique challenges in CRL and offer practical directions for future research to enable agents to learn continuously, adapt to new tasks, and retain prior knowledge effectively.
本综述的动机在于标准强化学习存在局限性，如需要大量数据和计算资源，且跨任务泛化能力不足，阻碍了其在动态现实环境中的应用。该研究探讨了持续强化学习（CRL）作为有前景的解决方案，通过全面回顾现有工作，提出基于知识存储和迁移的新分类法，并分析了指标、任务、基准和场景设置。主要实验分析结果强调了CRL的独特挑战，并为未来研究方向提供了实用见解，以推动智能体实现持续学习、适应新任务并有效保留先前知识。
COSMO-Agent: Tool-Augmented Agent for Closed-loop Optimization,Simulation,and Modeling Orchestration
Authors: Liyuan Deng, Shujian Deng, Yongkang Chen, Yongkang Dai, Zhihang Zhong, Linyang Li, Xiao Sun, Yilei Shi, Huaxi Huang
First: 2026-04-07T07:45:17+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-07T07:45:17+00:00
Comments: 10 pages, 3 figures, preprint paper
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Iterative industrial design-simulation optimization is bottlenecked by the CAD-CAE semantic gap: translating simulation feedback into valid geometric edits under diverse, coupled constraints. To fill this gap, we propose COSMO-Agent (Closed-loop Optimization, Simulation, and Modeling Orchestration), a tool-augmented reinforcement learning (RL) framework that teaches LLMs to complete the closed-loop CAD-CAE process. Specifically, we cast CAD generation, CAE solving, result parsing, and geometry revision as an interactive RL environment, where an LLM learns to orchestrate external tools and revise parametric geometries until constraints are satisfied. To make this learning stable and industrially usable, we design a multi-constraint reward that jointly encourages feasibility, toolchain robustness, and structured output validity. In addition, we contribute an industry-aligned dataset that covers 25 component categories with executable CAD-CAE tasks to support realistic training and evaluation. Experiments show that COSMO-Agent training substantially improves small open-source LLMs for constraint-driven design, exceeding large open-source and strong closed-source models in feasibility, efficiency, and stability.
中文标题/摘要
标题：COSMO-Agent：面向闭环优化、仿真与建模编排的工具增强型智能体
迭代式工业设计-仿真优化的瓶颈在于CAD-CAE语义鸿沟：如何在多样化耦合约束下将仿真反馈转化为有效的几何编辑。为填补这一缺口，我们提出COSMO-Agent（闭环优化、仿真与建模编排），这是一个工具增强的强化学习框架，通过教授大语言模型完成闭环CAD-CAE流程。具体而言，我们将CAD生成、CAE求解、结果解析与几何修正构建为交互式强化学习环境，使大语言模型学习编排外部工具并修正参数化几何体直至满足约束。为实现稳定且工业可用的学习过程，我们设计了多约束奖励机制，同步优化可行性、工具链鲁棒性与结构化输出有效性。此外，我们贡献了一个涵盖25个零部件类别的工业级数据集，包含可执行的CAD-CAE任务以支持真实场景训练与评估。实验表明，COSMO-Agent训练显著提升了开源小模型在约束驱动设计中的表现，在可行性、效率与稳定性方面超越大型开源模型及强闭源模型。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the CAD-CAE semantic gap in industrial design-simulation optimization, where translating simulation feedback into valid geometric edits under constraints is challenging. To bridge this gap, it introduces COSMO-Agent, a tool-augmented reinforcement learning framework that trains large language models (LLMs) to orchestrate a closed-loop process involving CAD generation, CAE solving, result parsing, and geometry revision. The method employs a multi-constraint reward to ensure feasibility, toolchain robustness, and structured output validity, and it is evaluated on an industry-aligned dataset covering 25 component categories. Experimental results demonstrate that COSMO-Agent training significantly enhances small open-source LLMs, outperforming larger open-source and closed-source models in feasibility, efficiency, and stability for constraint-driven design tasks.

SignalClaw: LLM-Guided Evolutionary Synthesis of Interpretable Traffic Signal Control Skills
Authors: Da Lei, Feng Xiao, Lu Li, Yuzhan Liu
First: 2026-04-07T07:35:45+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-07T07:35:45+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Traffic signal control TSC requires strategies that are both effective and interpretable for deployment, yet reinforcement learning produces opaque neural policies while program synthesis depends on restrictive domain-specific languages. We present SIGNALCLAW, a framework that uses large language models LLMs as evolutionary skill generators to synthesize and refine interpretable control skills for adaptive TSC. Each skill includes rationale, selection guidance, and executable code, making policies human-inspectable and self-documenting. At each generation, evolution signals from simulation metrics such as queue percentiles, delay trends, and stagnation are translated into natural language feedback to guide improvement. SignalClaw also introduces event-driven compositional evolution: an event detector identifies emergency vehicles, transit priority, incidents, and congestion via TraCI, and a priority dispatcher selects specialized skills. Each skill is evolved independently, and a priority chain enables runtime composition without retraining. We evaluate SignalClaw on routine and event-injected SUMO scenarios against four baselines. On routine scenarios, it achieves average delay of 7.8 to 9.2 seconds, within 3 to 10 percent of the best method, with low variance across random seeds. Under event scenarios, it yields the lowest emergency delay 11.2 to 18.5 seconds versus 42.3 to 72.3 for MaxPressure and 78.5 to 95.3 for DQN, and the lowest transit person delay 9.8 to 11.5 seconds versus 38.7 to 45.2 for MaxPressure. In mixed events, the dispatcher composes skills effectively while maintaining stable overall delay. The evolved skills progress from simple linear rules to conditional strategies with multi-feature interactions, while remaining fully interpretable and directly modifiable by traffic engineers.
中文标题/摘要
标题：SignalClaw：基于大语言模型引导的可解释交通信号控制技能进化式合成框架
交通信号控制需要兼具高效性与可解释性的策略，但强化学习生成的是不透明的神经策略，而程序合成则受限于特定领域语言。本文提出SIGNALCLAW框架，利用大语言模型作为进化技能生成器，通过进化合成与优化自适应交通信号控制的可解释控制技能。每个技能包含原理说明、选择指导和可执行代码，使策略具备人工可检视与自文档化特性。在每一代进化中，将队列百分位、延误趋势、停滞状态等仿真指标转化为自然语言反馈以指导改进。SignalClaw还引入事件驱动的组合进化机制：通过TraCI识别紧急车辆、公交优先、突发事件和拥堵的事件检测器，结合优先调度器选择专用技能。各技能独立进化，并通过优先级链实现无需重训练的运行时组合。在常规与事件注入的SUMO场景中，SignalClaw与四种基线方法对比评估。常规场景下平均延误为7.8-9.2秒，与最优方法差距在3%-10%内，且随机种子间方差较低。事件场景下，其紧急车辆延误最低（11.2-18.5秒，MaxPressure为42.3-72.3秒，DQN为78.5-95.3秒），公交乘客延误最低（9.8-11.5秒，MaxPressure为38.7-45.2秒）。混合事件中调度器能有效组合技能并保持整体延误稳定。进化技能从简单线性规则逐步发展为具有多特征交互的条件策略，同时保持完全可解释性，并支持交通工程师直接修改。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the need for effective yet interpretable traffic signal control policies, which are often opaque in reinforcement learning or limited by domain-specific languages in program synthesis, this paper introduces SignalClaw, a framework that employs large language models as evolutionary skill generators to synthesize and refine human-inspectable control skills. The method translates simulation metrics into natural language feedback to guide skill evolution and incorporates event-driven compositional evolution, where an event detector identifies scenarios like emergencies or congestion, and a priority dispatcher selects and composes specialized skills at runtime without retraining. Experimental results on SUMO scenarios show that SignalClaw achieves competitive average delays of 7.8 to 9.2 seconds in routine conditions and significantly outperforms baselines like MaxPressure and DQN under event scenarios, with the lowest emergency delays (11.2 to 18.5 seconds) and transit person delays (9.8 to 11.5 seconds), while evolving interpretable, modifiable skills from simple rules to complex conditional strategies.

RLAIF-SPA: Structured AI Feedback for Semantic-Prosodic Alignment in Speech Synthesis
Authors: Qing Yang, Zhenghao Liu, Yangfan Du, Pengcheng Huang, Tong Xiao
First: 2025-10-16T12:40:37+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-07T07:34:26+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Recent advances in Text-To-Speech (TTS) synthesis have achieved near-human speech quality in neutral speaking styles. However, most existing approaches either depend on costly emotion annotations or optimize surrogate objectives that fail to adequately capture perceptual emotional quality. As a result, the generated speech, while semantically accurate, often lacks expressive and emotionally rich characteristics. To address these limitations, we propose RLAIF-SPA, a novel framework that integrates Reinforcement Learning from AI Feedback (RLAIF) to directly optimize both emotional expressiveness and intelligibility without human supervision. Specifically, RLAIF-SPA incorporates Automatic Speech Recognition (ASR) to provide semantic accuracy feedback, while leveraging structured reward modeling to evaluate prosodic-emotional consistency. RLAIF-SPA enables more precise and nuanced control over expressive speech generation along four structured evaluation dimensions: Structure, Emotion, Speed, and Tone. Extensive experiments on Libri-Speech, MELD, and Mandarin ESD datasets demonstrate consistent gains across clean read speech, conversational dialogue, and emotional speech. On Libri-Speech, RLAIF-SPA consistently outperforms Chat-TTS, achieving a 26.1% reduction in word error rate, a 9.1% improvement in SIM-O, and over 10% gains in human subjective evaluations.
中文标题/摘要
标题：RLAIF-SPA：面向语音合成中语义-韵律对齐的结构化人工智能反馈
当前文本转语音（TTS）合成技术在中性说话风格上已实现接近人声的质量，但现有方法大多依赖昂贵的情感标注数据，或采用难以充分捕捉感知情感质量的替代优化目标，导致生成语音虽语义准确，却常缺乏表现力与情感丰富性。为此，我们提出RLAIF-SPA——一种融合人工智能反馈强化学习（RLAIF）的新型框架，可在无需人工监督的情况下直接优化情感表现力与可懂度。该框架通过自动语音识别（ASR）提供语义准确性反馈，并利用结构化奖励建模评估韵律-情感一致性，从而在结构、情感、语速、音调四个结构化评估维度上实现更精准细腻的表现性语音生成控制。在Libri-Speech、MELD和汉语ESD数据集上的大量实验表明，本方法在清晰朗读语音、对话式语音及情感语音中均取得稳定提升：在Libri-Speech上持续超越Chat-TTS，词错误率降低26.1%，SIM-O指标提升9.1%，人类主观评价增益超10%。
