ActivityEditor: Learning to Synthesize Physically Valid Human Mobility
Authors: Chenjie Yang, Yutian Jiang, Anqi Liang, Wei Qi, Chenyu Wu, Junbo Zhang
First: 2026-04-07T07:28:20+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-07T07:28:20+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Human mobility modeling is indispensable for diverse urban applications. However, existing data-driven methods often suffer from data scarcity, limiting their applicability in regions where historical trajectories are unavailable or restricted. To bridge this gap, we propose \textbf{ActivityEditor}, a novel dual-LLM-agent framework designed for zero-shot cross-regional trajectory generation. Our framework decomposes the complex synthesis task into two collaborative stages. Specifically, an intention-based agent, which leverages demographic-driven priors to generate structured human intentions and coarse activity chains to ensure high-level socio-semantic coherence. These outputs are then refined by editor agent to obtain mobility trajectories through iteratively revisions that enforces human mobility law. This capability is acquired through reinforcement learning with multiple rewards grounded in real-world physical constraints, allowing the agent to internalize mobility regularities and ensure high-fidelity trajectory generation. Extensive experiments demonstrate that \textbf{ActivityEditor} achieves superior zero-shot performance when transferred across diverse urban contexts. It maintains high statistical fidelity and physical validity, providing a robust and highly generalizable solution for mobility simulation in data-scarce scenarios. Our code is available at: https://anonymous.4open.science/r/ActivityEditor-066B.
中文标题/摘要
标题：ActivityEditor：学习合成物理有效的人类移动性
人类移动建模对于多样化城市应用至关重要。然而，现有数据驱动方法常受数据稀缺性困扰，限制了其在历史轨迹不可用或受限区域的适用性。为弥补这一差距，我们提出\textbf{ActivityEditor}，一种新颖的双LLM智能体框架，专为零样本跨区域轨迹生成设计。该框架将复杂合成任务分解为两个协作阶段：首先，基于意图的智能体利用人口统计驱动的先验生成结构化人类意图和粗略活动链，以确保高层次的社会语义连贯性；随后，编辑智能体通过迭代修订对这些输出进行精细化处理，强制执行人类移动规律以获取移动轨迹。此能力通过基于现实物理约束的多奖励强化学习获得，使智能体内化移动规律并确保高保真轨迹生成。大量实验表明，\textbf{ActivityEditor}在不同城市语境间迁移时实现了卓越的零样本性能，保持高统计保真度和物理有效性，为数据稀缺场景下的移动模拟提供了稳健且高度可泛化的解决方案。代码发布于：https://anonymous.4open.science/r/ActivityEditor-066B。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the challenge of data scarcity in human mobility modeling, which limits the applicability of data-driven methods in regions with unavailable or restricted historical trajectories, this paper introduces ActivityEditor, a novel dual-LLM-agent framework for zero-shot cross-regional trajectory generation. The method decomposes the synthesis task into two collaborative stages: an intention-based agent generates structured human intentions and coarse activity chains using demographic-driven priors for socio-semantic coherence, followed by an editor agent that refines these into mobility trajectories through iterative revisions enforced by reinforcement learning with rewards based on real-world physical constraints to internalize mobility regularities. MemFactory: Unified Inference & Training Framework for Agent Memory
Authors: Ziliang Guo, Ziheng Li, Bo Tang, Feiyu Xiong, Zhiyu Li
First: 2026-03-31T09:38:21+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-07T07:28:08+00:00
Comments: fixed Figure 1 typos, clarified ambiguous wording in the abstract, added 1 missing citation, Code: https://github.com/MemTensor/MemFactory
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Memory-augmented Large Language Models (LLMs) are essential for developing capable, long-term AI agents. Recently, applying Reinforcement Learning (RL) to optimize memory operations, such as extraction, updating, and retrieval, has emerged as a highly promising research direction. However, existing implementations remain highly fragmented and task-specific, lacking a unified infrastructure to streamline the integration, training, and evaluation of these complex pipelines. To address this gap, we present MemFactory, the first unified, highly modular training and inference framework specifically designed for memory-augmented agents. Inspired by the success of unified fine-tuning frameworks like LLaMA-Factory, MemFactory abstracts the memory lifecycle into atomic, plug-and-play components, enabling researchers to seamlessly construct custom memory agents via a "Lego-like" architecture. Furthermore, the framework natively integrates Group Relative Policy Optimization (GRPO) to fine-tune internal memory management policies driven by multi-dimensional environmental rewards. MemFactory provides out-of-the-box support for recent cutting-edge paradigms, including Memory-R1, RMM, and MemAgent. We empirically validate MemFactory on the open-source MemAgent architecture using its publicly available training and evaluation data. Across the evaluation sets, MemFactory improves performance over the corresponding base models on average, with relative gains of up to 14.8%. By providing a standardized, extensible, and easy-to-use infrastructure, MemFactory significantly lowers the barrier to entry, paving the way for future innovations in memory-driven AI agents.
中文标题/摘要
标题：MemFactory：面向智能体记忆的统一推理与训练框架

UniCreative: Unifying Long-form Logic and Short-form Sparkle via Reference-Free Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Xiaolong Wei, Zerun Zhu, Simin Niu, Xingyu Zhang, Peiying Yu, Changxuan Xiao, Yuchen Li, Jicheng Yang, Zhejun Zhao, Chong Meng, Long Xia, Daiting Shi
Venue: ACL 2026
First: 2026-04-07T07:15:28+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-07T07:15:28+00:00
Comments: Accepted to Findings of ACL 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
A fundamental challenge in creative writing lies in reconciling the inherent tension between maintaining global coherence in long-form narratives and preserving local expressiveness in short-form texts. While long-context generation necessitates explicit macroscopic planning, short-form creativity often demands spontaneous, constraint-free expression. Existing alignment paradigms, however, typically employ static reward signals and rely heavily on high-quality supervised data, which is costly and difficult to scale. To address this, we propose \textbf{UniCreative}, a unified reference-free reinforcement learning framework. We first introduce \textbf{AC-GenRM}, an adaptive constraint-aware reward model that dynamically synthesizes query-specific criteria to provide fine-grained preference judgments. Leveraging these signals, we propose \textbf{ACPO}, a policy optimization algorithm that aligns models with human preferences across both content quality and structural paradigms without supervised fine-tuning and ground-truth references. Empirical results demonstrate that AC-GenRM aligns closely with expert evaluations, while ACPO significantly enhances performance across diverse writing tasks. Crucially, our analysis reveals an emergent meta-cognitive ability: the model learns to autonomously differentiate between tasks requiring rigorous planning and those favoring direct generation, validating the effectiveness of our direct alignment approach.
中文标题/摘要
标题：UniCreative：通过无参考强化学习统一长篇逻辑与短篇灵光
创意写作的一个根本挑战在于调和长篇叙事所需的全局连贯性与短篇文本的局部表现力之间的内在张力。长文本生成需要明确的宏观规划，而短篇创作则常需自发、无约束的表达。然而，现有对齐范式通常采用静态奖励信号，并严重依赖高质量监督数据，成本高昂且难以扩展。为此，我们提出\textbf{UniCreative}，一个统一的无参考强化学习框架。我们首先引入\textbf{AC-GenRM}，一种自适应约束感知奖励模型，能动态合成针对特定查询的标准，以提供细粒度偏好判断。利用这些信号，我们提出\textbf{ACPO}，一种策略优化算法，可在无需监督微调和真实参考的情况下，使模型在内容质量与结构范式上对齐人类偏好。实证结果表明，AC-GenRM与专家评估高度一致，而ACPO在多种写作任务中显著提升性能。关键的是，我们的分析揭示了一种新兴的元认知能力：模型学会自主区分需要严格规划的任务与适合直接生成的任务，验证了我们直接对齐方法的有效性。

The paper addresses the challenge of balancing long-form narrative coherence with short-form expressive creativity in writing, which typically requires different approaches: explicit planning for long contexts and spontaneous generation for short texts. The proposed UniCreative framework introduces an adaptive constraint-aware reward model (AC-GenRM) that dynamically generates query-specific criteria for fine-grained preference judgments, and a policy optimization algorithm (ACPO) that aligns models with human preferences without relying on supervised fine-tuning or ground-truth references. Experimental results show that AC-GenRM closely matches expert evaluations, and ACPO improves performance across various writing tasks, with the model developing a meta-cognitive ability to autonomously decide between planning-based and direct generation strategies.

OmniDiagram: Advancing Unified Diagram Code Generation via Visual Interrogation Reward
Authors: Haoyue Yang, Xuanle Zhao, Xuexin Liu, Feibang Jiang, Yao Zhu
Venue: ACL 2026
First: 2026-04-07T07:10:24+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-07T07:10:24+00:00
Comments: Accepted to ACL 2026 Findings
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
The paradigm of programmable diagram generation is evolving rapidly, playing a crucial role in structured visualization. However, most existing studies are confined to a narrow range of task formulations and language support, constraining their applicability to diverse diagram types. In this work, we propose OmniDiagram, a unified framework that incorporates diverse diagram code languages and task definitions. To address the challenge of aligning code logic with visual fidelity in Reinforcement Learning (RL), we introduce a novel visual feedback strategy named Visual Interrogation Verifies All (\textsc{Viva}). Unlike brittle syntax-based rules or pixel-level matching, \textsc{Viva} rewards the visual structure of rendered diagrams through a generative approach. Specifically, \textsc{Viva} actively generates targeted visual inquiries to scrutinize diagram visual fidelity and provides fine-grained feedback for optimization. This mechanism facilitates a self-evolving training process, effectively obviating the need for manually annotated ground truth code. Furthermore, we construct M3$^2$Diagram, the first large-scale diagram code generation dataset, containing over 196k high-quality instances. Experimental results confirm that the combination of SFT and our \textsc{Viva}-based RL allows OmniDiagram to establish a new state-of-the-art (SOTA) across diagram code generation benchmarks.

标题：OmniDiagram：通过视觉质询奖励推进统一图表代码生成
可编程图表生成范式正在快速发展，在结构化可视化中发挥着关键作用。然而，现有研究大多局限于有限的任务形式与语言支持，难以适应多样化的图表类型。本研究提出OmniDiagram——一个融合多种图表代码语言与任务定义的统一框架。针对强化学习中代码逻辑与视觉保真度对齐的挑战，我们引入了名为“视觉质询验证一切”（Viva）的新型视觉反馈策略。与脆弱的基于语法规则或像素级匹配方法不同，Viva通过生成式方法对渲染图表的视觉结构进行奖励。具体而言，Viva主动生成针对性视觉质询以检验图表视觉保真度，并提供细粒度反馈用于优化。该机制实现了自我演进的训练过程，有效避免了人工标注真实代码的需求。此外，我们构建了首个大规模图表代码生成数据集M3²Diagram，包含超过19.6万条高质量实例。实验结果表明，监督微调与基于Viva的强化学习相结合，使OmniDiagram在图表代码生成基准测试中实现了新的最优性能。

Motivated by the limitations of existing programmable diagram generation methods, which are often restricted to narrow task formulations and language support, this paper introduces OmniDiagram, a unified framework that integrates diverse diagram code languages and task definitions. The method employs a novel visual feedback strategy called Visual Interrogation Verifies All (Viva), which uses generative visual inquiries to scrutinize and reward the visual fidelity of rendered diagrams, facilitating a self-evolving training process without manual ground truth code. Experimental results on the newly constructed large-scale M3^2Diagram dataset demonstrate that combining supervised fine-tuning with Viva-based reinforcement learning enables OmniDiagram to achieve state-of-the-art performance across diagram code generation benchmarks.

Can We Trust a Black-box LLM? LLM Untrustworthy Boundary Detection via Bias-Diffusion and Multi-Agent Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Xiaotian Zhou, Di Tang, Xiaofeng Wang, Xiaozhong Liu
First: 2026-04-07T06:24:01+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-07T06:24:01+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Large Language Models (LLMs) have shown a high capability in answering questions on a diverse range of topics. However, these models sometimes produce biased, ideologized or incorrect responses, limiting their applications if there is no clear understanding of which topics their answers can be trusted. In this research, we introduce a novel algorithm, named as GMRL-BD, designed to identify the untrustworthy boundaries (in terms of topics) of a given LLM, with black-box access to the LLM and under specific query constraints. Based on a general Knowledge Graph (KG) derived from Wikipedia, our algorithm incorporates with multiple reinforcement learning agents to efficiently identify topics (some nodes in KG) where the LLM is likely to generate biased answers. Our experiments demonstrated the efficiency of our algorithm, which can detect the untrustworthy boundary with just limited queries to the LLM. Additionally, we have released a new dataset containing popular LLMs including Llama2, Vicuna, Falcon, Qwen2, Gemma2 and Yi-1.5, along with labels indicating the topics on which each LLM is likely to be biased.
中文标题/摘要
标题：我们能否信任黑盒大语言模型？基于偏置扩散与多智能体强化学习的大语言模型不可信边界检测
大语言模型在广泛主题的问答任务中展现出卓越能力，但有时会产生带有偏见、意识形态化或错误的回答。若无法明确判断其回答在哪些主题上可信，将限制模型的实际应用。本研究提出名为GMRL-BD的创新算法，该算法在仅能黑盒访问大语言模型且受特定查询约束的条件下，旨在识别给定模型在主题层面的不可信边界。基于维基百科构建的通用知识图谱，本算法融合多智能体强化学习机制，高效定位知识图谱中可能引发模型偏见回答的主题节点。实验证明该算法仅需对模型进行有限次查询即可有效检测不可信边界。此外，我们发布了包含Llama2、Vicuna、Falcon、Qwen2、Gemma2和Yi-1.5等主流大语言模型的新数据集，并标注了各模型易产生偏见回答的主题标签。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the need to understand when large language models (LLMs) produce biased or incorrect responses, this paper introduces GMRL-BD, a method that detects an LLM's untrustworthy topic boundaries using only black-box access. The approach leverages a Wikipedia-derived knowledge graph and employs multi-agent reinforcement learning to efficiently identify topics where the model is prone to bias, minimizing queries to the LLM. Experimental results demonstrate the algorithm's effectiveness in mapping untrustworthy boundaries with limited queries, and the authors release a new dataset labeling biased topics for several popular LLMs including Llama2 and Qwen2.
本研究针对大型语言模型（LLM）可能产生偏见或错误回答的问题，提出了一种名为GMRL-BD的新算法，旨在仅通过黑盒访问检测LLM在哪些主题上不可信。该方法基于维基百科构建的知识图谱，结合多智能体强化学习来高效识别模型容易产生偏见的主题节点，同时最小化对LLM的查询次数。实验结果表明，该算法能以有限查询有效探测出不可信边界，并发布了一个包含Llama2、Qwen2等多个流行LLM的新数据集，其中标注了各模型可能存有偏见的主题。
Reproducing AlphaZero on Tablut: Self-Play RL for an Asymmetric Board Game
Authors: Tõnis Lees, Tambet Matiisen
First: 2026-04-07T06:16:19+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-07T06:16:19+00:00
Comments: For the code see https://github.com/tonislees/TablutZero
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
This work investigates the adaptation of the AlphaZero reinforcement learning algorithm to Tablut, an asymmetric historical board game featuring unequal piece counts and distinct player objectives (king capture versus king escape). While the original AlphaZero architecture successfully leverages a single policy and value head for symmetric games, applying it to asymmetric environments forces the network to learn two conflicting evaluation functions, which can hinder learning efficiency and performance. To address this, the core architecture is modified to use separate policy and value heads for each player role, while maintaining a shared residual trunk to learn common board features. During training, the asymmetric structure introduced training instabilities, notably catastrophic forgetting between the attacker and defender roles. These issues were mitigated by applying C4 data augmentation, increasing the replay buffer size, and having the model play 25 percent of training games against randomly sampled past checkpoints. Over 100 self-play iterations, the modified model demonstrated steady improvement, achieving a BayesElo rating of 1235 relative to a randomly initialized baseline. Training metrics also showed a significant decrease in policy entropy and average remaining pieces, reflecting increasingly focused and decisive play. Ultimately, the experiments confirm that AlphaZero's self-play framework can transfer to highly asymmetric games, provided that distinct policy/value heads and robust stabilization techniques are employed.

标题：在塔布勒棋上复现AlphaZero：非对称棋盘游戏的自博弈强化学习
本研究探讨将AlphaZero强化学习算法适配至塔布勒棋——一种具有非对称性的历史棋盘游戏，其特点为双方棋子数量不等且玩家目标不同（擒王方需捕获国王，护王方需助国王逃脱）。原始AlphaZero架构虽能通过单一策略头与价值头处理对称游戏，但在非对称环境中需同时学习两套相互冲突的评估函数，这会降低学习效率与性能。为此，本研究改进核心架构，为不同玩家角色设置独立的策略头与价值头，同时保留共享残差主干网络以学习通用棋盘特征。训练过程中，非对称结构引发了训练不稳定性，特别是攻守角色间的灾难性遗忘问题。通过采用C4数据增强、扩大回放缓冲区容量，以及安排模型在25%的训练对局中与随机抽取的历史检查点对抗，这些问题得到缓解。经过100轮自博弈迭代，改进模型展现出稳定进步，相对于随机初始化基线获得1235的贝叶斯Elo评分。训练指标同时显示策略熵与平均剩余棋子数显著下降，反映出对局策略日趋专注且决策更具决定性。实验最终证实：只要采用独立的策略/价值头架构并配合鲁棒的稳定化技术，AlphaZero的自博弈框架可成功迁移至高度非对称的游戏环境。

Training faced instabilities like catastrophic forgetting, which were mitigated using C4 data augmentation, a larger replay buffer, and playing 25% of games against past checkpoints. Over 100 self-play iterations, the model showed steady improvement, achieving a BayesElo rating of 1235 against a random baseline, with metrics indicating more focused and decisive play as policy entropy and average remaining pieces decreased.

A Hessian-Free Actor-Critic Algorithm for Bi-Level Reinforcement Learning with Applications to LLM Fine-Tuning
Authors: Sihan Zeng, Sujay Bhatt, Sumitra Ganesh, Alec Koppel
First: 2026-01-23T02:12:24+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-07T04:32:45+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
We study a structured bi-level optimization problem where the upper-level objective is a smooth function and the lower-level problem is policy optimization in a Markov decision process (MDP). The upper-level decision variable parameterizes the reward of the lower-level MDP, and the upper-level objective depends on the optimal induced policy. Existing methods for bi-level optimization and RL often require second-order information, impose strong regularization at the lower level, or inefficiently use samples through nested-loop procedures. In this work, we propose a single-loop, first-order actor-critic algorithm that optimizes the bi-level objective via a penalty-based reformulation. We introduce into the lower-level RL objective an attenuating entropy regularization, which enables asymptotically unbiased upper-level hyper-gradient estimation without solving the unregularized RL problem exactly. We establish the finite-time and finite-sample convergence of the proposed algorithm to a stationary point of the original, unregularized bi-level optimization problem through a novel lower-level residual analysis under a special type of Polyak-Lojasiewicz condition. We validate the performance of our method through experiments on a GridWorld goal position problem and on happy tweet generation through reinforcement learning from human feedback (RLHF).
中文标题/摘要
标题：一种用于双层强化学习的无Hessian行动者-评论家算法及其在大语言模型微调中的应用
本文研究一个结构化双层优化问题，其中上层目标为光滑函数，下层问题为马尔可夫决策过程中的策略优化。上层决策变量参数化下层MDP的奖励函数，上层目标取决于诱导的最优策略。现有双层优化与强化学习方法常需二阶信息、对下层施加强正则化，或通过嵌套循环流程低效使用样本。本研究提出一种单循环一阶行动者-评论家算法，通过基于惩罚的重构优化双层目标。我们在下层RL目标中引入衰减熵正则化，使得无需精确求解无正则化RL问题即可实现渐近无偏的上层超梯度估计。通过特殊类型Polyak-Lojasiewicz条件下的新型下层残差分析，我们证明了所提算法在有限时间和有限样本内收敛至原始无正则化双层优化问题的稳定点。通过GridWorld目标定位实验和基于人类反馈强化学习的积极推文生成实验，验证了方法的有效性。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the computational challenges in bi-level reinforcement learning, where an upper-level objective depends on the optimal policy of a lower-level MDP parameterized by a reward function. The motivation is to overcome the need for second-order derivatives, strong regularization, or inefficient nested loops in existing methods. The proposed method is a single-loop, first-order actor-critic algorithm that uses a penalty-based reformulation with an attenuating entropy regularization in the lower-level RL objective, enabling asymptotically unbiased hyper-gradient estimation. Experimental results demonstrate convergence to a stationary point of the unregularized bi-level problem, validated on a GridWorld task and a reinforcement learning from human feedback application for happy tweet generation.
本文针对双层强化学习中的计算挑战展开研究，其中上层目标函数依赖于由奖励函数参数化的下层马尔可夫决策过程的最优策略。其动机是克服现有方法对二阶导数、强正则化或低效嵌套循环的需求。所提出的方法是一种单循环、一阶的演员-评论家算法，采用基于惩罚的重构方法，并在下层RL目标中引入衰减的熵正则化，从而实现渐近无偏的超梯度估计。实验结果表明，该方法能收敛到无正则化双层问题的稳定点，并在GridWorld目标定位任务和基于人类反馈的快乐推文生成强化学习应用中得到了验证。
Multi-Agent Pathfinding with Non-Unit Integer Edge Costs via Enhanced Conflict-Based Search and Graph Discretization
Authors: Hongkai Fan, Qinjing Xie, Bo Ouyang, Yaonan Wang, Zhi Yan, Jiawen He, Zheng Fang
First: 2026-04-07T04:24:50+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-07T04:24:50+00:00
Comments: 16 pages, 7 figures, submitted to cs.AI, Multi-Agent Systems, Pathfinding Optimization
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Multi-Agent Pathfinding (MAPF) plays a critical role in various domains. Traditional MAPF methods typically assume unit edge costs and single-timestep actions, which limit their applicability to real-world scenarios. MAPFR extends MAPF to handle non-unit costs with real-valued edge costs and continuous-time actions, but its geometric collision model leads to an unbounded state space that compromises solver efficiency. In this paper, we propose MAPFZ, a novel MAPF variant on graphs with non-unit integer costs that preserves a finite state space while offering improved realism over classical MAPF. To solve MAPFZ efficiently, we develop CBS-NIC, an enhanced Conflict-Based Search framework incorporating time-interval-based conflict detection and an improved Safe Interval Path Planning (SIPP) algorithm. Additionally, we propose Bayesian Optimization for Graph Design (BOGD), a discretization method for non-unit edge costs that balances efficiency and accuracy with a sub-linear regret bound. Extensive experiments demonstrate that our approach outperforms state-of-the-art methods in runtime and success rate across diverse benchmark scenarios.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于增强型冲突搜索与图离散化的非单位整数边成本多智能体路径规划
多智能体路径规划（MAPF）在多个领域具有关键作用。传统MAPF方法通常假设单位边成本和单时间步动作，这限制了其在现实场景中的应用。MAPFR将MAPF扩展至处理非单位成本，支持实值边成本和连续时间动作，但其几何碰撞模型导致状态空间无限，影响求解效率。本文提出MAPFZ，一种在非单位整数成本图上的新型MAPF变体，既保持有限状态空间，又比经典MAPF更具现实性。为高效求解MAPFZ，我们开发了CBS-NIC，一种增强型冲突搜索框架，融合基于时间间隔的冲突检测和改进的安全间隔路径规划（SIPP）算法。此外，我们提出图设计贝叶斯优化（BOGD），一种针对非单位边成本的离散化方法，以次线性遗憾界平衡效率与精度。大量实验表明，本方法在多种基准场景下的运行时间和成功率均优于现有先进方法。

This paper addresses the limitations of traditional Multi-Agent Pathfinding (MAPF), which assumes unit edge costs and single-timestep actions, by introducing MAPFZ, a novel variant that handles non-unit integer edge costs while maintaining a finite state space for improved realism and computational tractability. The method develops CBS-NIC, an enhanced Conflict-Based Search framework with time-interval conflict detection and an improved Safe Interval Path Planning algorithm, alongside Bayesian Optimization for Graph Design (BOGD) to discretize non-unit costs with a sub-linear regret bound. Experimental results show that the proposed approach outperforms state-of-the-art methods in runtime and success rate across various benchmark scenarios.
本文针对传统多智能体路径规划（MAPF）假设单位边成本和单时间步动作的局限性，提出了MAPFZ这一新变体，它处理非单位整数边成本，同时保持有限状态空间，以提高现实性和计算可行性。方法上开发了CBS-NIC，一个增强的基于冲突的搜索框架，包含基于时间间隔的冲突检测和改进的安全间隔路径规划算法，以及贝叶斯优化图设计（BOGD）来离散化非单位成本，并具有次线性遗憾界。实验结果表明，该方法在多种基准场景下的运行时间和成功率均优于现有先进方法。
Neural Assistive Impulses: Synthesizing Exaggerated Motions for Physics-based Characters
Authors: Zhiquan Wang, Bedrich Benes
First: 2026-04-07T03:47:14+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-07T03:47:14+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Physics-based character animation has become a fundamental approach for synthesizing realistic, physically plausible motions. While current data-driven deep reinforcement learning (DRL) methods can synthesize complex skills, they struggle to reproduce exaggerated, stylized motions, such as instantaneous dashes or mid-air trajectory changes, which are required in animation but violate standard physical laws. The primary limitation stems from modeling the character as an underactuated floating-base system, in which internal joint torques and momentum conservation strictly govern motion. Direct attempts to enforce such motions via external wrenches often lead to training instability, as velocity discontinuities produce sparse, high-magnitude force spikes that prevent policy convergence. We propose Assistive Impulse Neural Control, a framework that reformulates external assistance in impulse space rather than force space to ensure numerical stability. We decompose the assistive signal into an analytic high-frequency component derived from Inverse Dynamics and a learned low-frequency residual correction, governed by a hybrid neural policy. We demonstrate that our method enables robust tracking of highly agile, dynamically infeasible maneuvers that were previously intractable for physics-based methods.
中文标题/摘要
标题：神经辅助冲量：为物理角色合成夸张运动
基于物理的角色动画已成为合成真实、物理合理运动的基础方法。当前数据驱动的深度强化学习方法虽能合成复杂技能，却难以复现动画所需但违背标准物理定律的夸张风格化运动，如瞬时冲刺或空中轨迹变化。主要限制源于将角色建模为欠驱动浮动基系统，其内部关节扭矩与动量守恒严格约束运动。直接通过外部力矩强制此类运动常导致训练不稳定，因速度不连续性会产生稀疏、高幅值力峰值，阻碍策略收敛。我们提出辅助冲量神经控制框架，将外部辅助重构于冲量空间而非力空间以确保数值稳定性。辅助信号被分解为源自逆动力学的解析高频分量与由混合神经策略调控的学习型低频残差校正。实验表明，本方法能稳健跟踪高度敏捷、动态不可行的机动动作，此类动作以往对基于物理的方法难以实现。
Summary / 总结
The motivation for this work is to enable physics-based character animation to synthesize exaggerated, stylized motions, such as instantaneous dashes, which are common in animation but violate standard physical laws and are difficult for current data-driven deep reinforcement learning methods that model characters as underactuated systems. The proposed method, Assistive Impulse Neural Control, reformulates external assistance in impulse space instead of force space to ensure numerical stability, decomposing the assistive signal into an analytic high-frequency component from Inverse Dynamics and a learned low-frequency residual correction via a hybrid neural policy. The main experimental results demonstrate that this framework enables robust tracking of highly agile, dynamically infeasible maneuvers that were previously intractable for physics-based animation methods.
本研究的动机是使基于物理的角色动画能够合成夸张的风格化运动，例如瞬时冲刺，这些运动在动画中常见但违反标准物理定律，且对于当前将角色建模为欠驱动系统的数据驱动深度强化学习方法而言难以实现。所提出的方法——辅助脉冲神经控制——将外部辅助重新表述在脉冲空间而非力空间以确保数值稳定性，将辅助信号分解为来自逆动力学的解析高频分量和通过混合神经策略学习的低频残差校正。主要实验结果表明，该框架能够稳健地跟踪高度敏捷、动态不可行的机动动作，这些动作以往对于基于物理的动画方法是难以处理的。
Breakthrough the Suboptimal Stable Point in Value-Factorization-Based Multi-Agent Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Lesong Tao, Yifei Wang, Haodong Jing, Jingwen Fu, Miao Kang, Shitao Chen, Nanning Zheng
First: 2026-04-07T01:05:13+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-07T01:05:13+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Value factorization, a popular paradigm in MARL, faces significant theoretical and algorithmic bottlenecks: its tendency to converge to suboptimal solutions remains poorly understood and unsolved. Theoretically, existing analyses fail to explain this due to their primary focus on the optimal case. To bridge this gap, we introduce a novel theoretical concept: the stable point, which characterizes the potential convergence of value factorization in general cases. Through an analysis of stable point distributions in existing methods, we reveal that non-optimal stable points are the primary cause of poor performance. However, algorithmically, making the optimal action the unique stable point is nearly infeasible. In contrast, iteratively filtering suboptimal actions by rendering them unstable emerges as a more practical approach for global optimality. Inspired by this, we propose a novel Multi-Round Value Factorization (MRVF) framework. Specifically, by measuring a non-negative payoff increment relative to the previously selected action, MRVF transforms inferior actions into unstable points, thereby driving each iteration toward a stable point with a superior action. Experiments on challenging benchmarks, including predator-prey tasks and StarCraft II Multi-Agent Challenge (SMAC), validate our analysis of stable points and demonstrate the superiority of MRVF over state-of-the-art methods.
中文标题/摘要
标题：突破基于价值分解的多智能体强化学习中的次优稳定点
价值分解作为多智能体强化学习的主流范式，面临显著的理论与算法瓶颈：其收敛至次优解的倾向尚未得到充分理解与解决。理论上，现有分析因主要关注最优情形而未能解释此现象。为填补这一空白，我们引入了一个新颖的理论概念——稳定点，用以刻画价值分解在一般情况下的潜在收敛性。通过对现有方法中稳定点分布的分析，我们发现非最优稳定点是性能不佳的主要原因。然而在算法层面，使最优动作成为唯一稳定点几乎不可行。相比之下，通过使次优动作失稳而进行迭代筛选，成为实现全局最优的更可行路径。受此启发，我们提出了多轮价值分解框架。具体而言，通过衡量相对于先前选定动作的非负收益增量，该框架将劣质动作转化为不稳定点，从而驱动每轮迭代向具有更优动作的稳定点收敛。在捕食者-猎物任务及星际争霸II多智能体挑战等复杂基准测试中的实验，验证了我们对稳定点的理论分析，并证明了该框架相较于前沿方法的优越性。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the problem of value-factorization-based multi-agent reinforcement learning (MARL) converging to suboptimal solutions, a bottleneck that lacks theoretical understanding. The authors introduce the concept of a stable point to characterize general convergence and analyze its distribution, identifying non-optimal stable points as the key performance limiter. To overcome this, they propose the Multi-Round Value Factorization (MRVF) framework, which iteratively filters suboptimal actions by making them unstable, thereby guiding convergence toward globally superior actions. Experimental results on predator-prey tasks and the StarCraft II Multi-Agent Challenge confirm the analysis and show MRVF outperforming state-of-the-art methods.
本文针对基于价值分解的多智能体强化学习（MARL）易收敛至次优解的问题，这一瓶颈缺乏理论理解。作者引入了稳定点的概念来描述一般收敛情况，并通过分析其分布，指出非最优稳定点是性能受限的主要原因。为解决此问题，他们提出了多轮价值分解（MRVF）框架，通过使次优动作变得不稳定来迭代过滤它们，从而引导收敛朝向全局更优动作。在捕食者-猎物任务和星际争霸II多智能体挑战上的实验结果验证了稳定点分析，并表明MRVF优于现有先进方法。
Why Code, Why Now: An Information-Theoretic Perspective on the Limits of Machine Learning
Authors: Zhimin Zhao
First: 2026-02-15T00:14:31+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-07T00:34:41+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
This paper offers a new perspective on the limits of machine learning: the ceiling on progress is set not by model size or algorithm choice but by the information structure of the task itself. Code generation has progressed more reliably than reinforcement learning, largely because code provides dense, local, verifiable feedback at every token, whereas most reinforcement learning problems do not. This difference in feedback quality is not binary but graded. We propose a five-level hierarchy of learnability based on information structure and argue that diagnosing a task's position in this hierarchy is more predictive of scaling outcomes than any property of the model. The hierarchy rests on a formal distinction among three properties of computational problems (expressibility, computability, and learnability). We establish their pairwise relationships, including where implications hold and where they fail, and present a unified template that makes the structural differences explicit. The analysis suggests why supervised learning on code scales predictably while reinforcement learning does not, and why the common assumption that scaling alone will solve remaining ML challenges warrants scrutiny.
中文标题/摘要
标题：为何是代码，为何是现在：从信息论视角看机器学习的局限
本文提出审视机器学习局限的新视角：进步的上限并非由模型规模或算法选择决定，而是由任务本身的信息结构所设定。代码生成比强化学习进展更稳定，主要因为代码在每个标记处提供密集、局部且可验证的反馈，而多数强化学习问题则不然。这种反馈质量的差异并非二元对立，而是存在梯度。我们基于信息结构提出五级可学习性层次体系，并论证通过诊断任务在该体系中的位置，比依赖模型任何特性更能预测规模化效果。该体系建立在计算问题三大特性（可表达性、可计算性、可学习性）的形式化区分之上，阐明其两两关系（包括蕴含成立与失效的情形），并提出使结构差异显式化的统一模板。分析揭示了代码监督学习可预测扩展而强化学习不能的原因，并对‘仅靠扩展就能解决机器学习剩余挑战’的普遍假设提出审慎反思。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the observation that code generation scales more reliably than reinforcement learning, this paper argues that the fundamental limit of machine learning is determined by the information structure of the task rather than model scale or algorithms. The method introduces a five-level hierarchy of learnability based on formal distinctions among expressibility, computability, and learnability, providing a unified template to diagnose a task's structural properties. The main experimental results, derived from theoretical analysis, demonstrate that tasks like supervised code learning offer dense, verifiable feedback enabling predictable scaling, whereas many reinforcement learning problems lack such structure, explaining their inconsistent progress and challenging the assumption that scaling alone will overcome remaining ML hurdles.
本文观察到代码生成比强化学习更具可扩展性，由此提出机器学习的基本极限取决于任务的信息结构而非模型规模或算法。方法上，基于可表达性、可计算性和可学习性之间的形式区分，建立了一个五级可学习性层次结构，并提供了一个统一模板来诊断任务的结构特性。主要实验结果通过理论分析表明，像监督式代码学习这类任务能提供密集、可验证的反馈，从而实现可预测的扩展，而许多强化学习问题缺乏此类结构，这解释了其进展不一致的原因，并对仅靠扩展就能解决剩余机器学习挑战的常见假设提出了质疑。
Vehicle-as-Prompt: A Unified Deep Reinforcement Learning Framework for Heterogeneous Fleet Vehicle Routing Problem
Authors: Shihong Huang, Shengjie Wang, Lei Gao, Hong Ma, Zhanluo Zhang, Feng Zhang, Weihua Zhou
First: 2026-04-06T21:48:52+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-06T21:48:52+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Unlike traditional homogeneous routing problems, the Heterogeneous Fleet Vehicle Routing Problem (HFVRP) involves heterogeneous fixed costs, variable travel costs, and capacity constraints, rendering solution quality highly sensitive to vehicle selection. Furthermore, real-world logistics applications often impose additional complex constraints, markedly increasing computational complexity. However, most existing Deep Reinforcement Learning (DRL)-based methods are restricted to homogeneous scenarios, leading to suboptimal performance when applied to HFVRP and its complex variants. To bridge this gap, we investigate HFVRP under complex constraints and develop a unified DRL framework capable of solving the problem across various variant settings. We introduce the Vehicle-as-Prompt (VaP) mechanism, which formulates the problem as a single-stage autoregressive decision process. Building on this, we propose VaP-CSMV, a framework featuring a cross-semantic encoder and a multi-view decoder that effectively addresses various problem variants and captures the complex mapping relationships between vehicle heterogeneity and customer node attributes. Extensive experimental results demonstrate that VaP-CSMV significantly outperforms existing state-of-the-art DRL-based neural solvers and achieves competitive solution quality compared to traditional heuristic solvers, while reducing inference time to mere seconds. Furthermore, the framework exhibits strong zero-shot generalization capabilities on large-scale and previously unseen problem variants, while ablation studies validate the vital contribution of each component.
中文标题/摘要
标题：车辆即提示：面向异构车队车辆路径问题的统一深度强化学习框架
与传统同构路径规划问题不同，异构车队车辆路径问题（HFVRP）涉及异构的固定成本、可变行驶成本和容量约束，使得解的质量对车辆选择高度敏感。此外，现实物流应用常附加复杂约束，显著增加计算复杂度。然而，现有基于深度强化学习（DRL）的方法多局限于同构场景，应用于HFVRP及其复杂变体时性能欠佳。为填补这一空白，本研究在复杂约束下探索HFVRP，开发出能适应多种变体设置的统一DRL框架。我们提出“车辆即提示”（VaP）机制，将问题构建为单阶段自回归决策过程。在此基础上，提出VaP-CSMV框架，该框架采用跨语义编码器和多视图解码器，有效处理各类问题变体，并捕捉车辆异构性与客户节点属性间的复杂映射关系。大量实验结果表明，VaP-CSMV显著优于现有基于DRL的先进神经求解器，相比传统启发式求解器获得具有竞争力的解质量，同时将推理时间缩短至数秒。此外，该框架在大规模及未见问题变体上展现出强大的零样本泛化能力，消融实验验证了各核心组件的重要贡献。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the limitations of existing Deep Reinforcement Learning (DRL) methods, which are largely confined to homogeneous vehicle routing and perform poorly on the Heterogeneous Fleet Vehicle Routing Problem (HFVRP) with its complex real-world constraints, this paper proposes a unified DRL framework. The method introduces a Vehicle-as-Prompt (VaP) mechanism to formulate HFVRP as a single-stage autoregressive process and develops the VaP-CSMV framework with a cross-semantic encoder and multi-view decoder to model relationships between heterogeneous vehicles and customer nodes. Experimental results show that VaP-CSMV significantly outperforms other DRL-based neural solvers, achieves competitive quality with traditional heuristic methods in seconds, and demonstrates strong zero-shot generalization to unseen, large-scale problem variants, with ablations confirming each component's importance.

Cross-fitted Proximal Learning for Model-Based Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Nishanth Venkatesh, Andreas A. Malikopoulos
First: 2026-04-06T21:29:57+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-06T21:29:57+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Model-based reinforcement learning is attractive for sequential decision-making because it explicitly estimates reward and transition models and then supports planning through simulated rollouts. In offline settings with hidden confounding, however, models learned directly from observational data may be biased. This challenge is especially pronounced in partially observable systems, where latent factors may jointly affect actions, rewards, and future observations. Recent work has shown that policy evaluation in such confounded partially observable Markov decision processes (POMDPs) can be reduced to estimating reward-emission and observation-transition bridge functions satisfying conditional moment restrictions (CMRs). In this paper, we study the statistical estimation of these bridge functions. We formulate bridge learning as a CMR problem with nuisance objects given by a conditional mean embedding and a conditional density. We then develop a $K$-fold cross-fitted extension of the existing two-stage bridge estimator. The proposed procedure preserves the original bridge-based identification strategy while using the available data more efficiently than a single sample split. We also derive an oracle-comparator bound for the cross-fitted estimator and decompose the resulting error into a Stage I term induced by nuisance estimation and a Stage II term induced by empirical averaging.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于模型的强化学习中的交叉拟合近端学习
基于模型的强化学习因其能显式估计奖励和转移模型，并通过模拟推演支持规划，在序列决策中备受青睐。然而，在存在隐藏混杂因素的离线设置中，直接从观测数据学习的模型可能存在偏差。这一挑战在部分可观测系统中尤为突出，其中潜在因素可能共同影响行动、奖励和未来观测。近期研究表明，在此类混杂部分可观测马尔可夫决策过程中，策略评估可简化为估计满足条件矩限制的奖励-发射和观测-转移桥函数。本文研究这些桥函数的统计估计方法。我们将桥学习构建为条件矩限制问题，其干扰对象由条件均值嵌入和条件密度给出。随后，我们开发了现有两阶段桥估计器的K折交叉拟合扩展。该方案保留了基于桥函数的原始识别策略，同时比单一样本分割更高效地利用数据。我们还推导了交叉拟合估计器的预言机比较界，并将误差分解为由干扰估计引起的第一阶段项和由经验平均引起的第二阶段项。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the challenge of biased model estimation in offline model-based reinforcement learning due to hidden confounding in partially observable systems, where latent factors can distort the relationships between actions, rewards, and observations. To overcome this, the authors formulate bridge function estimation as a conditional moment restriction problem involving nuisance objects like conditional mean embeddings and densities, and propose a K-fold cross-fitted extension of an existing two-stage bridge estimator to improve data efficiency over single sample splits. Experimental results, supported by theoretical analysis, show that the cross-fitted estimator achieves an oracle-comparator error bound, decomposing error into Stage I nuisance estimation and Stage II empirical averaging components, thereby enhancing statistical reliability in confounded partially observable Markov decision processes.
本文针对离线模型强化学习中因部分可观测系统存在隐藏混杂而导致的模型估计偏差问题，其中潜在因素会扭曲动作、奖励和观测之间的关系。为解决此问题，作者将桥函数估计构建为涉及条件均值嵌入和密度等冗余对象的条件矩限制问题，并提出了一种K折交叉拟合的扩展方法，改进现有两阶段桥估计器，相比单一样本分割提高了数据利用效率。实验结果表明，交叉拟合估计器实现了与理论最优比较的误差界限，将误差分解为第一阶段冗余估计和第二阶段经验平均两部分，从而增强了在混杂部分可观测马尔可夫决策过程中的统计可靠性。
Training LLMs for Multi-Step Tool Orchestration with Constrained Data Synthesis and Graduated Rewards
Authors: Cheng Jiayang, Xin Liu, Zhihan Zhang, Haoyang Wen, Zixuan Zhang, Qingyu Yin, Shiyang Li, Priyanka Nigam, Bing Yin, Chao Zhang, Yangqiu Song
First: 2026-03-25T18:31:39+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-06T20:50:24+00:00
Comments: Under Review
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Multi-step tool orchestration remains challenging for LLMs, as state-of-the-art models frequently fail on full sequence execution due to parameter errors. Training for these workflows faces two obstacles: the lack of environments supporting complex real-world API dependencies, and sparse binary rewards that provide no signal for partial correctness. We propose a reinforcement learning framework addressing both challenges. First, we construct a deterministic environment backed by a large-scale cache of real API responses, enabling constrained synthesis of valid multi-step traces with controllable complexity. Second, we introduce a graduated reward that decomposes correctness into atomic validity (call-level correctness at increasing granularity) and orchestration consistency (correct sequencing with dependency respect). On ComplexFuncBench, our approach substantially improves turn accuracy, with ablations confirming both reward components are essential. Cross-benchmark evaluation on BFCL v4 shows that the learned orchestration skills transfer to entirely different API ecosystems (e.g., agentic web search and memory management), yielding consistent gains while maintaining stable single-step performance. Code is available at https://github.com/horizon-rl/ToolOrchestrationReward
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于约束数据合成与渐进奖励的大语言模型多步骤工具编排训练
多步骤工具编排对大语言模型仍具挑战性，当前最先进模型常因参数错误导致完整序列执行失败。此类工作流训练面临两大障碍：缺乏支持复杂现实API依赖的环境，以及稀疏二元奖励无法为部分正确性提供信号。我们提出一个强化学习框架以应对这两项挑战。首先，我们构建由大规模真实API响应缓存支持的确定性环境，实现可控复杂度的有效多步骤轨迹约束合成。其次，我们引入渐进式奖励机制，将正确性分解为原子有效性（逐层细化的调用级正确性）与编排一致性（遵循依赖关系的正确序列）。在ComplexFuncBench上的实验表明，该方法显著提升轮次准确率，消融实验证实两个奖励组件均不可或缺。在BFCL v4的跨基准评估显示，习得的编排技能可迁移至完全不同的API生态系统（如智能网络搜索与内存管理），在保持稳定单步性能的同时获得持续增益。代码发布于https://github.com/horizon-rl/ToolOrchestrationReward

Experimental results on ComplexFuncBench show substantial improvements in turn accuracy, with ablations confirming the importance of both reward components, and cross-benchmark evaluation on BFCL v4 demonstrates that the learned skills transfer to different API ecosystems, yielding consistent gains while maintaining stable single-step performance.

Learning to Focus: CSI-Free Hierarchical MARL for Reconfigurable Reflectors
Authors: Hieu Le, Mostafa Ibrahim, Oguz Bedir, Jian Tao, Sabit Ekin
First: 2026-04-06T20:50:03+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-06T20:50:03+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Reconfigurable Intelligent Surfaces (RIS) has a potential to engineer smart radio environments for next-generation millimeter-wave (mmWave) networks. However, the prohibitive computational overhead of Channel State Information (CSI) estimation and the dimensionality explosion inherent in centralized optimization severely hinder practical large-scale deployments. To overcome these bottlenecks, we introduce a ``CSI-free" paradigm powered by a Hierarchical Multi-Agent Reinforcement Learning (HMARL) architecture to control mechanically reconfigurable reflective surfaces. By substituting pilot-based channel estimation with accessible user localization data, our framework leverages spatial intelligence for macro-scale wave propagation management. The control problem is decomposed into a two-tier neural architecture: a high-level controller executes temporally extended, discrete user-to-reflector allocations, while low-level controllers autonomously optimize continuous focal points utilizing Multi-Agent Proximal Policy Optimization (MAPPO) under a Centralized Training with Decentralized Execution (CTDE) scheme. Comprehensive deterministic ray-tracing evaluations demonstrate that this hierarchical framework achieves massive RSSI improvements of up to 7.79 dB over centralized baselines. Furthermore, the system exhibits robust multi-user scalability and maintains highly resilient beam-focusing performance under practical sub-meter localization tracking errors. By eliminating CSI overhead while maintaining high-fidelity signal redirection, this work establishes a scalable and cost-effective blueprint for intelligent wireless environments.

可重构智能表面（RIS）具备为下一代毫米波网络构建智能无线电环境的潜力。然而，信道状态信息（CSI）估计的过高计算开销以及集中式优化固有的维度爆炸问题，严重阻碍了实际大规模部署。为突破这些瓶颈，本文提出一种由层次化多智能体强化学习（HMARL）架构驱动的“无CSI”范式，用于控制机械可重构反射面。该框架通过以可获取的用户定位数据替代基于导频的信道估计，利用空间智能实现宏观尺度波传播管理。控制问题被分解为双层神经架构：高层控制器执行时间扩展的离散用户-反射面分配，而低层控制器在集中训练分散执行（CTDE）方案下，利用多智能体近端策略优化（MAPPO）自主优化连续焦点。基于确定性射线追踪的综合评估表明，该层次化框架相比集中式基线实现了高达7.79 dB的大规模接收信号强度指数提升。此外，系统展现出稳健的多用户扩展性，并在实际亚米级定位跟踪误差下保持高度韧性的波束聚焦性能。通过消除CSI开销同时维持高保真信号重定向，本研究为智能无线环境提供了可扩展且经济高效的蓝图。

Bypassing the CSI Bottleneck: MARL-Driven Spatial Control for Reflector Arrays
Authors: Hieu Le, Oguz Bedir, Mostafa Ibrahim, Jian Tao, Sabit Ekin
First: 2026-04-06T20:47:50+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-06T20:47:50+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Reconfigurable Intelligent Surfaces (RIS) are pivotal for next-generation smart radio environments, yet their practical deployment is severely bottlenecked by the intractable computational overhead of Channel State Information (CSI) estimation. To bypass this fundamental physical-layer barrier, we propose an AI-native, data-driven paradigm that replaces complex channel modeling with spatial intelligence. This paper presents a fully autonomous Multi-Agent Reinforcement Learning (MARL) framework to control mechanically adjustable metallic reflector arrays. By mapping high-dimensional mechanical constraints to a reduced-order virtual focal point space, we deploy a Centralized Training with Decentralized Execution (CTDE) architecture. Using Multi-Agent Proximal Policy Optimization (MAPPO), our decentralized agents learn cooperative beam-focusing strategies relying on user coordinates, achieving CSI-free operation. High-fidelity ray-tracing simulations in dynamic non-line-of-sight (NLOS) environments demonstrate that this multi-agent approach rapidly adapts to user mobility, yielding up to a 26.86 dB enhancement over static flat reflectors and outperforming single-agent and hardware-constrained DRL baselines in both spatial selectivity and temporal stability. Crucially, the learned policies exhibit good deployment resilience, sustaining stable signal coverage even under 1.0-meter localization noise. These results validate the efficacy of MARL-driven spatial abstractions as a scalable, highly practical pathway toward AI-empowered wireless networks.

Non-monotonic causal discovery with Kolmogorov-Arnold Fuzzy Cognitive Maps
Authors: Jose L. Salmeron
Venue: IEEE Transactions on Fuzzy Systems 2026
First: 2026-04-06T19:56:12+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-06T19:56:12+00:00
Comments: Fuzzy Cognitive Maps, Kolmogorov-Arnold Networks, Causal Modeling, Neuro-Symbolic AI
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Fuzzy Cognitive Maps constitute a neuro-symbolic paradigm for modeling complex dynamic systems, widely adopted for their inherent interpretability and recurrent inference capabilities. However, the standard FCM formulation, characterized by scalar synaptic weights and monotonic activation functions, is fundamentally constrained in modeling non-monotonic causal dependencies, thereby limiting its efficacy in systems governed by saturation effects or periodic dynamics. To overcome this topological restriction, this research proposes the Kolmogorov-Arnold Fuzzy Cognitive Map (KA-FCM), a novel architecture that redefines the causal transmission mechanism. Drawing upon the Kolmogorov-Arnold representation theorem, static scalar weights are replaced with learnable, univariate B-spline functions located on the model edges. This fundamental modification shifts the non-linearity from the nodes' aggregation phase directly to the causal influence phase. This modification allows for the modeling of arbitrary, non-monotonic causal relationships without increasing the graph density or introducing hidden layers. The proposed architecture is validated against both baselines (standard FCM trained with Particle Swarm Optimization) and universal black-box approximators (Multi-Layer Perceptron) across three distinct domains: non-monotonic inference (Yerkes-Dodson law), symbolic regression, and chaotic time-series forecasting. Experimental results demonstrate that KA-FCMs significantly outperform conventional architectures and achieve competitive accuracy relative to MLPs, while preserving graph- based interpretability and enabling the explicit extraction of mathematical laws from the learned edges.

标题：基于Kolmogorov-Arnold模糊认知图的非单调因果发现
模糊认知图作为一种神经符号范式，因其固有的可解释性和循环推理能力，被广泛用于复杂动态系统建模。然而，标准FCM采用标量突触权重和单调激活函数，本质上难以建模非单调因果依赖，限制了其在饱和效应或周期性动态系统中的应用。为突破这一拓扑限制，本研究提出Kolmogorov-Arnold模糊认知图——一种重新定义因果传递机制的新型架构。基于Kolmogorov-Arnold表示定理，该模型将静态标量权重替换为位于模型边缘的可学习单变量B样条函数。这一根本性修改将非线性从节点聚合阶段直接转移至因果影响阶段，使得无需增加图密度或引入隐藏层即可建模任意非单调因果关系。通过在三个不同领域（非单调推理的耶基斯-多德森定律、符号回归、混沌时间序列预测）与基线方法（粒子群优化训练的标准FCM）及通用黑盒近似器（多层感知机）进行对比验证，实验结果表明：KA-FCM在保持图结构可解释性的同时，显著优于传统架构，且相对MLP达到具有竞争力的精度，并能从学习到的边中显式提取数学规律。

Reasoning Through Chess: How Reasoning Evolves from Data Through Fine-Tuning and Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Lucas Dionisopoulos, Nicklas Majamaki, Prithviraj Ammanabrolu
Venue: NeurIPS 2025 Oral
First: 2026-04-06T19:53:39+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-06T19:53:39+00:00
Comments: Accepted at the NeurIPS 2025 Foundations of Reasoning in Language Models (FoRLM) Workshop (Oral)
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
How can you get a language model to reason in a task it natively struggles with? We study how reasoning evolves in a language model -- from supervised fine-tuning (SFT) to reinforcement learning (RL) -- by analyzing how a set of theoretically-inspired datasets impacts language model performance in chess. We find that fine-tuning a model to directly predict the best move leads to effective RL and the strongest downstream performance -- however, the RL step elicits unfaithful reasoning (reasoning inconsistent with the chosen move). Alternatively, training on multi-move trajectories yields comparable downstream performance with faithful reasoning and more stable RL. We show that RL induces a substantial positive shift in the distribution of move quality and reduces hallucination rates as a side effect. Finally, we find several SFT-checkpoint metrics -- metrics spanning evaluation performance, hallucination rates, and reasoning quality -- to be predictive of post-RL model performance. We release checkpoints and final models as well as training data, evaluations, and code which allowed us to surpass leading open-source reasoning models in chess with a 7B-parameter model.

标题：通过国际象棋进行推理：从数据到微调与强化学习的推理能力演化

Toward Virtuous Reinforcement Learning: A Critique and Roadmap
Authors: Majid Ghasemi, Mark Crowley
Venue: AAAI 2026
First: 2025-12-03T20:30:37+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-06T19:43:12+00:00
Comments: Accepted as a workshop paper at Machine Ethics: From Formal Methods to Emergent Machine Ethics workshop at the AAAI 2026 Conference
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
This paper critiques common patterns in machine ethics for Reinforcement Learning (RL) and argues for a virtue focused alternative. We highlight two recurring limitations in much of the current literature: (i) rule based (deontological) methods that encode duties as constraints or shields often struggle under ambiguity and nonstationarity and do not cultivate lasting habits, and (ii) many reward based approaches, especially single objective RL, implicitly compress diverse moral considerations into a single scalar signal, which can obscure trade offs and invite proxy gaming in practice. We instead treat ethics as policy level dispositions, that is, relatively stable habits that hold up when incentives, partners, or contexts change. This shifts evaluation beyond rule checks or scalar returns toward trait summaries, durability under interventions, and explicit reporting of moral trade offs. Our roadmap combines four components: (1) social learning in multi agent RL to acquire virtue like patterns from imperfect but normatively informed exemplars; (2) multi objective and constrained formulations that preserve value conflicts and incorporate risk aware criteria to guard against harm; (3) affinity based regularization toward updateable virtue priors that support trait like stability under distribution shift while allowing norms to evolve; and (4) operationalizing diverse ethical traditions as practical control signals, making explicit the value and cultural assumptions that shape ethical RL benchmarks.
中文标题/摘要
标题：迈向德性强化学习：批判与路线图
本文批判了强化学习（RL）机器伦理领域的常见范式，并提出以德性伦理为核心的替代路径。我们指出当前文献中两个普遍局限：（1）基于规则（义务论）的方法将道德义务编码为约束或防护机制，常在模糊性与非稳态环境中失效，且难以培养持久的行为习惯；（2）多数基于奖励的方法（尤其是单目标RL）将多元道德考量隐式压缩为单一标量信号，可能模糊价值权衡并引发实践中的代理博弈问题。我们主张将伦理视为策略层面的倾向性——即在激励、合作方或情境变化时仍能保持的相对稳定习惯。这使评估标准从规则检查或标量回报转向特质归纳、干预下的稳健性以及道德权衡的显式报告。我们的路线图整合四个要素：（1）通过多智能体RL的社会学习，从具有规范指导意义的不完美范例中习得类德性模式；（2）采用多目标与约束优化框架以保留价值冲突，并引入风险感知准则防范伤害；（3）基于亲和力的可更新德性先验正则化，在分布偏移中保持类特质稳定性的同时允许规范演进；（4）将多元伦理传统具象化为可操作的控制信号，显式揭示塑造伦理RL基准的价值与文化预设。
Summary / 总结
This paper critiques prevailing machine ethics approaches in Reinforcement Learning (RL), arguing that rule-based and single-objective reward methods often fail under ambiguity or obscure moral trade-offs. It proposes a virtue-focused alternative, treating ethics as stable policy-level habits evaluated through trait summaries and durability. The roadmap integrates social learning from exemplars, multi-objective formulations, affinity-based regularization, and operationalized ethical traditions to foster adaptable, transparent, and robust ethical dispositions in RL agents.
本文批判了强化学习中主流的机器伦理方法，指出基于规则和单一目标奖励的方法常在模糊性下失效或掩盖道德权衡。它提出一种以美德为中心的替代方案，将伦理视为稳定的策略层面习惯，通过特质总结和耐久性进行评估。路线图整合了从范例中社会学习、多目标表述、基于亲和力的正则化以及可操作的伦理传统，以培养强化学习智能体适应性强、透明且稳健的伦理倾向。
Vintix II: Decision Pre-Trained Transformer is a Scalable In-Context Reinforcement Learner
Authors: Andrei Polubarov, Lyubaykin Nikita, Alexander Derevyagin, Artyom Grishin, Igor Saprygin, Aleksandr Serkov, Mark Averchenko, Daniil Tikhonov, Maksim Zhdanov, Alexander Nikulin, Ilya Zisman, Albina Klepach, Alexey Zemtsov, Vladislav Kurenkov
Venue: ICLR 2026 Poster
First: 2026-04-06T19:18:12+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-06T19:18:12+00:00
Comments: ICLR 2026, Poster
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Recent progress in in-context reinforcement learning (ICRL) has demonstrated its potential for training generalist agents that can acquire new tasks directly at inference. Algorithm Distillation (AD) pioneered this paradigm and was subsequently scaled to multi-domain settings, although its ability to generalize to unseen tasks remained limited. The Decision Pre-Trained Transformer (DPT) was introduced as an alternative, showing stronger in-context reinforcement learning abilities in simplified domains, but its scalability had not been established. In this work, we extend DPT to diverse multi-domain environments, applying Flow Matching as a natural training choice that preserves its interpretation as Bayesian posterior sampling. As a result, we obtain an agent trained across hundreds of diverse tasks that achieves clear gains in generalization to the held-out test set. This agent improves upon prior AD scaling and demonstrates stronger performance in both online and offline inference, reinforcing ICRL as a viable alternative to expert distillation for training generalist agents.

标题：Vintix II：决策预训练Transformer是一种可扩展的上下文强化学习器
上下文强化学习（ICRL）的最新进展展示了其训练通用智能体的潜力，这些智能体能够在推理时直接学习新任务。算法蒸馏（AD）开创了这一范式，并随后扩展到多领域环境，但其对未见任务的泛化能力仍有限。决策预训练Transformer（DPT）作为替代方案被提出，在简化领域中展现出更强的上下文强化学习能力，但其可扩展性尚未得到验证。本研究将DPT扩展到多样化的多领域环境，采用流匹配作为自然训练方法，保持其作为贝叶斯后验采样的解释。由此获得的智能体在数百个多样化任务上训练，在保留测试集上实现了显著的泛化提升。该智能体改进了先前的AD扩展方法，在在线和离线推理中均表现出更强性能，进一步确立了ICRL作为专家蒸馏替代方案训练通用智能体的可行性。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the need for scalable generalist agents that can learn new tasks in-context without fine-tuning, this work extends the Decision Pre-Trained Transformer (DPT) to multi-domain settings using Flow Matching as a training method, which maintains its Bayesian interpretation. The resulting agent, trained on hundreds of diverse tasks, demonstrates improved generalization to unseen tasks compared to prior approaches like Algorithm Distillation, showing stronger performance in both online and offline inference scenarios.

DeepSearch: Overcome the Bottleneck of Reinforcement Learning with Verifiable Rewards via Monte Carlo Tree Search
Authors: Fang Wu, Weihao Xuan, Heli Qi, Ximing Lu, Aaron Tu, Li Erran Li, Yejin Choi
First: 2025-09-29T20:00:29+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-06T19:16:24+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Although RLVR has become an essential component for developing advanced reasoning skills in language models, contemporary studies have documented training plateaus after thousands of optimization steps, i.e., notable decreases in performance gains despite increased computational investment. This limitation stems from the sparse exploration patterns inherent in current RLVR practices, where models rely on limited rollouts that often miss critical reasoning paths and fail to provide systematic coverage of the solution space. We present DeepSearch, a framework that integrates Monte Carlo Tree Search (MCTS) directly into RLVR training. In contrast to existing methods that rely on tree search only at inference, DeepSearch embeds structured search into the training loop, enabling systematic exploration and fine-grained credit assignment across reasoning steps. Through training-time exploration, DeepSearch addresses the fundamental bottleneck of insufficient exploration, which leads to diminishing performance gains over prolonged training. Our contributions include: (1) a global frontier selection strategy that prioritizes promising nodes across the search tree, (2) selection with entropy-based guidance that identifies confident paths for supervision, and (3) adaptive replay buffer training with solution caching for efficiency. Experiments on mathematical reasoning benchmarks show that DeepSearch achieves an average accuracy of 62.95\% and establishes a new state-of-the-art reasoning model, while using 5.7x fewer GPU hours than extended training approaches. These results highlight the importance of strategic exploration over brute-force scaling and demonstrate the promise of algorithmic innovation for advancing RLVR methodologies. DeepSearch establishes a new direction for scaling reasoning capabilities through systematic search rather than prolonged computation.

标题：DeepSearch：通过蒙特卡洛树搜索突破可验证奖励强化学习的瓶颈
尽管可验证奖励强化学习已成为提升语言模型高级推理能力的关键技术，但现有研究表明，经过数千步优化后常出现训练平台期——即计算资源持续增加而性能增益显著下降。这一局限源于当前可验证奖励强化学习方法固有的稀疏探索模式：模型依赖有限次数的路径采样，往往遗漏关键推理路径，且无法系统覆盖解空间。本文提出DeepSearch框架，将蒙特卡洛树搜索直接整合至可验证奖励强化学习训练中。与仅在推理阶段使用树搜索的现有方法不同，DeepSearch将结构化搜索嵌入训练循环，实现系统化探索和推理步骤间的细粒度信用分配。通过训练阶段的探索机制，DeepSearch从根本上解决了探索不足导致的性能增益递减瓶颈。主要贡献包括：（1）全局前沿节点选择策略，优先探索搜索树中潜力节点；（2）基于熵的引导选择机制，识别高置信路径用于监督；（3）结合解缓存的自适应回放缓冲区训练方案以提升效率。在数学推理基准测试中，DeepSearch平均准确率达62.95%，建立了新的最先进推理模型，同时比延长训练方法减少5.7倍GPU时耗。这些结果凸显了策略性探索相对于暴力扩展的重要性，并证明了算法创新对推进可验证奖励强化学习方法的潜力。DeepSearch通过系统化搜索而非延长计算时间，为扩展推理能力开辟了新方向。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the training plateaus and sparse exploration in Reinforcement Learning with Verifiable Rewards (RLVR), which limit performance gains despite increased computation, this paper introduces DeepSearch, a framework that integrates Monte Carlo Tree Search (MCTS) directly into the RLVR training loop to enable systematic exploration and fine-grained credit assignment across reasoning steps. The method employs a global frontier selection strategy, entropy-based guidance for path selection, and adaptive replay buffer training with solution caching. Experimental results on mathematical reasoning benchmarks show that DeepSearch achieves a state-of-the-art average accuracy of 62.95% while using 5.7 times fewer GPU hours than extended training approaches, demonstrating the efficacy of strategic exploration over brute-force scaling.

Multiplayer Nash Preference Optimization
Authors: Fang Wu, Xu Huang, Weihao Xuan, Zhiwei Zhang, Yijia Xiao, Guancheng Wan, Xiaomin Li, Bing Hu, Peng Xia, Jure Leskovec, Yejin Choi
First: 2025-09-27T04:18:33+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-06T19:14:12+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Reinforcement learning from human feedback (RLHF) has emerged as the standard paradigm for aligning large language models with human preferences. However, reward-based methods grounded in the Bradley-Terry assumption struggle to capture the nontransitivity and heterogeneity of real-world preferences. To address this, recent studies have reframed alignment as a two-player Nash game, giving rise to Nash learning from human feedback (NLHF). While this perspective has inspired algorithms such as INPO, ONPO, and EGPO that offer strong theoretical and empirical guarantees, they remain fundamentally restricted to two-player interactions, introducing a single-opponent bias that fails to capture the full complexity of realistic preference structures. This work introduces Multiplayer Nash Preference Optimization (MNPO), a novel framework that generalizes NLHF to the multiplayer regime. It formulates alignment as an n-player game, where each policy competes against a population of opponents while being regularized toward a reference model. We demonstrate that MNPO inherits the equilibrium guarantees of two-player methods while enabling richer competitive dynamics and improved coverage of diverse preference structures. Comprehensive empirical evaluation shows that MNPO consistently outperforms existing NLHF baselines on instruction-following benchmarks, achieving superior alignment quality under heterogeneous annotator conditions and mixed-policy evaluation scenarios. Together, these results establish MNPO as a principled and scalable framework for aligning LLMs with complex, non-transitive human preferences. Code is available at: https://github.com/smiles724/MNPO

标题：多人纳什偏好优化
基于人类反馈的强化学习已成为将大语言模型与人类偏好对齐的标准范式。然而，基于布拉德利-特里假设的奖励方法难以捕捉现实偏好的非传递性和异质性。为此，近期研究将对齐问题重构为双人纳什博弈，催生了基于人类反馈的纳什学习。尽管该视角已衍生出INPO、ONPO、EGPO等具备坚实理论与实证保证的算法，但其本质上仍局限于双人交互，存在单一对手偏差，无法捕捉现实偏好结构的完整复杂性。本研究提出多人纳什偏好优化框架，将NLHF推广至多人博弈体系。该框架将对齐问题建模为n人博弈，每个策略在与对手群体竞争的同时，通过参考模型进行正则化。我们证明MNPO在继承双人方法均衡保证的同时，能实现更丰富的竞争动态，并提升对多样化偏好结构的覆盖能力。综合实验评估表明，在指令遵循基准测试中，MNPO持续优于现有NLHF基线方法，在异质标注者条件与混合策略评估场景下均实现更优的对齐质量。这些成果共同确立了MNPO作为应对复杂非传递性人类偏好的原则性可扩展对齐框架。代码已开源：https://github.com/smiles724/MNPO

Stratifying Reinforcement Learning with Signal Temporal Logic
Authors: Justin Curry, Alberto Speranzon
First: 2026-04-06T17:58:58+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-06T17:58:58+00:00
Comments: 8 pages, 13 figures
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
In this paper, we develop a stratification-based semantics for Signal Temporal Logic (STL) in which each atomic predicate is interpreted as a membership test in a stratified space. This perspective reveals a novel correspondence principle between stratification theory and STL, showing that most STL formulas can be viewed as inducing a stratification of space-time. The significance of this interpretation is twofold. First, it offers a fresh theoretical framework for analyzing the structure of the embedding space generated by deep reinforcement learning (DRL) and relates it to the geometry of the ambient decision space. Second, it provides a principled framework that both enables the reuse of existing high-dimensional analysis tools and motivates the creation of novel computational techniques. To ground the theory, we (1) illustrate the role of stratification theory in Minigrid games and (2) apply numerical techniques to the latent embeddings of a DRL agent playing such a game where the robustness of STL formulas is used as the reward. In the process, we propose computationally efficient signatures that, based on preliminary evidence, appear promising for uncovering the stratification structure of such embedding spaces.

本文为信号时序逻辑（STL）建立了一种基于分层理论的语义框架，其中每个原子谓词被解释为分层空间中的隶属度检验。这一视角揭示了分层理论与STL之间新颖的对应原理，表明大多数STL公式可视为诱导了时空的分层结构。该解释具有双重意义：首先，为分析深度强化学习（DRL）生成的嵌入空间结构提供了全新理论框架，并将其与环境决策空间的几何特性相关联；其次，构建了一个原则性框架，既能复用现有高维分析工具，又激励新型计算技术的开发。为验证理论，我们（1）在Minigrid游戏中演示分层理论的作用，（2）将数值技术应用于DRL智能体在同类游戏中的潜在嵌入表示，其中STL公式的鲁棒性被用作奖励函数。在此过程中，我们提出了计算高效的签名方法，初步证据表明该方法在揭示此类嵌入空间的分层结构方面具有潜力。

Analyzing Symbolic Properties for DRL Agents in Systems and Networking
Authors: Mohammad Zangooei, Jannis Weil, Amr Rizk, Mina Tahmasbi Arashloo, Raouf Boutaba
First: 2026-04-06T17:55:15+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-06T17:55:15+00:00
Comments: Accepted in ACM SIGMETRICS'26
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Deep reinforcement learning (DRL) has shown remarkable performance on complex control problems in systems and networking, including adaptive video streaming, wireless resource management, and congestion control. For safe deployment, however, it is critical to reason about how agents behave across the range of system states they encounter in practice. Existing verification-based methods in this domain primarily focus on point properties, defined around fixed input states, which offer limited coverage and require substantial manual effort to identify relevant input-output pairs for analysis. In this paper, we study symbolic properties, that specify expected behavior over ranges of input states, for DRL agents in systems and networking. We present a generic formulation for symbolic properties, with monotonicity and robustness as concrete examples, and show how they can be analyzed using existing DNN verification engines. Our approach encodes symbolic properties as comparisons between related executions of the same policy and decomposes them into practically tractable sub-properties. These techniques serve as practical enablers for applying existing verification tools to symbolic analysis. Using our framework, diffRL, we conduct an extensive empirical study across three DRL-based control systems, adaptive video streaming, wireless resource management, and congestion control. Through these case studies, we analyze symbolic properties over broad input ranges, examine how property satisfaction evolves during training, study the impact of model size on verifiability, and compare multiple verification backends. Our results show that symbolic properties provide substantially broader coverage than point properties and can uncover non-obvious, operationally meaningful counterexamples, while also revealing practical solver trade-offs and limitations.
中文标题/摘要
标题：系统与网络领域深度强化学习智能体的符号属性分析
深度强化学习（DRL）在系统与网络领域的复杂控制问题中展现出卓越性能，包括自适应视频流、无线资源管理和拥塞控制。然而，为确保安全部署，必须对智能体在实际可能遇到的系统状态范围内的行为进行推理。该领域现有的基于验证的方法主要关注围绕固定输入状态定义的点属性，其覆盖范围有限且需要大量人工工作来识别相关输入-输出对。本文针对系统与网络中的DRL智能体，研究在输入状态范围内指定预期行为的符号属性。我们提出符号属性的通用形式化框架，以单调性和鲁棒性作为具体示例，并展示如何利用现有深度神经网络验证引擎进行分析。该方法将符号属性编码为同一策略相关执行间的比较，并将其分解为实际可处理的子属性。这些技术为应用现有验证工具进行符号分析提供了实用支撑。基于我们开发的diffRL框架，我们在三个基于DRL的控制系统（自适应视频流、无线资源管理、拥塞控制）上开展了广泛实证研究。通过案例研究，我们分析了宽泛输入范围内的符号属性，检验了训练过程中属性满足度的演化规律，研究了模型规模对可验证性的影响，并比较了多种验证后端。结果表明：符号属性比点属性提供更广泛的覆盖范围，能发现非显然且具有操作意义的反例，同时揭示了实际求解器的权衡与局限。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the need for safe deployment of deep reinforcement learning (DRL) agents in systems and networking applications like adaptive video streaming and congestion control, this paper addresses the limitations of existing verification methods that focus only on point properties. The method introduces a generic formulation for symbolic properties, such as monotonicity and robustness, and presents diffRL, a framework that encodes these properties as comparisons between related policy executions and decomposes them into tractable sub-properties for analysis using existing DNN verification engines. Experimental results across three DRL-based control systems demonstrate that symbolic properties offer broader coverage than point properties, uncover operationally meaningful counterexamples, and reveal practical trade-offs in solver performance, while also showing how property satisfaction evolves during training and is affected by model size.

Not All Tokens Matter: Towards Efficient LLM Reasoning via Token Significance in Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Hanbing Liu, Lang Cao, Yuanyi Ren, Mengyu Zhou, Haoyu Dong, Xiaojun Ma, Shi Han, Dongmei Zhang
First: 2025-06-09T18:27:26+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-06T17:47:33+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Large language models (LLMs) show strong reasoning abilities but often produce unnecessarily long explanations that reduce efficiency. Although reinforcement learning (RL) has been used to improve reasoning, most methods focus on accuracy and rely on uniform length-based rewards that overlook the differing contributions of individual tokens, often harming correctness. We revisit length optimization in RL through the perspective of token significance. Observing that many chain-of-thought (CoT) tokens contribute little to the final answer, we introduce a significance-aware length reward that selectively penalizes insignificance tokens, reducing redundancy while preserving essential reasoning. We also propose a dynamic length reward that encourages more detailed reasoning early in training and gradually shifts toward conciseness as learning progresses. Integrating these components into standard policy optimization yields a framework that improves both reasoning efficiency and accuracy. Experiments across multiple benchmarks demonstrate substantial reductions in response length while preserving or improving correctness, highlighting the importance of modeling token significance for efficient LLM reasoning.
中文标题/摘要
标题：并非所有令牌都重要：基于强化学习中令牌重要性实现高效大语言模型推理
大语言模型展现出强大的推理能力，但常生成冗余冗长的解释而降低效率。尽管强化学习已被用于改进推理，现有方法多聚焦准确性，并依赖基于长度的均匀奖励机制，忽视了单个令牌的差异化贡献，甚至可能损害正确性。本研究从令牌重要性视角重新审视强化学习的长度优化：观察到思维链中许多令牌对最终答案贡献甚微，我们提出一种重要性感知的长度奖励机制，选择性惩罚无关紧要的令牌以降低冗余，同时保留核心推理逻辑；另提出动态长度奖励机制，在训练初期鼓励详细推理，随学习进程逐步转向简洁表达。将上述组件整合至标准策略优化框架后，实验表明该方案能在保持或提升准确性的同时显著缩短响应长度，验证了建模令牌重要性对提升大语言模型推理效率的关键价值。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the inefficiency of large language models (LLMs) in reasoning tasks, where they often generate overly long chain-of-thought explanations without improving accuracy. The authors propose a reinforcement learning approach that optimizes reasoning by focusing on token significance, introducing a significance-aware length reward to penalize redundant tokens and a dynamic length reward that initially encourages detail before shifting toward conciseness. Experimental results across multiple benchmarks show that this method substantially reduces response length while maintaining or even enhancing correctness, demonstrating the value of modeling token contributions for efficient LLM reasoning.
本文针对大语言模型在推理任务中效率低下的问题，即其常生成冗长的思维链解释却未提升准确性。研究者提出一种基于强化学习的方法，通过关注令牌重要性来优化推理，引入了显著性感知的长度奖励以惩罚冗余令牌，以及动态长度奖励在训练初期鼓励详细推理后逐步转向简洁。在多个基准测试上的实验结果表明，该方法能显著缩短响应长度，同时保持甚至提高正确性，凸显了建模令牌重要性对于实现高效大语言模型推理的重要性。
QED-Nano: Teaching a Tiny Model to Prove Hard Theorems
Authors: LM-Provers, Yuxiao Qu, Amrith Setlur, Jasper Dekoninck, Edward Beeching, Jia Li, Ian Wu, Lewis Tunstall, Aviral Kumar
First: 2026-04-06T17:44:25+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-06T17:44:25+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Proprietary AI systems have recently demonstrated impressive capabilities on complex proof-based problems, with gold-level performance reported at the 2025 International Mathematical Olympiad (IMO). However, the training pipelines behind these systems remain largely undisclosed, and their reliance on large "internal" models and scaffolds makes them expensive to run, difficult to reproduce, and hard to study or improve upon. This raises a central question: can small, open models also be trained to achieve competitive reasoning performance on difficult Olympiad-level math? In this paper, we answer this question by building QED-Nano, a 4B model post-trained for Olympiad-level proofs. Our training recipe has three stages: (1) supervised fine-tuning to imbue good proof-writing styles by distilling from DeepSeek-Math-V2, (2) reinforcement learning (RL) with rubric-based rewards, and (3) expanding RL with a reasoning cache, which decomposes long proofs into iterative summarize-and-refine cycles and enables stronger test-time reasoning. QED-Nano surpasses the proof-generation performance of much larger open models, including Nomos-1 and GPT-OSS-120B, and approaches the performance of proprietary models like Gemini 3 Pro, at a fraction of the inference cost. To support further research on open mathematical reasoning, we release the full QED-Nano pipeline, including the QED-Nano and QED-Nano-SFT models, the FineProofs-SFT and FineProofs-RL datasets, and the training and evaluation code.
中文标题/摘要
标题：QED-Nano：训练微型模型证明高难度定理
近期，专有AI系统在复杂证明类问题上展现出卓越能力，据报告在2025年国际数学奥林匹克竞赛（IMO）中达到金牌级表现。然而，这些系统的训练流程大多未公开，且依赖庞大的“内部”模型与架构，导致运行成本高昂、难以复现、不易研究与改进。这引出一个核心问题：小型开源模型能否通过训练，在奥数级难题上实现具备竞争力的推理性能？本文通过构建QED-Nano——一个针对奥数级证明进行后训练的40亿参数模型——对此给出肯定答案。我们的训练方案包含三个阶段：（1）通过从DeepSeek-Math-V2蒸馏进行监督微调，以习得优质证明书写风格；（2）基于评分标准的强化学习；（3）引入推理缓存的扩展强化学习，将长证明分解为迭代的“总结-精炼”循环，从而增强测试时推理能力。QED-Nano在证明生成性能上超越了包括Nomos-1和GPT-OSS-120B在内的更大规模开源模型，并以极低的推理成本逼近Gemini 3 Pro等专有模型性能。为促进开放数学推理研究，我们完整公开QED-Nano流程，包括QED-Nano与QED-Nano-SFT模型、FineProofs-SFT与FineProofs-RL数据集，以及训练与评估代码。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the high cost and opacity of proprietary AI systems that excel at complex mathematical proofs, this work investigates whether small, open models can achieve competitive reasoning on Olympiad-level problems. The method introduces QED-Nano, a 4B parameter model trained via a three-stage pipeline: supervised fine-tuning to distill proof-writing style from a larger model, reinforcement learning with rubric-based rewards, and an enhanced RL stage using a reasoning cache that breaks long proofs into iterative summarize-and-refine cycles. Experimental results show that QED-Nano outperforms much larger open models like Nomos-1 and GPT-OSS-120B in proof generation, approaches the performance of proprietary models such as Gemini 3 Pro, and does so at significantly lower inference cost, with the full pipeline and datasets released to support open research.

Rethinking Exploration in RLVR: From Entropy Regularization to Refinement via Bidirectional Entropy Modulation
Authors: Hengrui Gu, Xiaotian Han, Yujing Bian, Kaixiong Zhou
First: 2026-04-06T17:42:38+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-06T17:42:38+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards (RLVR) has significantly advanced the reasoning capabilities of large language models (LLMs). However, it faces a fundamental limitation termed \textit{restricted exploration}, where the policy rapidly converges to a narrow set of solutions. While entropy regularization is a popular approach used to sustain exploration, it often proves unreliable for LLMs, suffering from high hyperparameter sensitivity and yielding only marginal performance gains. Motivated by these inefficiencies, we propose to rethink the relationship between policy entropy and exploration. By deriving a parametric formulation of group-relative advantage estimation and analyzing entropy dynamics, we conceptually decompose policy entropy into \textit{informative entropy}, which preserves diverse solution paths, and \textit{spurious entropy}, which erodes reasoning patterns. Our analysis reveals that, in contrast to blind maximization, effective exploration requires \textit{entropy refinement}-a mechanism implicitly embedded in group-relative advantage estimation that sustains informative entropy on positive rollouts while suppressing spurious entropy on negative ones. Guided by this insight, we propose \textbf{AsymGRPO}, an exploratory framework that explicitly decouples the modulation of positive and negative rollouts. This allows for independent control over the preservation of informative entropy and the suppression of spurious noise. Extensive experiments demonstrate that AsymGRPO achieves superior performance compared to strong baselines and exhibits the potential to synergize with existing entropy regularization methods.
中文标题/摘要
标题：重新审视RLVR中的探索机制：从熵正则化到双向熵调制的精细化调控
可验证奖励强化学习（RLVR）显著提升了大语言模型（LLM）的推理能力，但其面临被称为“受限探索”的根本性局限——策略迅速收敛至狭窄解集。熵正则化虽是维持探索的常用方法，但对LLM常表现出不可靠性：超参数敏感性高且仅带来边际性能提升。基于此低效性，我们重新审视策略熵与探索的关系。通过推导组间相对优势估计的参数化形式并分析熵动态，我们在概念上将策略熵分解为保持多元解路径的“信息熵”与侵蚀推理模式的“伪熵”。分析表明，与盲目最大化不同，有效探索需要“熵精细化”——一种隐含于组间相对优势估计的机制，能在正向轨迹中维持信息熵，同时在负向轨迹中抑制伪熵。基于此洞见，我们提出非对称组间相对策略优化（AsymGRPO）探索框架，显式解耦正负轨迹的调制机制，实现对信息熵保持与伪噪声抑制的独立控制。大量实验表明，AsymGRPO在强基线对比中取得更优性能，并展现出与现有熵正则化方法的协同潜力。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the problem of restricted exploration in reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards (RLVR) for large language models, where policies quickly converge to a narrow solution set. Motivated by the limitations of traditional entropy regularization, which is hyperparameter-sensitive and offers minimal gains, the authors propose a refined view of policy entropy by decomposing it into informative entropy (preserving diverse solution paths) and spurious entropy (eroding reasoning patterns). Their method, AsymGRPO, introduces an exploratory framework that explicitly decouples the modulation of positive and negative rollouts via bidirectional entropy modulation, enabling independent control to sustain informative entropy while suppressing spurious noise. Experimental results show that AsymGRPO outperforms strong baselines and can synergize with existing entropy regularization techniques.

A Model Can Help Itself: Reward-Free Self-Training for LLM Reasoning
Authors: Mengqi Li, Lei Zhao, Anthony Man-Cho So, Ruoyu Sun, Xiao Li
First: 2025-10-21T17:15:56+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-06T17:41:53+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Can language models improve their reasoning performance without external rewards, using only their own sampled responses for training? We show that they can. We propose Self-evolving Post-Training (SePT), a simple post-training method that alternates between self-generation and training on self-generated responses. It repeatedly samples questions, uses the model itself to generate low-temperature responses, and then finetunes the model on the self-generated data. In this self-training loop, we use an online data refresh mechanism, where each new batch is generated by the most recently updated model. Across six math reasoning benchmarks, SePT improves a strong no-training baseline, defined as the untuned base model evaluated at its best swept decoding temperature, on several tested models. In some settings, SePT can even approach the performance of Reinforcement Learning with Verifiable Rewards (RLVR). Additional ablations demonstrate the importance of online data refresh and temperature decoupling. Overall, our results identify a practical regime in which reasoning can be improved using self-generated supervision alone. Our code is available at https://github.com/ElementQi/SePT.
中文标题/摘要
标题：模型自助训练：面向大语言模型推理的无奖励自训练方法
语言模型能否在不依赖外部奖励的情况下，仅利用自身生成的响应进行训练以提升推理性能？我们的研究表明这是可行的。我们提出自进化后训练方法，这是一种简洁的后训练方法，通过自我生成与自生成响应训练的交替循环实现。该方法持续采样问题，利用模型自身生成低温响应，随后基于自生成数据对模型进行微调。在此自训练循环中，我们采用在线数据刷新机制——每个新批次数据均由最新更新的模型生成。在六项数学推理基准测试中，该方法显著超越了强无训练基线（定义为未经调优的基模型在其最优扫描解码温度下的表现）。在某些实验设定下，该方法甚至能逼近带可验证奖励的强化学习的性能。进一步的消融实验验证了在线数据刷新与温度解耦机制的重要性。总体而言，我们的研究结果揭示了一种仅通过自生成监督即可提升推理性能的实用路径。代码已开源：https://github.com/ElementQi/SePT。

This paper investigates whether language models can enhance their reasoning capabilities without external rewards by leveraging their own generated responses for training. Experimental results across six math reasoning benchmarks show that SePT consistently improves upon a strong no-training baseline and, in some cases, approaches the performance of reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards, with ablations confirming the importance of online data refresh and temperature decoupling.

Data Attribution in Adaptive Learning
Authors: Amit Kiran Rege
First: 2026-04-06T17:41:32+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-06T17:41:32+00:00
Comments: Work in progress
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Machine learning models increasingly generate their own training data -- online bandits, reinforcement learning, and post-training pipelines for language models are leading examples. In these adaptive settings, a single training observation both updates the learner and shifts the distribution of future data the learner will collect. Standard attribution methods, designed for static datasets, ignore this feedback. We formalize occurrence-level attribution for finite-horizon adaptive learning via a conditional interventional target, prove that replay-side information cannot recover it in general, and identify a structural class in which the target is identified from logged data.
中文标题/摘要

机器学习模型越来越多地生成自身的训练数据——在线赌博机、强化学习以及语言模型的后训练流程是典型示例。在这些自适应场景中，单个训练观测既更新学习器，又改变学习器未来收集数据的分布。为静态数据集设计的标准归因方法忽略了这种反馈。我们通过条件干预目标形式化了有限时域自适应学习中的实例级归因，证明重放侧信息通常无法恢复该目标，并识别出可从记录数据中确定该目标的结构类别。
