Synthetic Sandbox for Training Machine Learning Engineering Agents
Authors: Yuhang Zhou, Lizhu Zhang, Yifan Wu, Jiayi Liu, Xiangjun Fan, Zhuokai Zhao, Hong Yan
First: 2026-04-06T17:19:29+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-06T17:19:29+00:00
Comments: 28 pages, 9 tables, 8 figures
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
As large language model agents advance beyond software engineering (SWE) tasks toward machine learning engineering (MLE), verifying agent behavior becomes orders of magnitude more expensive: while SWE tasks can be verified via fast-executing unit tests, MLE verification requires running full ML pipelines -- data preprocessing, model training, and metric evaluation -- on large datasets at each rollout step, rendering trajectory-wise on-policy reinforcement learning (RL) prohibitively slow. Existing approaches retreat to supervised fine-tuning (SFT) or offline proxy rewards, sacrificing the exploration and generalization benefits of on-policy RL. We observe that sandbox data size is the primary source of this bottleneck. Based on this insight, we introduce SandMLE, a multi-agent framework that generates diverse, verifiable synthetic MLE environments from a small number of seed tasks, preserving the structural and technical complexity of real-world problems while constraining datasets to micro-scale (each task is paired with only 50-200 training samples). Through extensive experiments, we show that SandMLE reduces execution time by over 13 times, enabling large-scale, on-policy trajectory-wise RL for the first time in the MLE domain. On MLE-bench-lite, SandMLE yields significant gains over SFT baselines across Qwen3-8B, 14B, and 30B-A3B, with relative medal rate improvements ranging from 20.3% to 66.9%. Furthermore, the trained policy generalizes across unseen agentic scaffolds, achieving up to 32.4% better HumanRank score on MLE-Dojo.
中文标题/摘要
标题：用于训练机器学习工程智能体的合成沙盒
随着大语言模型智能体从软件工程任务向机器学习工程任务演进，验证智能体行为的成本呈数量级增长：软件工程任务可通过快速执行的单元测试验证，而机器学习工程验证需要在每次迭代中于大规模数据集上运行完整的机器学习流水线——包括数据预处理、模型训练和指标评估——导致基于轨迹的在线强化学习变得极其缓慢。现有方法退而采用监督微调或离线代理奖励，牺牲了在线强化学习的探索与泛化优势。我们发现沙盒数据规模是这一瓶颈的主要根源。基于此洞见，我们提出了SandMLE——一个多智能体框架，可从少量种子任务生成多样化、可验证的合成机器学习工程环境，在保持现实问题结构和技术复杂性的同时，将数据集约束至微规模（每个任务仅包含50-200个训练样本）。大量实验表明，SandMLE将执行时间缩短超过13倍，首次在机器学习工程领域实现了大规模、基于轨迹的在线强化学习。在MLE-bench-lite基准测试中，SandMLE在Qwen3-8B、14B和30B-A3B模型上均显著超越监督微调基线，相对奖牌率提升幅度达20.3%至66.9%。此外，训练所得策略能泛化至未见过的智能体架构，在MLE-Dojo上取得最高32.4%的HumanRank分数提升。

Experimental results show that SandMLE cuts execution time by over 13 times, enabling effective on-policy RL and outperforming supervised fine-tuning baselines on models like Qwen3-8B, 14B, and 30B-A3B with medal rate improvements of 20.3% to 66.9%, while also generalizing well to unseen agent scaffolds with up to 32.4% better HumanRank scores.
本文针对大语言模型代理在机器学习工程任务中验证成本高昂的问题，提出了一种解决方案：由于传统在线策略强化学习需要在大数据集上运行完整ML流程而难以实施，作者开发了SandMLE多智能体框架，该框架从少量种子任务生成多样化的合成MLE环境，每个任务仅使用50-200个训练样本的微规模数据集，在保持真实问题复杂性的同时大幅降低执行时间。实验表明，SandMLE将执行时间减少超过13倍，首次在MLE领域实现了大规模在线策略强化学习，在Qwen3-8B、14B和30B-A3B等模型上相比监督微调基线获得20.3%至66.9%的奖牌率提升，并且在未见过的智能体框架上泛化能力良好，HumanRank分数最高提升32.4%。
Large Language Model Guided Incentive Aware Reward Design for Cooperative Multi-Agent Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Dogan Urgun, Gokhan Gungor
First: 2026-03-25T14:05:59+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-06T16:20:35+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Designing effective auxiliary rewards for cooperative multi-agent systems remains challenging, as misaligned incentives can induce suboptimal coordination, particularly when sparse task rewards provide insufficient grounding for coordinated behavior. This study introduces an automated reward design framework that uses large language models to synthesize executable reward programs from environment instrumentation. The procedure constrains candidate programs within a formal validity envelope and trains policies from scratch using MAPPO under a fixed computational budget. The candidates are then evaluated based on their performance, and selection across generations relies solely on the sparse task returns. The framework is evaluated in four Overcooked-AI layouts characterized by varying levels of corridor congestion, handoff dependencies, and structural asymmetries. The proposed reward design approach consistently yields higher task returns and delivery counts, with the most pronounced gains observed in environments dominated by interaction bottlenecks. Diagnostic analysis of the synthesized shaping components reveals stronger interdependence in action selection and improved signal alignment in coordination-intensive tasks. These results demonstrate that the proposed LLM-guided reward search framework mitigates the need for manual engineering while producing shaping signals compatible with cooperative learning under finite budgets.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于大语言模型引导的激励感知奖励设计用于协作多智能体强化学习
为协作多智能体系统设计有效的辅助奖励仍具挑战性，因为激励错位可能导致次优协调，尤其在稀疏任务奖励无法为协作行为提供充分依据时。本研究提出一种自动化奖励设计框架，利用大语言模型从环境监测数据中合成可执行的奖励程序。该流程将候选程序约束在形式化有效范围内，并在固定计算预算下使用MAPPO从头训练策略。随后根据性能评估候选方案，代际选择仅依赖稀疏任务回报。该框架在四种具有不同走廊拥堵程度、交接依赖性和结构不对称性的《Overcooked-AI》场景中进行评估。所提出的奖励设计方法持续产生更高的任务回报和配送数量，在交互瓶颈主导的环境中增益最为显著。对合成塑形组件的诊断分析显示，在协作密集型任务中动作选择的相互依赖性更强，信号对齐性得到改善。这些结果表明，所提出的LLM引导奖励搜索框架减少了对人工工程的需求，同时生成与有限预算下协作学习兼容的塑形信号。
Summary / 总结
This study addresses the challenge of designing effective auxiliary rewards for cooperative multi-agent systems, where sparse task rewards often lead to suboptimal coordination due to misaligned incentives. The authors propose an automated reward design framework that leverages large language models to generate executable reward programs from environment instrumentation, constraining candidates within a formal validity envelope and training policies from scratch using MAPPO under a fixed computational budget. Evaluated in four Overcooked-AI layouts with varying congestion and dependencies, the framework consistently achieves higher task returns and delivery counts, particularly in environments with interaction bottlenecks, while diagnostic analysis shows improved action interdependence and signal alignment in coordination-intensive tasks, demonstrating its ability to reduce manual engineering while producing shaping signals suitable for cooperative learning.
本研究针对合作多智能体系统中辅助奖励设计困难的问题，提出了一种自动化奖励设计框架，利用大语言模型根据环境信息生成可执行的奖励程序，并将候选程序约束在形式化有效范围内，在固定计算预算下使用MAPPO从头训练策略。在四个具有不同拥堵程度和依赖关系的Overcooked-AI布局中评估，该框架始终获得更高的任务回报和交付数量，尤其在存在交互瓶颈的环境中效果最显著；诊断分析显示，在协调密集型任务中，合成出的奖励组件增强了动作选择的相互依赖性和信号对齐，表明该框架能减少人工设计需求，同时生成适用于有限预算下合作学习的奖励信号。
Selecting Decision-Relevant Concepts in Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Naveen Raman, Stephanie Milani, Fei Fang
First: 2026-04-06T16:12:42+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-06T16:12:42+00:00
Comments: 16 pages, 13 figures
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Training interpretable concept-based policies requires practitioners to manually select which human-understandable concepts an agent should reason with when making sequential decisions. This selection demands domain expertise, is time-consuming and costly, scales poorly with the number of candidates, and provides no performance guarantees. To overcome this limitation, we propose the first algorithms for principled automatic concept selection in sequential decision-making. Our key insight is that concept selection can be viewed through the lens of state abstraction: intuitively, a concept is decision-relevant if removing it would cause the agent to confuse states that require different actions. As a result, agents should rely on decision-relevant concepts; states with the same concept representation should share the same optimal action, which preserves the optimal decision structure of the original state space. This perspective leads to the Decision-Relevant Selection (DRS) algorithm, which selects a subset of concepts from a candidate set, along with performance bounds relating the selected concepts to the performance of the resulting policy. Empirically, DRS automatically recovers manually curated concept sets while matching or exceeding their performance, and improves the effectiveness of test-time concept interventions across reinforcement learning benchmarks and real-world healthcare environments.
中文标题/摘要
标题：强化学习中决策相关概念的选择
训练基于可解释概念的策略需要从业者手动选择智能体在序列决策时应使用哪些人类可理解的概念。这种选择需要领域专业知识，耗时耗力，难以随候选概念数量扩展，且无法提供性能保证。为克服这一局限，我们提出了首个用于序列决策中原则性自动概念选择的算法。核心洞见在于：概念选择可通过状态抽象的视角来理解——直观上，若移除某个概念会导致智能体混淆需要不同行动的状态，则该概念具有决策相关性。因此，智能体应依赖决策相关概念；具有相同概念表征的状态应共享相同的最优行动，从而保留原始状态空间的最优决策结构。这一视角催生了决策相关选择（DRS）算法，该算法从候选集中选择概念子集，并提供将所选概念与策略性能关联的性能边界。实证表明，DRS能自动恢复人工筛选的概念集，同时达到或超越其性能，并在强化学习基准测试和真实医疗环境中提升了测试时概念干预的有效性。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the challenge of manually selecting human-understandable concepts for interpretable reinforcement learning policies, which is costly and lacks performance guarantees. To automate this, the authors propose viewing concept selection through state abstraction, where a concept is decision-relevant if its removal confuses states requiring different actions, leading to the Decision-Relevant Selection (DRS) algorithm that selects concepts while preserving optimal decision structures. Experimental results show that DRS automatically recovers manually curated concept sets, matches or exceeds their performance, and improves concept intervention effectiveness in RL benchmarks and real-world healthcare settings.
该论文针对强化学习中手动选择可解释概念策略的成本高且缺乏性能保证的问题，提出将概念选择视为状态抽象，即如果一个概念的移除会导致需要不同动作的状态混淆，则该概念具有决策相关性，从而开发了决策相关选择（DRS）算法来自动选择概念并保持最优决策结构。实验结果表明，DRS能自动恢复手动筛选的概念集，匹配或超越其性能，并在强化学习基准和真实医疗环境中提升了概念干预的有效性。
An Information-Theoretic Analysis of OOD Generalization in Meta-Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Xingtu Liu
First: 2025-10-27T15:52:23+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-06T16:08:29+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
In this work, we study out-of-distribution (OOD) generalization in meta-reinforcement learning from an information-theoretic perspective. We begin by establishing OOD generalization bounds for meta-supervised learning under two distinct distribution shift scenarios: standard distribution mismatch and a broad-to-narrow training setting. Building on this foundation, we formalize the generalization problem in meta-reinforcement learning and establish fine-grained generalization bounds that exploit the structure of Markov Decision Processes. Lastly, we analyze the generalization performance of a gradient-based meta-reinforcement learning algorithm.
中文标题/摘要
标题：元强化学习中分布外泛化的信息论分析
本文从信息论角度研究元强化学习中的分布外泛化问题。首先，我们在两种分布偏移场景下为元监督学习建立分布外泛化界：标准分布失配与宽泛到狭窄的训练设置。基于此，我们形式化元强化学习中的泛化问题，并利用马尔可夫决策过程的结构建立细粒度泛化界。最后，我们分析一种基于梯度的元强化学习算法的泛化性能。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the need to understand out-of-distribution generalization in meta-reinforcement learning, this paper adopts an information-theoretic perspective. The method involves first establishing generalization bounds for meta-supervised learning under two distribution shift scenarios, then formalizing the problem for meta-reinforcement learning to derive fine-grained bounds that leverage Markov Decision Process structure. The main experimental results include the derivation of these generalization bounds and an analysis demonstrating the generalization performance of a gradient-based meta-reinforcement learning algorithm.
本文旨在从信息论角度研究元强化学习中的分布外泛化问题。方法上，首先为元监督学习在两种分布偏移场景下建立了泛化界，进而形式化元强化学习的泛化问题，利用马尔可夫决策过程的结构推导出细粒度的泛化界。主要实验结果包括这些泛化界的建立，以及对一种基于梯度的元强化学习算法泛化性能的分析。
Multi-Agent Environments for Vehicle Routing Problems
Authors: Ricardo Gama, Ricardo Cunha, Daniel Fuertes, Carlos R. del-Blanco, Hugo L. Fernandes
First: 2024-11-21T18:46:23+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-06T16:01:44+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Research on Reinforcement Learning (RL) approaches for discrete optimization problems has increased considerably, extending RL to areas classically dominated by Operations Research (OR). Vehicle routing problems are a good example of discrete optimization problems with high practical relevance, for which RL techniques have achieved notable success. Despite these advances, open-source development frameworks remain scarce, hindering both algorithm testing and objective comparison of results. This situation ultimately slows down progress in the field and limits the exchange of ideas between the RL and OR communities. Here, we propose MAEnvs4VRP library, a unified framework for multi-agent vehicle routing environments that supports classical, dynamic, stochastic, and multi-task problem variants within a single modular design. The library, built on PyTorch, provides a flexible and modular architecture design that facilitates customization and the incorporation of new routing problems. It follows the Agent Environment Cycle ("AEC") games model and features an intuitive API, enabling rapid adoption and seamless integration into existing reinforcement learning frameworks. The project source code can be found at https://github.com/ricgama/maenvs4vrp.

标题：面向车辆路径问题的多智能体环境库

Cog-DRIFT: Exploration on Adaptively Reformulated Instances Enables Learning from Hard Reasoning Problems
Authors: Justin Chih-Yao Chen, Archiki Prasad, Zaid Khan, Joykirat Singh, Runchu Tian, Elias Stengel-Eskin, Mohit Bansal
First: 2026-04-06T15:38:38+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-06T15:38:38+00:00
Comments: 22 pages, 4 figures. Code: https://github.com/dinobby/Cog-DRIFT
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Reinforcement learning from verifiable rewards (RLVR) has improved the reasoning abilities of LLMs, yet a fundamental limitation remains: models cannot learn from problems that are too difficult to solve under their current policy, as these yield no meaningful reward signal. We propose a simple yet effective solution based on task reformulation. We transform challenging open-ended problems into cognitively simpler variants -- such as multiple-choice and cloze formats -- that preserve the original answer while reducing the effective search space and providing denser learning signals. These reformulations span a spectrum from discriminative to generative tasks, which we exploit to bootstrap learning: models first learn from structured, easier formats, and this knowledge transfers back to improve performance on the original open-ended problems. Building on this insight, we introduce Cog-DRIFT, a framework that constructs reformulated variants and organizes them into an adaptive curriculum based on difficulty. Training progresses from easier to harder formats, enabling the model to learn from problems that previously yielded zero signal under standard RL post-training. Cog-DRIFT not only improves on the originally unsolvable hard problems (absolute +10.11% for Qwen and +8.64% for Llama) but also generalizes well to other held-out datasets. Across 2 models and 6 reasoning benchmarks, our method consistently outperforms standard GRPO and strong guided-exploration baselines. On average, Cog-DRIFT shows +4.72% (Qwen) and +3.23% (Llama) improvements over the second-best baseline. We further show that Cog-DRIFT improves pass@k at test time, and the curriculum improves sample efficiency. Overall, our results highlight task reformulation and curriculum learning as an effective paradigm for overcoming the exploration barrier in LLM post-training.
中文标题/摘要
标题：Cog-DRIFT：基于自适应重构问题实例的探索助力大语言模型从困难推理问题中学习
基于可验证奖励的强化学习（RLVR）虽已提升了大语言模型的推理能力，但仍存在根本局限：模型无法从当前策略下过于困难、无法解决的问题中学习，因为这些难题无法提供有效的奖励信号。我们提出了一种基于任务重构的简洁有效方案：将具有挑战性的开放式问题转化为认知上更简单的变体（如选择题和完形填空），这些变体在保留原答案的同时，缩小了有效搜索空间并提供更密集的学习信号。这些重构任务覆盖了从判别式到生成式的谱系，我们借此引导学习过程：模型首先从结构化、更简单的格式中学习，再将习得的知识迁移回原始开放式问题以提升性能。基于此洞见，我们提出了Cog-DRIFT框架，该框架构建重构变体并根据难度将其组织成自适应课程。训练从易到难逐步推进，使模型能够从原本在标准RL后训练中无法获得信号的问题中学习。Cog-DRIFT不仅在原不可解的难题上取得显著提升（Qwen绝对提升+10.11%，Llama+8.64%），还能良好泛化至其他保留数据集。在2个模型和6个推理基准测试中，我们的方法持续优于标准GRPO及强引导探索基线，平均较次优基线分别提升+4.72%（Qwen）和+3.23%（Llama）。我们进一步证明Cog-DRIFT能提升测试时的pass@k指标，且课程设计提高了样本效率。总体而言，我们的研究凸显了任务重构与课程学习作为突破大语言模型后训练探索瓶颈的有效范式。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses a key limitation in reinforcement learning from verifiable rewards (RLVR) for large language models (LLMs), where models fail to learn from problems too difficult to solve under their current policy due to a lack of reward signal. To overcome this, the authors propose Cog-DRIFT, a framework that adaptively reformulates hard open-ended reasoning problems into cognitively simpler variants, such as multiple-choice or cloze formats, which preserve the original answer but reduce search space and provide denser learning signals. These reformulations are organized into a curriculum from easier to harder tasks, enabling models to bootstrap learning and transfer knowledge back to the original problems. Experimental results show that Cog-DRIFT significantly improves performance on previously unsolvable hard problems, with absolute gains of +10.11% for Qwen and +8.64% for Llama models, and consistently outperforms baselines across six reasoning benchmarks, demonstrating enhanced generalization and sample efficiency.
本文针对大型语言模型在可验证奖励强化学习中存在的关键限制：模型无法从当前策略下过于困难的问题中学习，因为这些问题缺乏有效的奖励信号。为此，作者提出了Cog-DRIFT框架，通过自适应地将困难的开放式推理问题重构为认知上更简单的变体，如多项选择或完形填空格式，这些变体保留了原始答案，但减少了搜索空间并提供了更密集的学习信号。这些重构任务被组织成从易到难的课程，使模型能够从简单格式开始学习，并将知识迁移回原始问题。实验结果表明，Cog-DRIFT显著提升了在原本无法解决的困难问题上的性能，Qwen和Llama模型的绝对增益分别达到+10.11%和+8.64%，并在六个推理基准测试中持续优于基线方法，展现了良好的泛化能力和样本效率。
Discovering Failure Modes in Vision-Language Models using RL
Authors: Kanishk Jain, Qian Yang, Shravan Nayak, Parisa Kordjamshidi, Nishanth Anand, Aishwarya Agrawal
First: 2026-04-06T15:00:54+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-06T15:00:54+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Vision-language Models (VLMs), despite achieving strong performance on multimodal benchmarks, often misinterpret straightforward visual concepts that humans identify effortlessly, such as counting, spatial reasoning, and viewpoint understanding. Previous studies manually identified these weaknesses and found that they often stem from deficits in specific skills. However, such manual efforts are costly, unscalable, and subject to human bias, which often overlooks subtle details in favor of salient objects, resulting in an incomplete understanding of a model's vulnerabilities. To address these limitations, we propose a Reinforcement Learning (RL)-based framework to automatically discover the failure modes or blind spots of any candidate VLM on a given data distribution without human intervention. Our framework trains a questioner agent that adaptively generates queries based on the candidate VLM's responses to elicit incorrect answers. Our approach increases question complexity by focusing on fine-grained visual details and distinct skill compositions as training progresses, consequently identifying 36 novel failure modes in which VLMs struggle. We demonstrate the broad applicability of our framework by showcasing its generalizability across various model combinations.
中文标题/摘要
标题：利用强化学习发现视觉语言模型的失效模式
视觉语言模型（VLM）虽然在多模态基准测试中表现出色，却常误判人类能轻易识别的直观视觉概念，如计数、空间推理和视角理解。先前研究通过人工方式识别这些缺陷，发现其常源于特定技能缺失，但人工方法成本高、难以扩展且易受主观偏差影响，往往忽略细微细节而关注显著对象，导致对模型缺陷的理解不全面。为突破这些局限，我们提出基于强化学习（RL）的框架，可在无需人工干预的情况下，自动发现任意候选VLM在给定数据分布中的失效模式或盲点。该框架训练提问智能体，根据候选VLM的响应自适应生成查询以诱发错误答案。通过聚焦细粒度视觉细节和差异化技能组合，我们的方法在训练过程中逐步提升问题复杂度，最终识别出36种VLM难以应对的新型失效模式。通过展示框架在不同模型组合间的泛化能力，我们验证了其广泛适用性。

The proposed method is a Reinforcement Learning (RL) framework that trains a questioner agent to automatically generate progressively more complex queries targeting fine-grained details and skill combinations, thereby eliciting incorrect answers from a candidate VLM without human intervention. The main experimental results show that this approach successfully discovered 36 novel failure modes where VLMs struggle and demonstrated generalizability across different model combinations.

Diffusion-based Evolutionary Optimization for 3D Multi-Objective Molecular Generation
Authors: Ruiqing Sun, Dawei Feng, Sen Yang, Ronghang Wang, Huaiyuan Song, Bo Ding, Yijie Wang, Huaimin Wang
First: 2025-05-16T09:32:40+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-06T14:58:35+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
In 3D molecular discovery, optimizing conflicting physicochemical properties while strictly adhering to complex structural constraints constitutes a Constrained Multi-Objective Optimization Problem (CMOP). Solving this remains highly challenging: applying traditional Evolutionary Algorithm (EA) operators directly to 3D coordinates destroys chemical validity, whereas valid 3D diffusion models act as rigid generators unable to adapt to novel objectives without retraining. Moreover, employing traditional EA frameworks causes a severe loss of structural diversity, ultimately impairing algorithmic convergence. To overcome these challenges, we propose the Evolutionary-Guided Diffusion (EGD) operator, which executes crossover and mutation exclusively within the continuous noise space at an appropriate noise intensity. EGD enables topological hybridization while leveraging a pre-trained denoising network to project intermediate states back onto the valid chemical manifold. To tackle Multi-Objective Problems (MOPs), we introduce a Structure-Aware Environmental Selection (SAES) mechanism that explicitly enforces geometric diversity. Building upon this, to specifically solve CMOPs, we develop the Diffusion-based Evolutionary Molecular Optimization (DEMO) framework, utilizing a tri-population architecture with distinct responsibilities to safely navigate disjoint feasible regions. Extensive experiments across single-property targeting, unconstrained MOPs, multi-fragment constrained generation, and 3D protein-ligand docking demonstrate that DEMO comprehensively outperforms train-free guidance methods and EA baselines. Without any model retraining, DEMO successfully discovers highly diverse, chemically valid Pareto frontiers, establishing a robust paradigm for complex 3D molecular optimization.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于扩散的进化优化用于三维多目标分子生成
在三维分子发现中，优化相互冲突的理化性质并严格遵循复杂结构约束构成了一个约束多目标优化问题。解决此问题仍极具挑战：将传统进化算法算子直接应用于三维坐标会破坏化学有效性，而有效的三维扩散模型则作为刚性生成器，无法适应新目标而无需重新训练。此外，采用传统进化算法框架会导致结构多样性严重丧失，最终损害算法收敛性。为克服这些挑战，我们提出了进化引导扩散算子，该算子仅在连续噪声空间中以适当噪声强度执行交叉和变异操作。进化引导扩散算子实现了拓扑杂交，同时利用预训练去噪网络将中间状态投影回有效化学流形。针对多目标问题，我们引入了结构感知环境选择机制，明确强制几何多样性。在此基础上，为专门解决约束多目标优化问题，我们开发了基于扩散的进化分子优化框架，采用具有不同职责的三种群架构以安全探索不相交可行区域。在单属性靶向、无约束多目标问题、多片段约束生成及三维蛋白质-配体对接等广泛实验中，基于扩散的进化分子优化框架全面优于免训练引导方法和进化算法基线。无需任何模型重新训练，基于扩散的进化分子优化框架成功发现了高度多样化、化学有效的帕累托前沿，为复杂三维分子优化建立了稳健范式。
Summary / 总结
This work addresses the challenge of 3D molecular discovery as a Constrained Multi-Objective Optimization Problem (CMOP), where traditional Evolutionary Algorithms (EAs) disrupt chemical validity and diffusion models lack adaptability. The proposed solution is the Diffusion-based Evolutionary Molecular Optimization (DEMO) framework, which introduces an Evolutionary-Guided Diffusion (EGD) operator to perform crossover and mutation in noise space, preserving validity via a pre-trained denoiser, and a Structure-Aware Environmental Selection (SAES) mechanism to maintain geometric diversity. Experimental results across tasks like single-property optimization and protein-ligand docking show that DEMO outperforms existing train-free guidance and EA baselines, generating diverse, valid Pareto frontiers without model retraining.
本研究针对三维分子发现中的约束多目标优化问题，传统进化算法会破坏化学有效性，而扩散模型则缺乏适应性。提出的解决方案是基于扩散的进化分子优化框架，它引入了进化引导扩散算子，在噪声空间执行交叉和变异，通过预训练去噪网络保持化学有效性，并采用结构感知环境选择机制维持几何多样性。在单属性优化、蛋白质-配体对接等任务上的实验表明，该框架优于现有的无训练引导方法和进化算法基线，无需模型重训练即可生成多样且有效的帕累托前沿。
Ranking Constraints via Topological Dual-Directional Search in Evolutionary Multi-Objective Optimization
Authors: Ruiqing Sun, Dawei Feng, Sheng Qi, Xing Zhou, Lianghao Li, Bo Ding, Yijie Wang, Rui Wang, Huaimin Wang
First: 2026-04-06T14:47:26+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-06T14:47:26+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Existing evolutionary algorithms for Constrained Multi-objective Optimization Problems (CMOPs) typically treat all constraints uniformly, overlooking their distinct geometric relationships with the true Constrained Pareto Front (CPF). In reality, constraints play different roles: some directly shape the final CPF, some create infeasible obstacles, while others are irrelevant. To exploit this insight, we propose a novel algorithm named RCCMO, which sequentially performs unconstrained exploration, single-constraint exploitation, and full-constraint refinement. The core innovation of RCCMO lies in a constraint prioritization method derived from these geometric insights, seamlessly coupled with a unique dual-directional search mechanism. Specifically, RCCMO first prioritizes constraints that constitute the final CPF, approaching them from the evolutionary direction (optimizing objectives) to locate the CPF directly shaped by single-constraint boundaries. Subsequently, for constraints that merely hinder the population's progress, RCCMO searches from the anti-evolutionary direction (targeting the infeasible boundaries where hindering constraints intersect with the CPF) to effectively discover how these constraints obstruct and form the final CPF. Meanwhile, irrelevant constraints are intentionally bypassed. Furthermore, a series of specialized mechanisms are proposed to accelerate the algorithm's execution, reduce heuristic misjudgments, and dynamically adjust search directions in real time. Extensive experiments on 5 benchmark test suites and 29 real-world CMOPs demonstrate that RCCMO significantly outperforms seven state-of-the-art algorithms.
中文标题/摘要
标题：进化多目标优化中基于拓扑双向搜索的约束排序方法
现有约束多目标优化问题（CMOPs）的进化算法通常对所有约束进行统一处理，忽略了它们与真实约束帕累托前沿（CPF）之间不同的几何关系。实际上，约束扮演着不同角色：有些直接塑造最终CPF，有些形成不可行障碍，而其他则无关紧要。为利用这一洞见，我们提出名为RCCMO的新算法，依次执行无约束探索、单约束利用和全约束精细化。RCCMO的核心创新在于基于几何洞见推导的约束优先级排序方法，并与独特的双向搜索机制无缝结合。具体而言，RCCMO首先优先处理构成最终CPF的约束，从进化方向（优化目标）逼近，定位由单约束边界直接塑造的CPF。随后，对于仅阻碍种群进展的约束，RCCMO从反进化方向（针对阻碍约束与CPF相交的不可行边界）进行搜索，以有效发现这些约束如何阻碍并最终形成CPF。同时，无关约束被有意绕过。此外，本文提出一系列专门机制以加速算法执行、减少启发式误判，并实时动态调整搜索方向。在5个基准测试套件和29个实际CMOPs上的大量实验表明，RCCMO显著优于七种先进算法。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the limitation of existing evolutionary algorithms for Constrained Multi-objective Optimization Problems (CMOPs) that treat all constraints uniformly, failing to account for their distinct geometric roles relative to the true Constrained Pareto Front (CPF). To exploit this, the authors propose RCCMO, an algorithm that prioritizes constraints based on whether they shape, hinder, or are irrelevant to the CPF, and employs a dual-directional search mechanism: it approaches shaping constraints from the evolutionary direction (optimizing objectives) and hindering constraints from the anti-evolutionary direction (targeting infeasible boundaries). Experimental results on 5 benchmark suites and 29 real-world CMOPs show that RCCMO significantly outperforms seven state-of-the-art algorithms.
本文针对现有约束多目标优化问题进化算法将所有约束同等对待、忽略其与真实约束帕累托前沿不同几何关系的局限性，提出了一种名为RCCMO的新算法。该方法基于约束是塑造、阻碍还是无关乎前沿的几何洞察对约束进行优先级排序，并采用双向搜索机制：从进化方向逼近塑造性约束以优化目标，从反进化方向搜索阻碍性约束以定位不可行边界。在5个基准测试集和29个实际约束问题上的实验表明，RCCMO显著优于七种先进算法。
Anticipatory Reinforcement Learning: From Generative Path-Laws to Distributional Value Functions
Authors: Daniel Bloch
First: 2026-04-06T13:15:44+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-06T13:15:44+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
This paper introduces Anticipatory Reinforcement Learning (ARL), a novel framework designed to bridge the gap between non-Markovian decision processes and classical reinforcement learning architectures, specifically under the constraint of a single observed trajectory. In environments characterised by jump-diffusions and structural breaks, traditional state-based methods often fail to capture the essential path-dependent geometry required for accurate foresight. We resolve this by lifting the state space into a signature-augmented manifold, where the history of the process is embedded as a dynamical coordinate. By utilising a self-consistent field approach, the agent maintains an anticipated proxy of the future path-law, allowing for a deterministic evaluation of expected returns. This transition from stochastic branching to a single-pass linear evaluation significantly reduces computational complexity and variance. We prove that this framework preserves fundamental contraction properties and ensures stable generalisation even in the presence of heavy-tailed noise. Our results demonstrate that by grounding reinforcement learning in the topological features of path-space, agents can achieve proactive risk management and superior policy stability in highly volatile, continuous-time environments.
中文标题/摘要
标题：预期强化学习：从生成路径律到分布价值函数
本文提出预期强化学习（ARL），这一新颖框架旨在弥合非马尔可夫决策过程与经典强化学习架构之间的差距，特别是在单条观测轨迹的约束下。在具有跳跃扩散和结构突变特征的环境中，传统的基于状态的方法往往无法捕捉准确预测所需的路径依赖几何结构。我们通过将状态空间提升至签名增强流形来解决这一问题，其中过程的历史被嵌入为动态坐标。通过采用自洽场方法，智能体维持对未来路径律的预期代理，从而实现对期望收益的确定性评估。这种从随机分支到单次线性评估的转变显著降低了计算复杂性和方差。我们证明该框架保留了基本收缩性质，并确保即使在重尾噪声存在下也能实现稳定泛化。结果表明，通过将强化学习建立在路径空间的拓扑特征上，智能体能在高度波动的连续时间环境中实现主动风险管理和更优的策略稳定性。
Summary / 总结
This paper introduces Anticipatory Reinforcement Learning (ARL), motivated by the need to bridge non-Markovian decision processes and classical reinforcement learning under the constraint of a single observed trajectory, particularly in environments with jump-diffusions and structural breaks where traditional state-based methods fail to capture path-dependent geometry. The method resolves this by lifting the state space into a signature-augmented manifold, embedding process history as a dynamical coordinate, and using a self-consistent field approach to maintain an anticipated proxy of the future path-law for deterministic evaluation of expected returns, thereby reducing computational complexity and variance by transitioning from stochastic branching to single-pass linear evaluation. Experimental results demonstrate that this framework preserves contraction properties and ensures stable generalization even with heavy-tailed noise, enabling agents to achieve proactive risk management and superior policy stability in highly volatile, continuous-time environments by grounding reinforcement learning in the topological features of path-space.
本文提出了预期强化学习（ARL），其动机在于需要在单条观测轨迹的约束下，桥接非马尔可夫决策过程与经典强化学习，特别是在具有跳跃扩散和结构突变的环境中，传统基于状态的方法无法捕捉路径依赖的几何特征。该方法通过将状态空间提升至签名增强流形，将过程历史嵌入为动态坐标，并利用自洽场方法维持未来路径律的预期代理，以确定性评估期望回报，从而通过从随机分支转向单次线性评估，降低了计算复杂性和方差。实验结果证明，该框架即使在存在重尾噪声的情况下也能保持收缩性质并确保稳定的泛化能力，通过将强化学习建立在路径空间的拓扑特征上，使智能体能够在高度波动的连续时间环境中实现主动风险管理和更优的策略稳定性。
Making Bias Non-Predictive: Training Robust LLM Reasoning via Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Qian Wang, Xuandong Zhao, Zirui Zhang, Zhanzhi Lou, Nuo Chen, Dawn Song, Bingsheng He
First: 2026-02-02T01:43:48+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-06T12:42:42+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Large language models (LLMs) increasingly serve as reasoners and automated evaluators, yet they remain susceptible to cognitive biases -- often altering their reasoning when faced with spurious prompt-level cues such as consensus claims or authority appeals.} Existing mitigations via prompting or supervised fine-tuning fail to generalize, as they modify surface behavior without changing the optimization objective that makes bias cues attractive. We propose \textbf{Epistemic Independence Training (EIT)}, a reinforcement learning framework grounded in a key principle: to learn independence, bias cues must be made non-predictive of reward. EIT operationalizes this through a balanced conflict strategy where bias signals are equally likely to support correct and incorrect answers, combined with a reward design that penalizes bias-following without rewarding bias agreement. Experiments on Qwen3-4B demonstrate that EIT improves both accuracy and robustness under adversarial biases, while preserving performance when bias aligns with truth. Notably, models trained only on bandwagon bias generalize to unseen bias types such as authority and distraction, indicating that EIT induces transferable epistemic independence rather than bias-specific heuristics. \revised{EIT further generalizes across benchmarks (MedQA, HellaSwag), model families (Llama-3.2-3B), and scales (Qwen3-8B), and outperforms distribution-shift methods (GroupDRO, IRM) without requiring environment labels.} Code and data are available at https://anonymous.4open.science/r/bias-mitigation-with-rl-BC47
中文标题/摘要
标题：使偏见不可预测：通过强化学习训练稳健的大语言模型推理能力
大语言模型（LLMs）日益成为推理器和自动评估工具，但仍易受认知偏见影响——常因虚假提示线索（如共识主张或权威诉求）而改变推理。现有通过提示或监督微调的缓解方法因仅改变表面行为而未调整使偏见线索具有吸引力的优化目标，故难以泛化。我们提出\textbf{认知独立性训练（EIT）}，这是一个基于核心原则的强化学习框架：要学习独立性，必须使偏见线索对奖励不可预测。EIT通过平衡冲突策略实现该原则——使偏见信号同等可能支持正确与错误答案，并结合奖励设计以惩罚盲从偏见而不奖励偏见附和。在Qwen3-4B上的实验表明，EIT在对抗性偏见下同时提升准确性与鲁棒性，且在偏见与事实一致时保持性能。值得注意的是，仅针对从众偏见训练的模型可泛化至未见偏见类型（如权威和干扰），表明EIT诱导的是可迁移的认知独立性而非特定偏见启发式。\revised{EIT进一步在基准测试（MedQA、HellaSwag）、模型家族（Llama-3.2-3B）和规模（Qwen3-8B）上展现泛化能力，且无需环境标签即优于分布偏移方法（GroupDRO、IRM）。}代码与数据详见 https://anonymous.4open.science/r/bias-mitigation-with-rl-BC47
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the susceptibility of large language models (LLMs) to cognitive biases, such as consensus claims or authority appeals, which can spuriously alter their reasoning. The authors propose Epistemic Independence Training (EIT), a reinforcement learning framework designed to make bias cues non-predictive of reward by employing a balanced conflict strategy where bias signals equally support correct and incorrect answers, coupled with a reward design that penalizes bias-following. Experimental results on models like Qwen3-4B show that EIT improves both accuracy and robustness under adversarial biases while maintaining performance when bias aligns with truth, and it generalizes to unseen bias types and across different benchmarks and model families, outperforming methods like GroupDRO and IRM without needing environment labels.
本文针对大语言模型容易受到认知偏见（如从众效应或权威诉求）影响而错误改变推理的问题，提出了一种名为认知独立性训练（EIT）的强化学习框架。该方法的核心是通过平衡冲突策略，使偏见信号同等支持正确和错误答案，并结合奖励设计惩罚跟随偏见的行为，从而使偏见线索无法预测奖励。在Qwen3-4B等模型上的实验结果表明，EIT提高了模型在对抗性偏见下的准确性和鲁棒性，同时在偏见与事实一致时保持性能，并且能够泛化到未见过的偏见类型以及不同的基准测试和模型系列，其表现优于GroupDRO和IRM等方法，且无需环境标签。
Paper Espresso: From Paper Overload to Research Insight
Authors: Mingzhe Du, Luu Anh Tuan, Dong Huang, See-kiong Ng
First: 2026-04-06T09:45:21+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-06T09:45:21+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
The accelerating pace of scientific publishing makes it increasingly difficult for researchers to stay current. We present Paper Espresso, an open-source platform that automatically discovers, summarizes, and analyzes trending arXiv papers. The system uses large language models (LLMs) to generate structured summaries with topical labels and keywords, and provides multi-granularity trend analysis at daily, weekly, and monthly scales through LLM-driven topic consolidation. Over 35 months of continuous deployment, Paper Espresso has processed over 13,300 papers and publicly released all structured metadata, revealing rich dynamics in the AI research landscape: a mid-2025 surge in reinforcement learning for LLM reasoning, non-saturating topic emergence (6,673 unique topics), and a positive correlation between topic novelty and community engagement (2.0x median upvotes for the most novel papers). A live demo is available at https://huggingface.co/spaces/Elfsong/Paper_Espresso.
中文标题/摘要
标题：论文浓缩咖啡：从文献过载到研究洞察
科学出版速度的加快使研究人员愈发难以跟进前沿进展。我们推出开源平台Paper Espresso，可自动发现、总结与分析arXiv热门论文。该系统利用大语言模型生成带主题标签与关键词的结构化摘要，并通过LLM驱动的主题整合提供日/周/月多粒度趋势分析。在连续部署35个月期间，平台已处理超13,300篇论文并公开全部结构化元数据，揭示了AI研究领域的丰富动态：2025年中旬出现LLM推理强化学习热潮，非饱和主题持续涌现（6,673个独立主题），且主题新颖度与社区参与度呈正相关（最具新颖性论文的中位数点赞量达2.0倍）。实时演示详见https://huggingface.co/spaces/Elfsong/Paper_Espresso。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the challenge of keeping up with the rapidly accelerating pace of scientific publishing, this work introduces Paper Espresso, an open-source platform designed to automatically discover, summarize, and analyze trending arXiv papers. The method employs large language models (LLMs) to generate structured summaries with topical labels and keywords, and provides multi-granularity trend analysis through LLM-driven topic consolidation. Key experimental results from over 35 months of deployment, processing more than 13,300 papers, reveal rich dynamics in AI research, including a mid-2025 surge in reinforcement learning for LLM reasoning, the emergence of 6,673 unique non-saturating topics, and a positive correlation between topic novelty and community engagement, with the most novel papers receiving 2.0x the median upvotes.
本研究旨在应对科学出版速度日益加快、研究人员难以跟进最新进展的挑战，提出了一个名为Paper Espresso的开源平台，用于自动发现、总结和分析arXiv上的热门论文。该方法利用大语言模型生成带有主题标签和关键词的结构化摘要，并通过大语言模型驱动的主题整合提供日度、周度和月度等多粒度趋势分析。在超过35个月的持续部署中，该系统处理了超过13,300篇论文，实验结果显示AI研究领域丰富的动态变化：包括2025年中旬强化学习用于大语言模型推理的研究激增，出现了6,673个独特的非饱和主题，以及主题新颖性与社区参与度呈正相关，最具新颖性的论文获得的中位数点赞数是平均水平的2.0倍。
FlashSAC: Fast and Stable Off-Policy Reinforcement Learning for High-Dimensional Robot Control
Authors: Donghu Kim, Youngdo Lee, Minho Park, Kinam Kim, I Made Aswin Nahendra, Takuma Seno, Sehee Min, Daniel Palenicek, Florian Vogt, Danica Kragic, Jan Peters, Jaegul Choo, Hojoon Lee
First: 2026-04-06T09:03:41+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-06T09:03:41+00:00
Comments: preprint, 40pages
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Reinforcement learning (RL) is a core approach for robot control when expert demonstrations are unavailable. On-policy methods such as Proximal Policy Optimization (PPO) are widely used for their stability, but their reliance on narrowly distributed on-policy data limits accurate policy evaluation in high-dimensional state and action spaces. Off-policy methods can overcome this limitation by learning from a broader state-action distribution, yet suffer from slow convergence and instability, as fitting a value function over diverse data requires many gradient updates, causing critic errors to accumulate through bootstrapping. We present FlashSAC, a fast and stable off-policy RL algorithm built on Soft Actor-Critic. Motivated by scaling laws observed in supervised learning, FlashSAC sharply reduces gradient updates while compensating with larger models and higher data throughput. To maintain stability at increased scale, FlashSAC explicitly bounds weight, feature, and gradient norms, curbing critic error accumulation. Across over 60 tasks in 10 simulators, FlashSAC consistently outperforms PPO and strong off-policy baselines in both final performance and training efficiency, with the largest gains on high-dimensional tasks such as dexterous manipulation. In sim-to-real humanoid locomotion, FlashSAC reduces training time from hours to minutes, demonstrating the promise of off-policy RL for sim-to-real transfer.
中文标题/摘要
标题：FlashSAC：面向高维机器人控制的快速稳定离线策略强化学习
在缺乏专家演示时，强化学习是机器人控制的核心方法。在线策略方法如近端策略优化因其稳定性被广泛使用，但其对分布狭窄的在线策略数据的依赖，限制了在高维状态与动作空间中进行准确策略评估。离线策略方法可通过学习更广泛的状态-动作分布来克服此限制，但面临收敛慢和不稳定的问题，因为拟合多样数据上的价值函数需要大量梯度更新，导致通过自举产生的评论家误差累积。本文提出FlashSAC，一种基于柔性演员-评论家框架的快速稳定离线策略强化学习算法。受监督学习中观察到的缩放定律启发，FlashSAC大幅减少梯度更新，同时以更大模型和更高数据吞吐量作为补偿。为在扩大规模时保持稳定性，FlashSAC显式地约束权重、特征和梯度范数，从而抑制评论家误差累积。在10个模拟器的60多项任务中，FlashSAC在最终性能和训练效率上均持续优于PPO及强离线策略基线，并在灵巧操作等高维任务上取得最大优势。在仿真到现实的人形机器人 locomotion 任务中，FlashSAC将训练时间从数小时缩短至数分钟，展现了离线策略强化学习在仿真到现实迁移中的潜力。
Summary / 总结
The paper introduces FlashSAC, an off-policy reinforcement learning algorithm designed to address the slow convergence and instability of existing off-policy methods in high-dimensional robot control tasks, where on-policy approaches like PPO are stable but data-inefficient. Motivated by scaling laws from supervised learning, the method builds on Soft Actor-Critic by drastically reducing the number of gradient updates while compensating with larger models and higher data throughput, and it incorporates explicit bounds on weight, feature, and gradient norms to maintain stability and prevent critic error accumulation. Experimental results across over 60 tasks in 10 simulators show that FlashSAC consistently outperforms PPO and other off-policy baselines in final performance and training efficiency, with particularly large gains on high-dimensional tasks like dexterous manipulation, and it enables sim-to-real humanoid locomotion training to be reduced from hours to minutes.
本文提出了FlashSAC算法，旨在解决高维机器人控制任务中现有离策略方法收敛慢和不稳定的问题，而像PPO这样的在策略方法虽稳定但数据效率低。受监督学习中缩放定律的启发，该方法基于Soft Actor-Critic，通过大幅减少梯度更新次数，同时采用更大模型和更高数据吞吐量进行补偿，并引入对权重、特征和梯度范数的显式约束以保持稳定性并防止评论器误差累积。在10个模拟器的60多个任务上的实验结果表明，FlashSAC在最终性能和训练效率上均一致优于PPO和其他离策略基线，尤其在灵巧操作等高维任务上提升显著，并将仿真到现实的人形机器人运动训练时间从数小时缩短到数分钟。
TSPO: Breaking the Double Homogenization Dilemma in Multi-turn Search Policy Optimization
Authors: Shichao Ma, Zhiyuan Ma, Ming Yang, Xiaofan Li, Xing Wu, Jintao Du, Yu Cheng, Weiqiang Wang, Qiliang Liu, Zhengyang Zhou, Yang Wang
First: 2026-01-30T09:58:45+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-06T08:29:58+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Multi-turn tool-integrated reasoning enables Large Language Models (LLMs) to solve complex tasks through iterative information retrieval. However, current reinforcement learning (RL) frameworks for search-augmented reasoning predominantly rely on sparse outcome-level rewards, leading to a "Double Homogenization Dilemma." This manifests as (1) Process homogenization, where the thinking, reasoning, and tooling involved in generation are ignored. (2) Intra-group homogenization, coarse-grained outcome rewards often lead to inefficiencies in intra-group advantage estimation with methods like Group Relative Policy Optimization (GRPO) during sampling. To address this, we propose Turn-level Stage-aware Policy Optimization (TSPO). TSPO introduces the First-Occurrence Latent Reward (FOLR) mechanism, allocating partial rewards to the step where the ground-truth answer first appears, thereby preserving process-level signals and increasing reward variance within groups without requiring external reward models or any annotations. Extensive experiments demonstrate that TSPO significantly outperforms state-of-the-art baselines, achieving average performance gains of 24% and 13.6% on Qwen2.5-3B and 7B models, respectively. Code is available at https://github.com/Flipped-May/TSPO.
中文标题/摘要
标题：TSPO：破解多轮搜索策略优化中的双重同质化困境
多轮工具集成推理使大语言模型（LLM）能够通过迭代信息检索解决复杂任务。然而，当前用于搜索增强推理的强化学习（RL）框架主要依赖稀疏的结果级奖励，导致“双重同质化困境”。这表现为：（1）过程同质化，即生成过程中的思考、推理和工具使用被忽略；（2）组内同质化，粗粒度的结果奖励常导致在采样时（如使用组相对策略优化GRPO方法）组内优势估计效率低下。为解决此问题，我们提出轮次级阶段感知策略优化（TSPO）。TSPO引入首次出现潜在奖励（FOLR）机制，将部分奖励分配给真实答案首次出现的步骤，从而保留过程级信号并增加组内奖励方差，且无需外部奖励模型或任何标注。大量实验表明，TSPO显著优于现有先进基线，在Qwen2.5-3B和7B模型上分别实现了平均24%和13.6%的性能提升。代码发布于https://github.com/Flipped-May/TSPO。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the Double Homogenization Dilemma in multi-turn search-augmented reasoning for LLMs, where sparse outcome-level rewards cause both process homogenization (ignoring intermediate reasoning steps) and intra-group homogenization (inefficient advantage estimation). The proposed method, Turn-level Stage-aware Policy Optimization (TSPO), introduces a First-Occurrence Latent Reward (FOLR) mechanism that allocates partial rewards to the step where the correct answer first appears, preserving process-level signals and increasing reward variance without external models or annotations. Experimental results show TSPO significantly outperforms state-of-the-art baselines, achieving average performance gains of 24% and 13.6% on Qwen2.5-3B and 7B models, respectively.
本文针对大型语言模型在多轮搜索增强推理中的“双重同质化困境”提出解决方案，该困境源于稀疏的结果级奖励导致过程同质化（忽略中间推理步骤）和组内同质化（优势估计效率低下）。所提出的方法——轮次级阶段感知策略优化（TSPO）引入了首次出现潜在奖励（FOLR）机制，将部分奖励分配给正确答案首次出现的步骤，从而保留过程级信号并增加组内奖励方差，且无需外部奖励模型或标注。实验结果表明，TSPO显著优于现有基线方法，在Qwen2.5-3B和7B模型上分别实现了24%和13.6%的平均性能提升。
Fine-tuning is Not Enough: A Parallel Framework for Collaborative Imitation and Reinforcement Learning in End-to-end Autonomous Driving
Authors: Zhexi Lian, Haoran Wang, Xuerun Yan, Weimeng Lin, Xianhong Zhang, Yongyu Chen, Jia Hu
First: 2026-03-14T08:53:47+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-06T08:06:45+00:00
Comments: 11 pages, 7 figures, 6 tables
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
End-to-end autonomous driving is typically built upon imitation learning (IL), yet its performance is constrained by the quality of human demonstrations. To overcome this limitation, recent methods incorporate reinforcement learning (RL) through sequential fine-tuning. However, such a paradigm remains suboptimal: sequential RL fine-tuning can introduce policy drift and often leads to a performance ceiling due to its dependence on the pretrained IL policy. To address these issues, we propose PaIR-Drive, a general Parallel framework for collaborative Imitation and Reinforcement learning in end-to-end autonomous driving. During training, PaIR-Drive separates IL and RL into two parallel branches with conflict-free training objectives, enabling fully collaborative optimization. This design eliminates the need to retrain RL when applying a new IL policy. During inference, RL leverages the IL policy to further optimize the final plan, allowing performance beyond prior knowledge of IL. Furthermore, we introduce a tree-structured trajectory neural sampler to group relative policy optimization (GRPO) in the RL branch, which enhances exploration capability. Extensive analysis on NAVSIMv1 and v2 benchmark demonstrates that PaIR-Drive achieves Competitive performance of 91.2 PDMS and 87.9 EPDMS, building upon Transfuser and DiffusionDrive IL baselines. PaIR-Drive consistently outperforms existing RL fine-tuning methods, and could even correct human experts' suboptimal behaviors. Qualitative results further confirm that PaIR-Drive can effectively explore and generate high-quality trajectories.
中文标题/摘要
标题：微调不足够：端到端自动驾驶中协同模仿与强化学习的并行框架
端到端自动驾驶通常基于模仿学习（IL）构建，但其性能受限于人类示范的质量。为突破这一局限，近期方法通过顺序微调引入强化学习（RL）。然而，这种范式仍非最优：顺序RL微调可能引发策略漂移，且因其对预训练IL策略的依赖常导致性能瓶颈。为解决这些问题，我们提出PaIR-Drive——一种用于端到端自动驾驶中协同模仿与强化学习的通用并行框架。训练期间，PaIR-Drive将IL与RL分离为具有无冲突训练目标的并行分支，实现完全协同优化。该设计在应用新IL策略时无需重新训练RL。推理阶段，RL利用IL策略进一步优化最终规划，使性能突破IL先验知识。此外，我们在RL分支中引入树形轨迹神经采样器进行分组相对策略优化（GRPO），以增强探索能力。在NAVSIMv1和v2基准上的大量分析表明，基于Transfuser和DiffusionDrive IL基线，PaIR-Drive实现了91.2 PDMS和87.9 EPDMS的竞争性性能。PaIR-Drive持续优于现有RL微调方法，甚至能修正人类专家的次优行为。定性结果进一步证实PaIR-Drive能有效探索并生成高质量轨迹。
Summary / 总结
The motivation for this work is to overcome the limitations of sequential fine-tuning in end-to-end autonomous driving, where imitation learning (IL) performance is constrained by human demonstrations and subsequent reinforcement learning (RL) fine-tuning can cause policy drift and performance ceilings. The proposed method, PaIR-Drive, introduces a parallel framework that separates IL and RL into two branches with conflict-free objectives during training, enabling collaborative optimization without retraining RL for new IL policies, and employs a tree-structured trajectory neural sampler for grouped relative policy optimization in the RL branch to enhance exploration. Main experimental results on the NAVSIMv1 and v2 benchmarks show that PaIR-Drive achieves competitive performance scores of 91.2 PDMS and 87.9 EPDMS, outperforming existing RL fine-tuning methods and even correcting suboptimal human expert behaviors, with qualitative analysis confirming its ability to generate high-quality trajectories.
本研究的动机是为了克服端到端自动驾驶中顺序微调的局限性，即模仿学习（IL）的性能受限于人类演示数据，而后续的强化学习（RL）微调可能导致策略漂移和性能瓶颈。所提出的方法PaIR-Drive采用了一种并行框架，在训练时将IL和RL分离为两个具有无冲突目标的并行分支，实现了协同优化，且无需为新的IL策略重新训练RL，并在RL分支中引入了树形轨迹神经采样器进行分组相对策略优化以增强探索能力。在NAVSIMv1和v2基准测试上的主要实验结果表明，PaIR-Drive取得了91.2 PDMS和87.9 EPDMS的竞争性性能分数，优于现有的RL微调方法，甚至能纠正人类专家的次优行为，定性分析进一步证实了其有效探索和生成高质量轨迹的能力。
RAPTOR: A Foundation Policy for Quadrotor Control
Authors: Jonas Eschmann, Dario Albani, Giuseppe Loianno
First: 2025-09-15T00:05:40+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-06T08:06:29+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Humans are remarkably data-efficient when adapting to new unseen conditions, like driving a new car. In contrast, modern robotic control systems, like neural network policies trained using Reinforcement Learning (RL), are highly specialized for single environments. Because of this overfitting, they are known to break down even under small differences like the Simulation-to-Reality (Sim2Real) gap and require system identification and retraining for even minimal changes to the system. In this work, we present RAPTOR, a method for training a highly adaptive foundation policy for quadrotor control. Our method enables training a single, end-to-end neural-network policy to control a wide variety of quadrotors. We test 10 different real quadrotors from 32 g to 2.4 kg that also differ in motor type (brushed vs. brushless), frame type (soft vs. rigid), propeller type (2/3/4-blade), and flight controller (PX4/Betaflight/Crazyflie/M5StampFly). We find that a tiny, three-layer policy with only 2084 parameters is sufficient for zero-shot adaptation to a wide variety of platforms. The adaptation through in-context learning is made possible by using a recurrence in the hidden layer. The policy is trained through our proposed Meta-Imitation Learning algorithm, where we sample 1000 quadrotors and train a teacher policy for each of them using RL. Subsequently, the 1000 teachers are distilled into a single, adaptive student policy. We find that within milliseconds, the resulting foundation policy adapts zero-shot to unseen quadrotors. We extensively test the capabilities of the foundation policy under numerous conditions (trajectory tracking, indoor/outdoor, wind disturbance, poking, different propellers).
中文标题/摘要
标题：RAPTOR：一种用于四旋翼控制的基座策略
人类在适应新环境（如驾驶新车）时表现出极高的数据效率，而现代机器人控制系统（如通过强化学习训练的神经网络策略）则高度专用于单一环境。这种过拟合导致它们在面对微小差异（如仿真到现实的差距）时即失效，且系统稍有变动便需重新识别和训练。本文提出RAPTOR方法，用于训练具有高度适应性的四旋翼控制基座策略。该方法通过端到端神经网络策略实现对多种四旋翼的通用控制。我们测试了10款真实四旋翼（重量32克至2.4千克），涵盖不同电机类型（有刷/无刷）、机架类型（柔性/刚性）、螺旋桨类型（2/3/4叶）及飞控系统（PX4/Betaflight/Crazyflie/M5StampFly）。研究发现，仅含2084参数的三层微型策略即可实现跨平台的零样本适应，其隐层递归机制支持上下文学习式自适应。策略通过我们提出的元模仿学习算法训练：采样1000种四旋翼配置并分别用强化学习训练教师策略，最终将千名教师策略蒸馏为单一自适应学生策略。实验表明，该基座策略能在毫秒级时间内零样本适应未知四旋翼，并在轨迹跟踪、室内外环境、风扰干扰、物理触碰及螺旋桨更换等多场景测试中展现出卓越性能。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the need for robotic control policies that can adapt efficiently to new conditions without extensive retraining, unlike specialized reinforcement learning policies that often fail with minor environmental changes, this paper introduces RAPTOR, a method for training a foundation policy for quadrotor control. The method employs a Meta-Imitation Learning approach, where 1000 teacher policies trained via reinforcement learning on diverse simulated quadrotors are distilled into a single, compact student neural network with only 2084 parameters and a recurrent hidden layer to enable in-context learning. Experimental results demonstrate that this policy achieves zero-shot adaptation to 10 different real quadrotors, varying in weight, motor type, frame, propeller, and flight controller, and performs robustly in trajectory tracking, indoor/outdoor environments, and under disturbances like wind and physical poking.
本文的动机是解决机器人控制策略因过度专业化而难以适应新环境的问题，例如模拟到现实的差距，这通常需要重新训练；为此，作者提出了RAPTOR方法，用于训练一种适用于四旋翼控制的通用基础策略。该方法采用元模仿学习算法，通过强化学习训练1000个不同四旋翼的教师策略，并将其蒸馏成一个仅含2084参数、具有循环隐藏层的学生神经网络策略，以实现上下文学习。实验结果表明，该策略能够零样本适应10种真实四旋翼飞行器，这些飞行器在重量、电机类型、框架、螺旋桨和飞行控制器上各不相同，并在轨迹跟踪、室内外环境以及风扰和物理干扰等多种条件下表现出鲁棒性能。
MPCFormer: A physics-informed data-driven approach for explainable socially-aware autonomous driving
Authors: Jia Hu, Zhexi Lian, Xuerun Yan, Ruiang Bi, Dou Shen, Yu Ruan, Chunlong Xia, Haoran Wang
First: 2025-12-03T13:43:33+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-06T07:53:28+00:00
Comments: 17 pages, 17 figures
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Autonomous Driving (AD) vehicles still struggle to exhibit human-like behavior in highly dynamic and interactive traffic scenarios. The key challenge lies in AD's limited ability to interact with surrounding vehicles, largely due to a lack of understanding the underlying mechanisms of social interaction. To address this issue, we introduce MPCFormer, an explainable socially-aware autonomous driving approach with physics-informed and data-driven coupled social interaction dynamics. In this model, the dynamics are formulated into a discrete space-state representation, which embeds physics priors to enhance modeling explainability. The dynamics coefficients are learned from naturalistic driving data via a Transformer-based encoder-decoder architecture. To the best of our knowledge, MPCFormer is the first approach to explicitly model the dynamics of multi-vehicle social interactions. The learned social interaction dynamics enable the planner to generate manifold, human-like behaviors when interacting with surrounding traffic. By leveraging the MPC framework, the approach mitigates the potential safety risks typically associated with purely learning-based methods. Open-looped evaluation on NGSIM dataset demonstrates that MPCFormer achieves superior social interaction awareness, yielding the lowest trajectory prediction errors compared with other state-of-the-art approaches. The prediction achieves an ADE as low as 0.86 m over a long prediction horizon of 5 seconds. Close-looped experiments in highly intense interaction scenarios, where consecutive lane changes are required to exit an off-ramp, further validate the effectiveness of MPCFormer. Results show that MPCFormer achieves the highest planning success rate of 94.67%, improves driving efficiency by 15.75%, and reduces the collision rate from 21.25% to 0.5%, outperforming a frontier Reinforcement Learning (RL) based planner.
中文标题/摘要
标题：MPCFormer：一种基于物理信息数据驱动的可解释社会感知自动驾驶方法
自动驾驶车辆在高度动态和交互的交通场景中仍难以展现类人行为。核心挑战在于自动驾驶与周围车辆交互的能力有限，主要源于对社交互动内在机制的理解不足。为解决此问题，我们提出了MPCFormer，一种结合物理信息与数据驱动的社交交互动力学、具备可解释性的社会感知自动驾驶方法。该模型将动力学表述为离散状态空间表示，嵌入物理先验以增强模型可解释性。动力学系数通过基于Transformer的编码器-解码器架构从自然驾驶数据中学习。据我们所知，MPCFormer是首个显式建模多车社交交互动力学的方法。习得的社交交互动力学使规划器能在与周围交通互动时生成多样化的类人行为。通过利用MPC框架，该方法缓解了纯学习方法通常存在的潜在安全风险。在NGSIM数据集上的开环评估表明，MPCFormer实现了卓越的社交交互感知能力，相比其他先进方法取得了最低的轨迹预测误差——在5秒长预测范围内平均位移误差低至0.86米。在需要连续变道驶离匝道的高强度交互场景中，闭环实验进一步验证了MPCFormer的有效性：其规划成功率最高达94.67%，驾驶效率提升15.75%，碰撞率从21.25%降至0.5%，优于前沿的强化学习规划器。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the challenge of autonomous vehicles exhibiting limited human-like social interaction in dynamic traffic by proposing MPCFormer, an explainable approach that couples physics-informed priors with data-driven learning to model multi-vehicle interaction dynamics. The method formulates these dynamics into a discrete state-space representation, where coefficients are learned from naturalistic driving data using a Transformer-based encoder-decoder, and integrates them into a Model Predictive Control (MPC) framework for safe planning. Experimental results on the NGSIM dataset show MPCFormer achieves the lowest trajectory prediction error with an ADE of 0.86m over 5 seconds, and in closed-loop tests, it attains a 94.67% planning success rate, improves efficiency by 15.75%, and reduces collisions from 21.25% to 0.5%, outperforming reinforcement learning-based planners.
本文针对自动驾驶车辆在动态交通中缺乏类人社会交互能力的问题，提出了MPCFormer，一种可解释的方法，通过结合物理先验与数据驱动学习来建模多车辆交互动力学。该方法将动力学表述为离散状态空间形式，利用基于Transformer的编码器-解码器从自然驾驶数据中学习系数，并集成到模型预测控制框架中以实现安全规划。在NGSIM数据集上的实验表明，MPCFormer在5秒预测范围内实现了最低的轨迹预测误差（ADE为0.86米）；在闭环测试中，其规划成功率高达94.67%，效率提升15.75%，碰撞率从21.25%降至0.5%，优于基于强化学习的规划器。
One Model for All: Multi-Objective Controllable Language Models
Authors: Qiang He, Yucheng Yang, Tianyi Zhou, Meng Fang, Mykola Pechenizkiy, Setareh Maghsudi
First: 2026-04-06T07:48:32+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-06T07:48:32+00:00
Comments: Published in Transactions on Machine Learning Research (03/2026): https://openreview.net/forum?id=qAM5PmvFYY
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Aligning large language models (LLMs) with human preferences is critical for enhancing LLMs' safety, helpfulness, humor, faithfulness, etc. Current reinforcement learning from human feedback (RLHF) mainly focuses on a fixed reward learned from average human ratings, which may weaken the adaptability and controllability of varying preferences. However, creating personalized LLMs requires aligning LLMs with individual human preferences, which is non-trivial due to the scarce data per user and the diversity of user preferences in multi-objective trade-offs, varying from emphasizing empathy in certain contexts to demanding efficiency and precision in others. Can we train one LLM to produce personalized outputs across different user preferences on the Pareto front? In this paper, we introduce Multi-Objective Control (MOC), which trains a single LLM to directly generate responses in the preference-defined regions of the Pareto front. Our approach introduces multi-objective optimization (MOO) principles into RLHF to train an LLM as a preference-conditioned policy network. We improve the computational efficiency of MOC by applying MOO at the policy level, enabling us to fine-tune a 7B-parameter model on a single A6000 GPU. Extensive experiments demonstrate the advantages of MOC over baselines in three aspects: (i) controllability of LLM outputs w.r.t. user preferences on the trade-off among multiple rewards; (ii) quality and diversity of LLM outputs, measured by the hyper-volume of multiple solutions achieved; and (iii) generalization to unseen preferences. These results highlight MOC's potential for real-world applications requiring scalable and customizable LLMs.
中文标题/摘要
标题：一模型适万物：多目标可控语言模型
将大语言模型（LLMs）与人类偏好对齐对于提升模型的安全性、助益性、幽默感、忠实度等至关重要。当前基于人类反馈的强化学习（RLHF）主要依赖从平均人类评分习得的固定奖励机制，这可能削弱模型应对不同偏好的适应性与可控性。然而，构建个性化LLMs需要将模型与个体人类偏好对齐，这面临双重挑战：单用户数据稀缺性，以及多目标权衡中用户偏好的多样性——某些场景需侧重共情能力，另一些场景则要求效率与精确性。我们能否训练单一LLM在帕累托前沿上针对不同用户偏好生成个性化输出？本文提出多目标控制（MOC）方法，通过训练单个LLM直接在偏好定义的帕累托前沿区域生成响应。我们将多目标优化（MOO）原理融入RLHF框架，将LLM训练为偏好条件策略网络。通过在策略层面实施MOO提升计算效率，仅需单张A6000 GPU即可微调70亿参数模型。大量实验证明MOC在三方面优于基线方法：（i）LLM输出在多重奖励权衡中对用户偏好的可控性；（ii）以达成方案超体积度量的输出质量与多样性；（iii）对未见偏好的泛化能力。这些成果彰显了MOC在需要可扩展、可定制LLMs的现实应用中的潜力。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the limitation of standard reinforcement learning from human feedback (RLHF), which typically optimizes for a fixed average human preference, thereby reducing model adaptability and controllability for diverse individual preferences. The authors propose Multi-Objective Control (MOC), a method that integrates multi-objective optimization principles into RLHF to train a single large language model as a preference-conditioned policy, capable of generating outputs across various user-defined trade-offs on the Pareto front. Experimental results on a 7B-parameter model fine-tuned efficiently on a single GPU demonstrate that MOC outperforms baselines in controllability over multiple reward trade-offs, output quality and diversity as measured by hyper-volume, and generalization to unseen preferences, highlighting its potential for scalable, customizable LLM applications.
本文针对标准的人类反馈强化学习（RLHF）通常优化固定的人类平均偏好、从而降低模型对不同个体偏好的适应性和可控性的局限，提出了一种多目标控制（MOC）方法。该方法将多目标优化原则融入RLHF，训练单个大语言模型作为偏好条件策略，使其能够在帕累托前沿上根据用户定义的不同权衡生成输出。在单个GPU上高效微调70亿参数模型的实验结果表明，MOC在多个奖励权衡的可控性、以超体积衡量的输出质量与多样性，以及对未见偏好的泛化能力上均优于基线方法，凸显了其在可扩展、可定制大语言模型应用中的潜力。
Depth-Breadth Synergy in RLVR: Unlocking LLM Reasoning Gains with Adaptive Exploration
Authors: Zhicheng Yang, Zhijiang Guo, Yinya Huang, Yongxin Wang, Dongchun Xie, Hanhui Li, Yiwei Wang, Xiaodan Liang, Jing Tang
First: 2025-08-19T11:51:40+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-06T05:58:02+00:00
Comments: 20 pages, 17 figures
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Reinforcement Learning with Verifiable Reward (RLVR) has emerged as a powerful paradigm for unlocking reasoning capabilities in large language models, yet its full potential is hindered by two under-explored dimensions: Depth-the hardest problem a model can sample; Breadth-the number of instances consumed in a single iteration. We dissect the popular GRPO algorithm and reveal a systematic bias: the cumulative-advantage disproportionately weights samples with medium accuracy, while down-weighting the low-accuracy instances that are crucial for pushing reasoning boundaries. To rectify the depth neglect, we introduce Difficulty Adaptive Rollout Sampling (DARS), which re-weights hard problems through targeted multi-stage rollouts, thereby increasing the number of positive rollouts for hard problems. Empirically, naively enlarging rollout size only accelerates convergence and even hurts Pass@K. Our DARS, in contrast, delivers consistent Pass@K gains without extra inference cost at convergence. Just as we adaptively expanded the depth of exploration, we now ask whether aggressively scaling the breadth of training data can further amplify reasoning gains. To this end, we intensely scale batch size and replace PPO's mini-batch iterations with full-batch updates over multiple epochs. Increasing breadth significantly enhances Pass@1 performance. Large-breadth training sustains high token-level entropy, indicating continued exploration and reduced gradient noise. We further present DARS-B, which augments DARS with large breadth, and demonstrate simultaneous gains in Pass@K and Pass@1. The results confirm that breadth and adaptive exploration across depth operate as orthogonal dimensions in RLVR, which are key to unleashing the reasoning power of RLVR.
中文标题/摘要
标题：RLVR中的深度-广度协同：通过自适应探索释放大语言模型推理能力
可验证奖励强化学习（RLVR）已成为释放大语言模型推理能力的强大范式，但其全部潜力受限于两个未充分探索的维度：深度（模型能采样的最难问题）与广度（单次迭代消耗的实例数量）。我们剖析了流行的GRPO算法，揭示其存在系统性偏差：累积优势函数对中等准确率样本赋予过高权重，同时低估对突破推理边界至关重要的低准确率样本。为纠正深度忽视问题，我们提出难度自适应轨迹采样（DARS），通过定向多阶段轨迹重加权难题，从而增加难题的正向轨迹数量。实证表明，简单扩大轨迹规模仅加速收敛甚至损害Pass@K指标。相比之下，我们的DARS方法在收敛时不增加推理成本即可持续提升Pass@K。在实现深度自适应探索后，我们进一步探究：激进扩展训练数据广度能否放大推理收益？为此，我们大幅扩展批次规模，将PPO的小批次迭代替换为多轮次的全批次更新。广度扩展显著提升了Pass@1性能。大广度训练维持了较高的词元级熵值，表明探索持续且梯度噪声降低。我们进一步提出DARS-B方法，将DARS与大广度训练结合，在Pass@K和Pass@1指标上实现同步提升。结果证实：广度与跨深度的自适应探索在RLVR中构成正交维度，是释放RLVR推理潜能的关键。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses limitations in Reinforcement Learning with Verifiable Reward (RLVR) for enhancing large language model reasoning, identifying a systematic bias in algorithms like GRPO that neglect difficult problems crucial for depth. To rectify this, the authors propose Difficulty Adaptive Rollout Sampling (DARS), which re-weights hard problems through targeted multi-stage rollouts, and they also explore scaling training data breadth via large batch sizes and full-batch updates. Experimental results show that DARS improves Pass@K without extra inference cost, while breadth scaling boosts Pass@1 performance and maintains exploration; combining both in DARS-B yields simultaneous gains, confirming depth and breadth as orthogonal dimensions for unlocking RLVR's reasoning potential.
本文针对强化学习与可验证奖励在提升大语言模型推理能力中的局限性，指出如GRPO等算法存在系统性偏差，忽视了推动推理深度所需的高难度问题。为此，作者提出了难度自适应采样方法，通过定向多阶段采样重新加权难题，并探索了通过大批量和全批量更新来扩展训练数据广度。实验结果表明，该方法在不增加推理成本的情况下提升了Pass@K性能，而广度扩展则提高了Pass@1表现并保持了探索性；两者结合的DARS-B方法实现了同步增益，证实了深度与广度作为正交维度对于释放RLVR推理潜力的关键作用。
Explainable Autonomous Cyber Defense using Adversarial Multi-Agent Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Yiyao Zhang, Diksha Goel, Hussain Ahmad
First: 2026-04-06T05:40:43+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-06T05:40:43+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Autonomous agents are increasingly deployed in both offensive and defensive cyber operations, creating high-speed, closed-loop interactions in critical infrastructure environments. Advanced Persistent Threat (APT) actors exploit "Living off the Land" techniques and targeted telemetry perturbations to induce ambiguity in monitoring systems, causing automated defenses to overreact or misclassify benign behavior as malicious activity. Existing monolithic and multi-agent defense pipelines largely operate on correlation-based signals, lack structural constraints on response actions, and are vulnerable to reasoning drift under ambiguous or adversarial inputs. We present the Causal Multi-Agent Decision Framework (C-MADF), a structurally constrained architecture for autonomous cyber defense that integrates causal modeling with adversarial dual-policy control. C-MADF first learns a Structural Causal Model (SCM) from historical telemetry and compiles it into an investigation-level Directed Acyclic Graph (DAG) that defines admissible response transitions. This roadmap is formalized as a Markov Decision Process (MDP) whose action space is explicitly restricted to causally consistent transitions. Decision-making within this constrained space is performed by a dual-agent reinforcement learning system in which a threat-optimizing Blue-Team policy is counterbalanced by a conservatively shaped Red-Team policy. Inter-policy disagreement is quantified through a Policy Divergence Score and exposed via a human-in-the-loop interface equipped with an Explainability-Transparency Score that serves as an escalation signal under uncertainty. On the real-world CICIoT2023 dataset, C-MADF reduces the false-positive rate from 11.2%, 9.7%, and 8.4% in three cutting-edge literature baselines to 1.8%, while achieving 0.997 precision, 0.961 recall, and 0.979 F1-score.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于对抗性多智能体强化学习的可解释自主网络防御
自主智能体在攻防网络操作中的部署日益增多，在关键基础设施环境中形成高速闭环交互。高级持续性威胁（APT）行为者利用‘就地取材’技术和定向遥测扰动，在监控系统中制造模糊性，导致自动化防御系统过度反应或将良性行为误判为恶意活动。现有单体式和多智能体防御流程主要基于关联信号运行，缺乏对响应行动的结构性约束，在模糊或对抗性输入下易出现推理漂移。本文提出因果多智能体决策框架（C-MADF），这是一种融合因果建模与对抗性双策略控制的结构约束式自主网络防御架构。C-MADF首先从历史遥测数据学习结构因果模型（SCM），并将其编译为调查级有向无环图（DAG），以定义可允许的响应转移路径。该路线图被形式化为马尔可夫决策过程（MDP），其动作空间被显式限制于因果一致的转移路径。在此约束空间内的决策由双智能体强化学习系统执行，其中威胁优化的蓝队策略与保守塑造的红队策略相互制衡。策略间分歧通过策略分歧评分进行量化，并借助配备可解释性-透明度评分的人机交互界面进行可视化，该评分在不确定性条件下可作为升级信号。在真实世界CICIoT2023数据集上，C-MADF将三种前沿文献基线的误报率从11.2%、9.7%和8.4%降至1.8%，同时达到0.997精确率、0.961召回率和0.979 F1分数。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the need for robust autonomous cyber defense against Advanced Persistent Threats that exploit ambiguity to trigger false positives, this paper introduces the Causal Multi-Agent Decision Framework (C-MADF), which integrates causal modeling with adversarial multi-agent reinforcement learning. The method first learns a Structural Causal Model from historical data to create a causally constrained action space, then employs dual-agent reinforcement learning where a Blue-Team policy is adversarially shaped by a Red-Team policy, with policy divergence and explainability scores enabling human oversight. Experimental results on the CICIoT2023 dataset show C-MADF significantly reduces the false-positive rate to 1.8% from baseline rates of 11.2%, 9.7%, and 8.4%, while achieving high precision (0.997), recall (0.961), and F1-score (0.979).
针对高级持续性威胁利用模糊性引发误报的问题，本文提出了因果多智能体决策框架（C-MADF），以增强自主网络防御的鲁棒性。该方法首先从历史数据中学习结构因果模型，构建因果约束的动作空间，然后采用对抗性多智能体强化学习，其中蓝队策略由红队策略进行对抗性塑造，并通过策略分歧和可解释性评分实现人工监督。在CICIoT2023数据集上的实验结果表明，C-MADF将误报率从基线方法的11.2%、9.7%和8.4%显著降低至1.8%，同时实现了0.997的精确率、0.961的召回率和0.979的F1分数。
ReinVBC: A Model-based Reinforcement Learning Approach to Vehicle Braking Controller
Authors: Haoxin Lin, Junjie Zhou, Daheng Xu, Yang Yu
First: 2026-04-06T04:00:40+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-06T04:00:40+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Braking system, the key module to ensure the safety and steer-ability of current vehicles, relies on extensive manual calibration during production. Reducing labor and time consumption while maintaining the Vehicle Braking Controller (VBC) performance greatly benefits the vehicle industry. Model-based methods in offline reinforcement learning, which facilitate policy exploration within a data-driven dynamics model, offer a promising solution for addressing real-world control tasks. This work proposes ReinVBC, which applies an offline model-based reinforcement learning approach to deal with the vehicle braking control problem. We introduce useful engineering designs into the paradigm of model learning and utilization to obtain a reliable vehicle dynamics model and a capable braking policy. Several results demonstrate the capability of our method in real-world vehicle braking and its potential to replace the production-grade anti-lock braking system.
中文标题/摘要
标题：ReinVBC：一种基于模型的强化学习车辆制动控制器方法
制动系统作为保障现代车辆安全性与可操控性的关键模块，在生产过程中依赖大量人工标定。在维持车辆制动控制器性能的同时降低人力与时间成本，对汽车产业具有重要意义。基于模型的离线强化学习方法通过数据驱动的动力学模型促进策略探索，为应对现实控制任务提供了可行方案。本研究提出ReinVBC，采用离线基于模型的强化学习方法处理车辆制动控制问题。我们在模型学习与应用范式中引入实用工程设计，以获得可靠的车辆动力学模型与高效的制动策略。多项实验结果表明，该方法在实际车辆制动中具备优异性能，并具有替代生产级防抱死制动系统的潜力。

The motivation is to reduce the extensive manual calibration required for vehicle braking controllers by developing an automated, data-efficient solution that maintains safety and performance. 该研究的动机是通过开发自动化、数据高效的解决方案来减少车辆制动控制器所需的大量人工校准，同时保持安全性和性能。方法上，提出了一种名为ReinVBC的基于模型的离线强化学习方法，通过引入工程化设计来学习可靠的车辆动力学模型并从数据中推导出有效的制动策略。实验结果表明，该方法在真实车辆制动中表现出色，并具备替代生产级防抱死制动系统的潜力。
Finite-Time Analysis of Q-Value Iteration for General-Sum Stackelberg Games
Authors: Narim Jeong, Donghwan Lee
First: 2026-04-06T03:48:42+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-06T03:48:42+00:00
Comments: 8 pages
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Reinforcement learning has been successful both empirically and theoretically in single-agent settings, but extending these results to multi-agent reinforcement learning in general-sum Markov games remains challenging. This paper studies the convergence of Stackelberg Q-value iteration in two-player general-sum Markov games from a control-theoretic perspective. We introduce a relaxed policy condition tailored to the Stackelberg setting and model the learning dynamics as a switching system. By constructing upper and lower comparison systems, we establish finite-time error bounds for the Q-functions and characterize their convergence properties. Our results provide a novel control-theoretic perspective on Stackelberg learning. Moreover, to the best of the authors' knowledge, this paper offers the first finite-time convergence guarantees for Q-value iteration in general-sum Markov games under Stackelberg interactions.
中文标题/摘要
标题：一般和斯塔克尔伯格博弈中Q值迭代的有限时间分析
强化学习在单智能体场景中已取得实证与理论上的成功，但将相关成果拓展至一般和马尔可夫博弈中的多智能体强化学习仍具挑战。本文从控制理论视角研究双人一般和马尔可夫博弈中斯塔克尔伯格Q值迭代的收敛性。我们提出一种适配斯塔克尔伯格框架的松弛策略条件，并将学习动态建模为切换系统。通过构建上下界比较系统，确立了Q函数的有限时间误差界并刻画其收敛特性。研究结果为斯塔克尔伯格学习提供了新颖的控制理论视角。此外，据作者所知，本文首次为斯塔克尔伯格交互下一般和马尔可夫博弈中的Q值迭代提供了有限时间收敛性保证。
