The method introduces a relaxed policy condition specific to Stackelberg interactions and models the learning dynamics of Q-value iteration as a switching system, using upper and lower comparison systems to analyze convergence. The main experimental results establish finite-time error bounds for the Q-functions, providing the first such convergence guarantees for Q-value iteration in general-sum Markov games under Stackelberg settings, offering a novel control-theoretic perspective on this learning problem.
本文的动机在于将强化学习从单智能体环境扩展到多智能体一般和马尔可夫博弈的挑战，重点关注Stackelberg博弈框架。方法上，针对Stackelberg交互引入了一种宽松的策略条件，并将Q值迭代的学习动态建模为切换系统，通过构建上下比较系统来分析收敛性。主要实验结果确立了Q函数的有限时间误差界，首次为Stackelberg交互下一般和马尔可夫博弈中的Q值迭代提供了收敛性保证，为该学习问题提供了新颖的控制理论视角。
PlayWorld: Learning Robot World Models from Autonomous Play
Authors: Tenny Yin, Zhiting Mei, Zhonghe Zheng, Miyu Yamane, David Wang, Jade Sceats, Samuel M. Bateman, Lihan Zha, Apurva Badithela, Ola Shorinwa, Anirudha Majumdar
First: 2026-03-09T23:58:07+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-06T01:32:12+00:00
Comments: Website: https://robot-playworld.github.io/
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Project1
Abstract
Action-conditioned video models offer a promising path to building general-purpose robot simulators that can improve directly from data. Yet, despite training on large-scale robot datasets, current state-of-the-art video models still struggle to predict physically consistent robot-object interactions that are crucial in robotic manipulation. To close this gap, we present PlayWorld, a simple, scalable, and fully autonomous pipeline for training high-fidelity video world simulators from interaction experience. In contrast to prior approaches that rely on success-biased human demonstrations, PlayWorld is the first system capable of learning entirely from unsupervised robot self-play, enabling naturally scalable data collection while capturing complex, long-tailed physical interactions essential for modeling realistic object dynamics. Experiments across diverse manipulation tasks show that PlayWorld generates high-quality, physically consistent predictions for contact-rich interactions that are not captured by world models trained on human-collected data. We further demonstrate the versatility of PlayWorld in enabling fine-grained failure prediction and policy evaluation, with up to 40% improvements over human-collected data. Finally, we demonstrate how PlayWorld enables reinforcement learning in the world model, improving policy performance by 65% in success rates when deployed in the real world.
中文标题/摘要
标题：PlayWorld：通过自主游戏学习机器人世界模型
动作条件视频模型为构建通用机器人模拟器提供了可行路径，使其能直接从数据中优化。然而，尽管基于大规模机器人数据集进行训练，当前最先进的视频模型仍难以预测对机器人操作至关重要的物理一致性人机交互。为弥补这一差距，我们提出PlayWorld——一个简单、可扩展且完全自主的流程，用于从交互经验中训练高保真视频世界模拟器。与依赖成功偏向性人类示范的先前方法不同，PlayWorld是首个完全通过无监督机器人自主游戏进行学习的系统，既能实现自然可扩展的数据收集，又能捕捉对真实物体动力学建模至关重要的复杂长尾物理交互。跨多种操作任务的实验表明，PlayWorld能对密集接触交互生成高质量、物理一致的预测，这是基于人类收集数据训练的世界模型所无法实现的。我们进一步展示了PlayWorld在细粒度故障预测与策略评估方面的通用性，相比人类收集数据最高可提升40%的性能。最后，我们验证了PlayWorld在世界模型中实现强化学习的能力，在真实世界部署时将策略成功率提升了65%。
Summary / 总结
The motivation behind PlayWorld is to address the limitations of current action-conditioned video models in predicting physically consistent robot-object interactions, which are crucial for robotic manipulation, despite training on large-scale datasets. The method introduces a simple, scalable, and fully autonomous pipeline that learns world models from unsupervised robot self-play, enabling data collection without reliance on success-biased human demonstrations and capturing complex, long-tailed physical interactions. Experimental results show that PlayWorld generates high-quality, physically consistent predictions for contact-rich interactions, outperforms models trained on human-collected data by up to 40% in failure prediction and policy evaluation, and improves real-world policy performance by 65% in success rates through reinforcement learning in the world model.
PlayWorld的动机是解决当前基于动作的视频模型在预测物理一致的机器人-物体交互方面的局限性，尽管这些模型在大规模数据集上训练，但对机器人操作至关重要的交互预测仍不足。该方法提出了一种简单、可扩展且完全自主的流程，通过无监督的机器人自我游戏学习世界模型，避免了依赖人类演示的偏差，并能捕捉复杂的长尾物理交互。实验结果表明，PlayWorld能生成高质量、物理一致的接触丰富交互预测，在细粒度失败预测和策略评估上比基于人类收集数据的模型提升高达40%，并通过在世界模型中进行强化学习，将真实世界中的策略成功率提高了65%。
ALMAB-DC: Active Learning, Multi-Armed Bandits, and Distributed Computing for Sequential Experimental Design and Black-Box Optimization
Authors: Foo Hui-Mean, Yuan-chin I Chang
First: 2026-03-22T11:47:20+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-06T01:12:42+00:00
Comments: 33 pages, and 13 figures
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Sequential experimental design under expensive, gradient-free objectives is a central challenge in computational statistics: evaluation budgets are tightly constrained and information must be extracted efficiently from each observation. We propose \textbf{ALMAB-DC}, a GP-based sequential design framework combining active learning, multi-armed bandits (MAB), and distributed asynchronous computing for expensive black-box experimentation. A Gaussian process surrogate with uncertainty-aware acquisition identifies informative query points; a UCB or Thompson-sampling bandit controller allocates evaluations across parallel workers; and an asynchronous scheduler handles heterogeneous runtimes. We present cumulative regret bounds for the bandit components and characterize parallel scalability via Amdahl's Law. We validate ALMAB-DC on five benchmarks. On the two statistical experimental-design tasks, ALMAB-DC achieves lower simple regret than Equal Spacing, Random, and D-optimal designs in dose--response optimization, and in adaptive spatial field estimation matches the Greedy Max-Variance benchmark while outperforming Latin Hypercube Sampling; at $K=4$ the distributed setting reaches target performance in one-quarter of sequential wall-clock rounds. On three ML/engineering tasks (CIFAR-10 HPO, CFD drag minimization, MuJoCo RL), ALMAB-DC achieves 93.4\% CIFAR-10 accuracy (outperforming BOHB by 1.7\,pp and Optuna by 1.1\,pp), reduces airfoil drag to $C_D = 0.059$ (36.9\% below Grid Search), and improves RL return by 50\% over Grid Search. All advantages over non-ALMAB baselines are statistically significant under Bonferroni-corrected Mann--Whitney $U$ tests. Distributed execution achieves $7.5\times$ speedup at $K = 16$ agents, consistent with Amdahl's Law.
中文标题/摘要
标题：ALMAB-DC：面向序列实验设计与黑盒优化的主动学习、多臂老虎机与分布式计算框架
在昂贵且无梯度目标下的序列实验设计是计算统计学的核心挑战：评估预算严格受限，必须从每次观测中高效提取信息。我们提出基于高斯过程的序列设计框架ALMAB-DC，融合主动学习、多臂老虎机与分布式异步计算技术。该框架通过具备不确定性感知的高斯过程代理模型识别信息性查询点，采用UCB或汤普森采样的老虎机控制器分配并行计算资源，并通过异步调度器处理异构运行时间。我们给出了老虎机组件的累积遗憾界，并基于阿姆达尔定律刻画了并行可扩展性。在五个基准测试中验证表明：在两项统计实验设计任务中，ALMAB-DC在剂量响应优化中的简单遗憾低于等间距、随机和D最优设计；在自适应空间场估计中匹配贪婪最大方差基准，且优于拉丁超立方采样——分布式设置（K=4）仅需串行执行1/4的挂钟轮次即可达到目标性能。在三个ML/工程任务中（CIFAR-10超参优化、CFD阻力最小化、MuJoCo强化学习），ALMAB-DC分别实现93.4%的CIFAR-10准确率（优于BOHB 1.7个百分点、Optuna 1.1个百分点）、将翼型阻力系数降至0.059（较网格搜索降低36.9%）、强化学习回报较网格搜索提升50%。所有优势均通过邦费罗尼校正的曼-惠特尼U检验达到统计显著性。分布式执行在16个计算节点上实现7.5倍加速，符合阿姆达尔定律预测。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the challenge of sequential experimental design for expensive black-box optimization, where evaluations are costly and must be used efficiently. It introduces ALMAB-DC, a framework combining Gaussian process surrogates for active learning with multi-armed bandit controllers (UCB or Thompson sampling) to allocate evaluations across parallel workers, and an asynchronous scheduler to handle heterogeneous runtimes, supported by theoretical regret bounds and scalability analysis. Experimental results on five benchmarks show that ALMAB-DC outperforms baselines in statistical tasks like dose-response optimization and spatial field estimation, achieving lower regret and matching greedy benchmarks with distributed speedups, and in ML/engineering tasks it improves CIFAR-10 accuracy by 1.7 percentage points over BOHB, reduces airfoil drag by 36.9% compared to Grid Search, and enhances RL returns by 50%, with all gains being statistically significant and distributed execution yielding up to 7.5x speedup.
本文针对昂贵黑盒优化中的顺序实验设计挑战，其中评估成本高且必须高效利用信息。提出了ALMAB-DC框架，结合高斯过程代理进行主动学习，使用多臂老虎机控制器（UCB或Thompson采样）在并行工作节点间分配评估，并采用异步调度器处理异构运行时，辅以理论遗憾界和可扩展性分析。在五个基准测试上的实验结果表明，ALMAB-DC在统计任务（如剂量响应优化和空间场估计）中优于基线方法，实现了更低的遗憾并匹配贪婪基准，分布式设置下达到目标性能的时间缩短为四分之一；在ML/工程任务中，CIFAR-10准确率比BOHB提高1.7个百分点，翼型阻力比网格搜索降低36.9%，强化学习回报提升50%，所有优势均具有统计显著性，分布式执行实现了最高7.5倍的加速。
Boosted Distributional Reinforcement Learning: Analysis and Healthcare Applications
Authors: Zequn Chen, Wesley J. Marrero
First: 2026-04-06T01:00:08+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-06T01:00:08+00:00
Comments: Preprint. 40 pages,11 figures. Supplementary appendix included
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Researchers and practitioners are increasingly considering reinforcement learning to optimize decisions in complex domains like robotics and healthcare. To date, these efforts have largely utilized expectation-based learning. However, relying on expectation-focused objectives may be insufficient for making consistent decisions in highly uncertain situations involving multiple heterogeneous groups. While distributional reinforcement learning algorithms have been introduced to model the full distributions of outcomes, they can yield large discrepancies in realized benefits among comparable agents. This challenge is particularly acute in healthcare settings, where physicians (controllers) must manage multiple patients (subordinate agents) with uncertain disease progression and heterogeneous treatment responses. We propose a Boosted Distributional Reinforcement Learning (BDRL) algorithm that optimizes agent-specific outcome distributions while enforcing comparability among similar agents and analyze its convergence. To further stabilize learning, we incorporate a post-update projection step formulated as a constrained convex optimization problem, which efficiently aligns individual outcomes with a high-performing reference within a specified tolerance. We apply our algorithm to manage hypertension in a large subset of the US adult population by categorizing individuals into cardiovascular disease risk groups. Our approach modifies treatment plans for median and vulnerable patients by mimicking the behavior of high-performing references in each risk group. Furthermore, we find that BDRL improves the number and consistency of quality-adjusted life years compared with reinforcement learning baselines.
中文标题/摘要
标题：增强型分布强化学习：分析与医疗健康应用
研究者和实践者日益关注利用强化学习优化机器人、医疗健康等复杂领域的决策。目前这些工作主要采用基于期望值的学习方法，但在涉及多异质群体的高度不确定情境中，依赖期望目标可能不足以保证决策一致性。虽然分布强化学习算法已被引入以建模完整结果分布，但其在可比智能体间可能产生显著的收益差异。这一挑战在医疗场景尤为突出：医生（控制者）需管理具有不确定疾病进展和异质治疗反应的多名患者（从属智能体）。本文提出一种增强型分布强化学习算法，在优化个体结果分布的同时强制相似智能体间的可比性，并分析其收敛性。为提升学习稳定性，我们引入一个表述为约束凸优化问题的更新后投影步骤，可在指定容差内高效地将个体结果与高性能参照对齐。我们将该算法应用于美国成年人群高血压管理，通过心血管疾病风险分组对个体进行分类。该方法通过模仿各风险组内高性能参照的行为，调整中位患者与脆弱患者的治疗方案。实验表明，相较于强化学习基线方法，增强型分布强化学习显著提升了质量调整生命年的数量与一致性。
Summary / 总结
The paper is motivated by the need to move beyond expectation-based reinforcement learning in complex, uncertain domains like healthcare, where standard methods may fail to ensure equitable outcomes across heterogeneous agents. The authors propose a Boosted Distributional Reinforcement Learning (BDRL) algorithm that optimizes agent-specific outcome distributions while enforcing comparability among similar agents, incorporating a post-update projection step to stabilize learning by aligning outcomes with high-performing references. In experiments on hypertension management across cardiovascular risk groups, BDRL modifies treatment plans for median and vulnerable patients by mimicking high-performing references, improving both the number and consistency of quality-adjusted life years compared to baseline reinforcement learning methods.
本文的动机在于，在医疗等复杂不确定领域中，需要超越基于期望的强化学习方法，因为标准方法可能无法确保异质智能体之间的公平结果。作者提出了一种增强分布强化学习算法，该算法在优化智能体特定结果分布的同时，强制相似智能体之间的可比性，并通过后更新投影步骤来稳定学习，使个体结果与高性能参考在指定容差内对齐。在针对心血管风险人群的高血压管理实验中，该算法通过模仿各风险组中的高性能参考，调整了中位和脆弱患者的治疗计划，与基线强化学习方法相比，提高了质量调整生命年的数量和一致性。
SPHINX: A Synthetic Environment for Visual Perception and Reasoning
Authors: Md Tanvirul Alam, Saksham Aggarwal, Justin Yang Chae, Nidhi Rastogi
First: 2025-11-25T20:00:47+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-05T23:59:08+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
We present Sphinx, a synthetic environment for visual perception and reasoning that targets core cognitive primitives. Sphinx procedurally generates puzzles using motifs, tiles, charts, icons, and geometric primitives, each paired with verifiable ground-truth solutions, enabling both precise evaluation and large-scale dataset construction. The benchmark covers 25 task types spanning symmetry detection, geometric transformations, spatial reasoning, chart interpretation, and sequence prediction. Evaluating recent large vision-language models (LVLMs) shows that even state-of-the-art GPT-5 attains only 51.1% accuracy, well below human performance. Finally, we demonstrate that reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards (RLVR) substantially improves model accuracy on these tasks and yields gains on external visual reasoning benchmarks, highlighting its promise for advancing multimodal reasoning.
中文标题/摘要
标题：SPHINX：面向视觉感知与推理的合成环境
本文提出Sphinx——一个针对核心认知基元的视觉感知与推理合成环境。该系统通过程序化生成包含图案、图块、图表、图标及几何基元的谜题，每个谜题均配有可验证的真实解，支持精确评估与大规模数据集构建。基准测试涵盖对称检测、几何变换、空间推理、图表解读和序列预测等25类任务。对近期大型视觉语言模型（LVLM）的评估表明，即使最先进的GPT-5模型准确率也仅为51.1%，远低于人类水平。最后，我们验证了基于可验证奖励的强化学习（RLVR）能显著提升模型在这些任务上的准确率，并在外部视觉推理基准测试中取得进步，凸显了该方法对推进多模态推理研究的潜力。

Combining Tree-Search, Generative Models, and Nash Bargaining Concepts in Game-Theoretic Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Zun Li, Marc Lanctot, Kevin R. McKee, Luke Marris, Ian Gemp, Daniel Hennes, Paul Muller, Kate Larson, Yoram Bachrach, Michael P. Wellman
Venue: IJCAI
First: 2023-02-01T23:06:23+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-05T21:15:12+00:00
Comments: Accepted by IJCAI'25 main track
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Opponent modeling methods typically involve two crucial steps: building a belief distribution over opponents' strategies, and exploiting this opponent model by playing a best response. However, existing approaches typically require domain-specific heurstics to come up with such a model, and algorithms for approximating best responses are hard to scale in large, imperfect information domains. In this work, we introduce a scalable and generic multiagent training regime for opponent modeling using deep game-theoretic reinforcement learning. We first propose Generative Best Respoonse (GenBR), a best response algorithm based on Monte-Carlo Tree Search (MCTS) with a learned deep generative model that samples world states during planning. This new method scales to large imperfect information domains and can be plug and play in a variety of multiagent algorithms. We use this new method under the framework of Policy Space Response Oracles (PSRO), to automate the generation of an \emph{offline opponent model} via iterative game-theoretic reasoning and population-based training. We propose using solution concepts based on bargaining theory to build up an opponent mixture, which we find identifying profiles that are near the Pareto frontier. Then GenBR keeps updating an \emph{online opponent model} and reacts against it during gameplay. We conduct behavioral studies where human participants negotiate with our agents in Deal-or-No-Deal, a class of bilateral bargaining games. Search with generative modeling finds stronger policies during both training time and test time, enables online Bayesian co-player prediction, and can produce agents that achieve comparable social welfare and Nash bargaining score negotiating with humans as humans trading among themselves.
中文标题/摘要
标题：博弈论强化学习中结合树搜索、生成模型与纳什议价概念的研究
对手建模方法通常包含两个关键步骤：构建对手策略的信念分布，以及通过最佳响应策略利用该对手模型。然而，现有方法通常需要领域特定的启发式规则来构建此类模型，且近似最佳响应的算法在大型非完美信息领域中难以扩展。本研究提出一种基于深度博弈论强化学习的可扩展通用多智能体对手建模训练框架。我们首先提出生成式最佳响应算法，这是一种基于蒙特卡洛树搜索的最佳响应算法，通过学习的深度生成模型在规划过程中采样世界状态。这种新方法可扩展至大型非完美信息领域，并能即插即用于多种多智能体算法。我们将该方法应用于策略空间响应预言框架，通过迭代博弈论推理与基于种群的训练，实现离线对手模型的自动生成。我们提出基于议价理论的解概念来构建对手混合策略，该方法能识别接近帕累托边界的策略剖面。生成式最佳响应算法持续更新在线对手模型并在博弈过程中实时应对。我们在双边议价游戏类别的交易博弈中开展人类与智能体谈判的行为研究。实验表明：结合生成模型的搜索方法在训练与测试阶段均能发现更强策略，实现在线贝叶斯协同玩家预测，所构建的智能体与人类谈判时获得的社会福利与纳什议价分数，可达到人类间交易相当的水平。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses scalability and generalization issues in opponent modeling for multiagent systems, where existing methods rely on domain-specific heuristics and struggle in large imperfect-information games. The authors propose a novel approach combining Generative Best Response (GenBR), which integrates Monte-Carlo Tree Search with a deep generative model to sample world states during planning, and Policy Space Response Oracles (PSRO) framework enhanced with Nash bargaining concepts to build offline and online opponent models. Experimental results in bilateral bargaining games, such as Deal-or-No-Deal with human participants, show that GenBR yields stronger policies during training and testing, enables effective online co-player prediction, and achieves social welfare and Nash bargaining scores comparable to human-human negotiations.
本文针对多智能体系统中对手建模的可扩展性和泛化性问题，现有方法通常依赖领域特定启发式规则，且在大型不完全信息游戏中难以扩展。作者提出了一种新方法，结合了生成式最佳响应（GenBR）——通过蒙特卡洛树搜索与深度生成模型在规划中采样世界状态，以及策略空间响应预言（PSRO）框架，并引入纳什讨价还价概念来构建离线和在线对手模型。在双边讨价还价游戏（如与人类参与者进行的“成交与否”游戏）中的实验结果表明，GenBR在训练和测试期间能产生更强策略，实现有效的在线协同玩家预测，并且其智能体与人类谈判时获得的社会福利和纳什讨价还价分数与人类间谈判相当。
APPA: Adaptive Preference Pluralistic Alignment for Fair Federated RLHF of LLMs
Authors: Mahmoud Srewa, Tianyu Zhao, Salma Elmalaki
First: 2026-04-05T20:48:36+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-05T20:48:36+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Aligning large language models (LLMs) with diverse human preferences requires pluralistic alignment, where a single model must respect the values of multiple distinct groups simultaneously. In federated reinforcement learning from human feedback (FedRLHF), these groups align a shared policy without centralizing preference data, which makes fair reward aggregation essential. Existing aggregation methods exhibit clear trade offs: average based aggregation systematically under aligns worst performing groups, while min aggregation prioritizes worst group performance at the cost of overall alignment. We propose APPA, an Adaptive Preference Pluralistic Alignment framework that dynamically reweights group level rewards based on historical alignment rewards. Our approach prioritizes under aligned groups without degrading well aligned ones, while requiring no access to raw preference data. Integrated into a proximal policy optimization (PPO) based FedRLHF pipeline and evaluated on GLOBALQA and OQA across three model families (Gemma 2 2B, Llama 3.2 3B, Qwen3 0.6B), APPA achieves strong fairness alignment trade offs, improving worst group alignment by up to 28% over average aggregation while maintaining higher overall alignment than min aggregation across most configurations.
中文标题/摘要
标题：APPA：面向大语言模型公平联邦RLHF的自适应偏好多元对齐框架
使大语言模型（LLMs）与多样化人类偏好对齐需要多元对齐，即单一模型必须同时尊重多个不同群体的价值观。在基于人类反馈的联邦强化学习（FedRLHF）中，这些群体在无需集中偏好数据的情况下对齐共享策略，这使得公平的奖励聚合至关重要。现有聚合方法存在明显权衡：基于平均的聚合会系统性弱化表现最差群体的对齐效果，而最小化聚合则以牺牲整体对齐为代价优先保障最差群体表现。我们提出APPA（自适应偏好多元对齐框架），该框架基于历史对齐奖励动态调整群体级奖励权重。我们的方法优先提升未充分对齐群体的表现，同时不影响已良好对齐的群体，且无需访问原始偏好数据。将APPA集成至基于近端策略优化（PPO）的FedRLHF流程中，并在GLOBALQA和OQA数据集上对三种模型系列（Gemma 2 2B、Llama 3.2 3B、Qwen3 0.6B）进行评估，结果表明APPA实现了优异的公平性与对齐性权衡：相比平均聚合方法，最差群体对齐性提升最高达28%，同时在多数配置下保持比最小化聚合更高的整体对齐性。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the challenge of aligning large language models with diverse human preferences in federated settings, where centralized data collection is avoided, by proposing APPA, an Adaptive Preference Pluralistic Alignment framework. The method dynamically reweights group-level rewards based on historical alignment performance to prioritize under-aligned groups without degrading well-aligned ones, integrated into a proximal policy optimization-based federated RLHF pipeline. Experimental results on datasets like GLOBALQA and OQA across multiple model families show that APPA improves worst-group alignment by up to 28% over average aggregation while maintaining higher overall alignment than min aggregation, achieving a strong fairness-alignment trade-off.
本文针对联邦环境下大型语言模型与多样化人类偏好对齐的挑战，提出了自适应偏好多元对齐框架APPA，以避免集中式数据收集。该方法基于历史对齐奖励动态调整组级奖励权重，优先考虑未充分对齐的群体而不损害已对齐群体，并集成于基于近端策略优化的联邦RLHF流程中。在GLOBALQA和OQA等数据集及多个模型系列上的实验结果表明，APPA将最差群体对齐性能较平均聚合提升高达28%，同时在多数配置下保持比最小聚合更高的整体对齐度，实现了公平性与对齐性的良好平衡。
MC-CPO: Mastery-Conditioned Constrained Policy Optimization
Authors: Oluseyi Olukola, Nick Rahimi
First: 2026-04-05T20:13:34+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-05T20:13:34+00:00
Comments: 15 pages, 8 figures. Submitted to IEEE Transactions on Learning Technologies (TLT)
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Engagement-optimized adaptive tutoring systems may prioritize short-term behavioral signals over sustained learning outcomes, creating structural incentives for reward hacking in reinforcement learning policies. We formalize this challenge as a constrained Markov decision process (CMDP) with mastery-conditioned feasibility, in which pedagogical safety constraints dynamically restrict admissible actions according to learner mastery and prerequisite structure. We introduce Mastery-Conditioned Constrained Policy Optimization (MC-CPO), a two-timescale primal-dual algorithm that integrates structural action masking with constrained policy optimization. In the tabular regime, we establish feasibility preservation and convergence to stationary feasible points under standard stochastic approximation conditions and derive a safety gap result showing that optimization within the mastery-conditioned feasible set can strictly dominate post-hoc filtering under identical safety budgets. Empirical validation is conducted in minimal and extended tabular environments and in a neural tutoring setting. Across 10 random seeds and one million training steps in the neural regime, MC-CPO satisfies constraint budgets within tolerance, reduces discounted safety costs relative to unconstrained and reward-shaped baselines, and substantially lowers the Reward Hacking Severity Index (RHSI). These results indicate that embedding pedagogical structure directly into the feasible action space provides a principled foundation for mitigating reward hacking in instructional reinforcement learning systems.
中文标题/摘要
标题：MC-CPO：基于掌握程度的约束策略优化
以参与度优化的自适应教学系统可能优先考虑短期行为信号而非持续学习成果，这为强化学习策略中的奖励操纵创造了结构性激励。我们将此挑战形式化为一个具有掌握程度条件可行性的约束马尔可夫决策过程（CMDP），其中教学安全约束会根据学习者掌握程度和先决知识结构动态限制可采纳动作。 我们提出基于掌握程度的约束策略优化（MC-CPO），这是一种双时间尺度的原始对偶算法，将结构化动作屏蔽与约束策略优化相结合。在表格化场景中，我们在标准随机逼近条件下建立了可行性保持和向平稳可行点的收敛性，并推导出安全间隙结果，表明在相同安全预算下，在掌握程度条件可行集内的优化严格优于事后过滤方法。 我们在最小化及扩展的表格化环境以及神经教学场景中进行了实证验证。在神经场景的10个随机种子和一百万训练步数中，MC-CPO在容差范围内满足约束预算，相较于无约束和奖励塑形基线降低了折现安全成本，并显著降低了奖励操纵严重指数（RHSI）。 这些结果表明，将教学结构直接嵌入可行动作空间为缓解教学强化学习系统中的奖励操纵提供了原则性基础。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the issue in adaptive tutoring systems where reinforcement learning policies might prioritize short-term engagement over long-term learning, a form of reward hacking. To mitigate this, the authors formalize the problem as a constrained Markov decision process with mastery-conditioned feasibility, where pedagogical safety constraints dynamically limit actions based on learner mastery. They propose Mastery-Conditioned Constrained Policy Optimization (MC-CPO), a two-timescale primal-dual algorithm that combines structural action masking with constrained policy optimization. Experimental results in tabular and neural tutoring environments show that MC-CPO successfully adheres to constraint budgets, reduces safety costs compared to baselines, and significantly lowers the Reward Hacking Severity Index, demonstrating its effectiveness in embedding pedagogical structure to prevent reward hacking.
本文针对自适应教学系统中强化学习策略可能优先考虑短期参与而非长期学习（即奖励黑客）的问题。为解决此问题，作者将问题形式化为具有掌握条件可行性的约束马尔可夫决策过程，其中教学安全约束根据学习者掌握程度动态限制可采取的行动。他们提出了掌握条件约束策略优化（MC-CPO），这是一种结合了结构化行动掩码与约束策略优化的双时间尺度原始对偶算法。在表格和神经教学环境中的实验结果表明，MC-CPO成功遵守了约束预算，与基线方法相比降低了安全成本，并显著减少了奖励黑客严重性指数，证明了其通过嵌入教学结构来防止奖励黑客的有效性。
